Yellow origin’s twelve,
Governing qi of the Four Numinous.
Above heaven, below earth,
Courtyard penetrating the primordial root.

If no gate is inscribed, place the talismans at the four directions,
The center at the fasting hall.
At the door, lodge the initiation,
Burn incense and invoke:

Two *zhi* officials of the Emperor’s Direct Talisman emerge this day,
*This* matter is overseen by so-and-so,
With attending officials, dragon-tiger riders,
Each clad in crimson caps,
Holding jade tablets,
Ascending to the Emperor’s court to report.
Burn incense.
From this moment henceforth,
Until the rites are complete,
All shall be conveyed with precision,
Lest any be omitted.

**Omissions:**
In the third month of each season, report to the Yellow Emperor;
In the fourth month of each season, report to the Five Emperors.

*End of Volume Six of The Great Law of the Jade Hall of the Three Heavens of the Supreme Mystery-Origin*
*(Note: The original small heading is missing; supplied based on the following text.)*

*Volume Seven of The Great Law of the Jade Hall of the Three Heavens of the Supreme Mystery-Origin*
**Chapter Eight: Communing with the True and Reaching the Numinous**

The Master said: Those of shallow learning, superficially devoted to the Three Treasures, are further deluded by the turbid world, mistakenly clinging to form and appearance as their own body and mind. Thus, their true origin is submerged. Amidst their frantic rushing about, they cannot commune with the true or reach the numinous—how lamentable!

Therefore, this chapter on "Communing with the True" is established, employing ritual dignity to guard against external distractions. Through the secret practice of incantations and hand seals, the scattered mind is gathered, so that the Dao may be revered through solemnity, and the heart may stand in awe through sacred forms, lest one fall into delusion and disorder.

As for those who cultivate immortality—whose minds are empty and natures still, whose Dao is complete and true—when a single thought moves, the hearts of the Two Heavens merge as one. Even so, they may rely on external ritual to commune with the true; how much more should they observe this with care!

**Talismans for Offering Incense to the Ten Directions**

The Master said: The jade talismans of the ten directions are the secret methods for summoning the Brahmā, inviting the true, communing with the numinous, petitioning the Emperor, and beseeching grace. At dawn, face east; at noon, face south; at dusk, face north. Visualize the *qi* of each direction filling the sacred altar.

**East:**
Swallow saliva nine times, knock the teeth nine times. Visualize green *qi* like clouds entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Nine *qi* of green origin,
Riding fragrant smoke in flight.
Summon the true, reach the numinous,
Guard me as I ascend as an immortal.

**South:**
Swallow saliva three times, knock the teeth three times. Visualize red *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Three *qi* in harmonious ascent,
Purple *qi* suffuses the firmament.
The Crimson Plowman turns his chariot,
The spirit ascends beyond all bounds.

**West:**
Swallow saliva seven times, knock the teeth seven times. Visualize white *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Seven *qi* of radiant brightness,
Western true ones, golden well.
The Emperor’s chariot swiftly descends,
Preserving life, rooting its essence.

**North:**
Swallow saliva five times, knock the teeth five times. Visualize black *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
The Black Emperor holds authority,
Five *qi* of the Great Mystery.
Lush and auspicious mists arise,
Rushing toward my immortal flight.

**Northeast:**
Swallow saliva four times, knock the teeth four times. Visualize green-black *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Brahmā *qi* arises naturally,
Paying homage to the Most Exalted.
Preserving and uniting life’s *qi*,
Pacifying the demon gate.

**Southeast:**
Swallow saliva six times, knock the teeth six times. Visualize green-crimson *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
True *qi* unites with yang,
Descending to the jasper altar.
A thousand true spirits gather,
Flying into the Jade Hall.

**Southwest:**
Swallow saliva eight times, knock the teeth eight times. Visualize red-white *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Numinous *qi*, clear and bright,
Uniting with the Dao to realize truth.
Subduing demons, executing the wicked,
Paying homage to the flying spirits.

**Northwest:**
Swallow saliva twice, knock the teeth twice. Visualize white-black *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Upright *qi*, vast and boundless,
Jade light of the mysterious altar.
Corpse-demons perish and fall,
Paying homage to my Primordial Emperor.

**Above:**
Swallow saliva twice, knock the teeth twice. Visualize golden-light *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Auspicious *qi* descends upon the altar,
Descending true ones, summoning immortals.
The Gate of Life opens above,
Embodying the Emperor’s precedence.

**Below:**
Swallow saliva ten times, knock the teeth ten times. Visualize black *qi* entering the altar.
*Incantation:*
Upright *qi* surges forth,
Dispelling evil, repelling miasma.
True visions well forth,
Descending true ones, summoning the numinous.

The Master said: After completing the incense offerings to the ten directions, establish the earthly portal and burn the talisman for entering the portal. Recite the incantation silently. After entering, take three steps with each movement, visualizing oneself amidst the Brahmā *qi* and numinous light above the Nine Heavens, utterly unaware of the mundane world.

At this point, inwardly observe, gather the spirit, and return the hearing. Be cautious not to look back, cough, or spit. Proceed directly to the grotto altar, offer incense three times, knock the teeth thirty-six times, and burn the talisman for communing with the true. Visualize green, yellow, and white *qi* of three colors emanating from within oneself.

One must visualize offering incense three times. With each offering, visualize three-colored *qi* emerging from the crown of the head, forming a flower canopy that ascends to the Three Heavens. Then, open the incense burner.

**Talisman for Communing with the True at the Grotto Altar**
*Incantation:*
Pure *qi* forms heaven,
Turbid *qi* forms earth.
Central *qi* forms humanity,
Yin and yang unerringly balanced.
With the heart, commune with heaven,
Heaven’s law is revered with utmost sincerity.
Cinnabar sincerity ascends,
*Qi*-registers dissolve transgressions.
From the beginning of profound obscurity,
Swiftly transmit the communion with the true.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in the statutes and ordinances!*

Incense is the jade blossom scattering light,
Nine *qi* congealing into mist.
Fragrant clouds densely woven,
Directly piercing the Nine Heavens.
Visualize the three-colored cloud canopy,
Rising with the smoke to reach the Three Heavens.
The Golden Lad attendant of incense,
The Jade Maiden transmitter of words.
I now submit this petition,
Heard before the Emperor.
Descend light, bestow *qi*,
Communing with the true to attain immortality.
Longevity and eternal vision,
Sins and transgressions all absolved.
Nine generations transcend suffering,
Ascending from the dark night.
Demon kings vouchsafe,
The Three Realms attend the chariot.
Merits and virtues fulfilled,
Ascending in a cloud-borne chariot.
Moving in and out naturally,
Attended and guarded by the Three Heavens.
All petitions and wishes,
Are granted as spoken.

**Talisman for Entering the Portal**
*Incantation:*
Entering to pay homage to the Emperor’s true ones,
Life’s *qi* in ninefold layers.
Interpenetrating the dharma-body,
Yin demons are not tolerated.
The Red Child of the Three Fields,
Preserves my immortal merit.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in the true statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman for Opening the Incense Burner**
*Incantation:*

**Talisman for Completing the Altar Rites**
*Incantation:*
The Mysterious Altar’s work is done,
The yang spirit guards within.
Seal my Gate of Life,
True *qi* shrouds in secrecy.
Ascending to the Emperor’s palace,
Lifespan matches Heaven’s.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in the true statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman for Restoring the Incense Burner**
*Incantation:*
Primordial *qi* of the Mysterious Origin,
Three merge to return to the One.
Brahmā’s *qi* pervades the cosmos,
No evil may enter.
Uproot the Earth’s Gate,
Receive the Jade Decree on high.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in the true statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman for Exiting the Portal #1**
*Incantation:*
Summon the gods of my body,
The Three and Five within.
Transcendent immortals, divine spirits,
Yang unites with yin.
Each returns to their palace,
Guarding my primordial essence.
Exiting the altar naturally,
No outer demons may invade.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in the primordial statutes and ordinances!*

The above are the Ten Directions’ Incense Talismans—those for the altar’s register, kindling the burner, restoring the burner, entering and exiting the portal—all inscribed with the Jade Purity mudra, the *qi* of the cinnabar field’s inner landscape, breath held while vermilion-script is brushed on yellow silk.

**Ritual Attire**
The Master says: Those who ascend to the Jade Hall’s realm, whose bodies approach the Three Purities, who enter the innermost sanctum—these are not the duties of the lower realms.

The Nine-Colored Cloud Robe is the attire of the Heavenly Master when attending the Jade Emperor’s chamber, the vestment of the Jade Hall.

**Three-Fold Girdle with Interwoven Yellow and Purple Qi Talisman**
*Jade Hall’s Proper Robe*
The robe is made of azure silk, embroidered with gold, bearing thirty-six cloud-*qi* patterns. At its center is inscribed the Great Talisman for Ascending the Hall. The girdle bears the talisman of interwoven yellow and purple *qi*, topped with a blue crown, crimson slippers, and a jade tablet.

**Talisman for Rolling Up the Curtain**
With the Jade Purity mudra, visualize the altar’s platform radiant as polished jade. Within the void, a single luminous point, like a millet grain. The Great Veil enfolds it, penetrating as a strung pearl, guarding the Yellow Chamber’s secret decree.

*Incantation:*
*Qi* of the Great Beginning,
Unwrought and spontaneous.
The void bears form,
Suspended from the empty mystery.
Encompassing the ten thousand beings,
Nurturing and transforming gods and immortals.
Seen yet unseen,
Heard yet untransmitted.
No before nor after,
Mystery upon mystery.
May the numinous creation open,
That I may behold the Mysterious Origin.

**Talisman for Summoning the Yang Spirit**
*Incantation:*
Primordial Beginning’s □ *qi*,
Silently moves the primordial essence.
Harmonizing tones, aligning rhythms,
Stirring the turbid, raising the pure.
Subtle *qi* of the profound void,
*Qi*-image in its first coagulation.
Spiraling through the empty vastness,
The sound within Heaven.
Gathering essence, descending *qi*,
Uttering the true voice.
Yin voices join in concert,
Summoning the ten thousand spirits.

**Talisman for Calling the Yin Spirit**
*Incantation:*
Stillness births movement,
Yin returns to generate yang.
The Great Sound enters the wondrous,
Echoing through the empty valley.
Voice responds to *qi*’s seeking,
Intermingling in harmony.
Voice answers voice,
Transforming the Mysterious Altar.
The sound of stirring yang,
Aligns with Heaven’s firmness.
Yang spirit intermingles,
True *qi* blends in peace.
Strike the golden bell once,
Tap the left tooth once.
Strike the jade chime once,
Tap the right tooth once.
Visualize the two *qi* within—left and right—intermingling,
Filling the Mysterious Altar.

*Thus concludes Scroll Seven of The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Rites.*

*Scroll Eight of The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Rites begins: Chapter Nine, "Subduing Demons and Overcoming Malevolence."*

The Master said: When Heaven loses its constancy, comets and shooting stars appear. When Earth loses its constancy, springs dry and mountains collapse. When creatures lose their constancy, blossoms scatter and seedlings wither. When seasons lose their constancy, winter thunders and summer snows. These are but Heaven’s portents to issue warning—naturally, there exist methods of preservation and control.

As for the calamities of common folk, they differ from these. There may be twin-headed serpents writhing in combat, wild beasts entering homes, birds shrieking at rooftops, phantom voices echoing before and behind, strange hues shifting high and low, vipers and pythons blocking paths in frenzied entanglement, chickens and dogs crowing or barking out of season, looms suddenly tangling, doors swinging open on their own, foxes circling walls, dragons and serpents slithering into wells—such manifold omens cannot be fully recounted.

For the noble person, virtue overcomes malevolence. For the petty person, the self is no match for malevolence. When one’s power wanes, how can disaster be averted? Yet if exorcism is performed, will fortune not return? Thus arise the methods of repelling and subduing.

The Master said: When Heaven and Earth grow dark and murky, and dragons or mirage-beasts enter household wells, one should use talismans to suppress them. The malevolence will vanish of itself and be unable to cause harm.

**Talisman for Repelling Dragons Entering Wells**
Assume the Northern Emperor Mudra, wield the *qi*-charged brush, recite the Dipper Taboo seven times, face the *gang* and inscribe the talisman on a fresh brick, then cast it into the water where the creature lurks.

**Talisman for Repelling Serpents Entering Wells**
Proceed with the same method as above.

**Method for Repelling Well Overflow**
Assume the Dipper Mudra and recite the incantation, face the *gang* and inscribe the talisman on yellow paper, then burn it in the well. Recite the incantation again to command it.

**Incantation:**
*"Hark! Dragon spirit, be pacified and guard the pure spring.
Malevolent vapors disperse, earthly specters conceal their forms.
O Clear and Cool Youth, receive the talisman and proclaim its decree.
Neither overflow nor dry up—fortune flows ceaselessly.
May the myriad spirits protect this immortal source.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Northern Emperor commands!"*

**Method for Repelling Canine Specters**
Inscribe the *wu* character, face the *yin-sha* direction, harness northern *qi*, recite the incantation seven times, and face the *gang* to write the talisman. Prepare four copies: one to burn in the hearth, three to nail above the privy. Recite the incantation again and spray water for great auspiciousness.

**Incantation:**
*"By jade decree, the exorcism descends—receive this sacred writ.
Malevolent beasts and hidden specters disturb the loyal and good.
Those who defy my incantation—let the hundred specters perish.
Those who violate my talisman—let the demonic vanish without trace.
Disaster cannot harm, calamity cannot wound.
May the myriad spirits guard and defend, ever bestowing good fortune.
Swiftly, swiftly, by the Northern Emperor’s command!"*

**Method for Repelling Crows Cawing Overhead**
Inscribe the *wu* character, harness southern *qi*, recite the incantation nine times, face south to write the talisman, then burn it in the open air. The specter will disperse, and good fortune will descend at once.

**Incantation:**
*"O divine bird, divine crow, universally bestow good fortune.
Though you gather and caw, you cannot bring misfortune.
Crow spirit, obey the command—where the talisman arrives, comply.
To fly is to bring blessing; to caw is to bring prosperity.
Through all twelve hours, may no harm or injury befall.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Vermilion Bird of the South shines with radiant decree!"*

**Method for Repelling Wild Beasts Entering Homes**
Shake the Dipper Mudra, face the *gang* to harness *qi*, recite the incantation twelve times, and inscribe the talisman on a wooden tablet. Nail it at the four corners of the house, and also write on yellow paper to burn in the central courtyard. Pace the Dipper while reciting the incantation, then spray water to command it—the specter will cause no harm.

**Incantation:**
*"By the might of the Celestial Stem, sweep away malevolent spirits.
Wild boars, seductive foxes, and the spirits of mountain specters—
Hasten a thousand *li* away; dare not linger.
Should any dare to trespass, behead them without form.
Where the *Kuigang* points, crush them to dust.
If you depart swiftly, I shall pardon your dark transgressions.
I uphold the great might and virtue of the Celestial Stem’s fiery decree!"*

**Method for Repelling Utensils That Sound, Break, or Move on Their Own**
Pace the Dipper *gang*, turn to face north, and inscribe three talismans facing the *gang*. Hang one in the central courtyard, burn one in the hearth, and affix one above the privy. Recite the incantation and spray water to remedy it.

**Incantation:**
*"By the divine might of the Celestial Stem, universally sweep away misfortune.
Suppress specters and pacify demons—let *chimei* conceal themselves.
Turn misfortune to fortune, transform calamity to blessing.
Those who dare defy this decree shall be seized by the *Kuigang*.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Northern Emperor commands!"*

**Method for Repelling Ghostly Voices Outside the Door at Night**
This portends the listener’s soul departing—a sign of impending death. Perform exorcism at once.

**Incantation:**
*"The Heavenly Emperor commands me to restrain and subdue spirits and specters.
Dare any demonic anomaly disturb my good people?
Yin and yang intermingle—mortals hear ghostly voices.
They harm the human soul, startling and disturbing the spirit.
Where the divine talisman arrives, seal the ghostly gate.
Depart swiftly, depart swiftly—dare not linger!
Swiftly, swiftly, by the Northern Emperor’s command!"*

**Method for Repelling Livestock Dying on Their Own**
Inscribe the *sha* character, recite the incantation three times, infuse the brush with eastern *qi* to write the talisman, and burn it where the livestock died. Burn another copy to fumigate—the specter will be unable to cause further harm, and peace will be restored.

**Incantation:**
*"I uphold Heaven’s decree to subdue misfortune and calamity.
How dare the specters of beasts and livestock bring harm?
By the radiance of the *gang*, drive them away and bestow good fortune.
May the myriad spirits guard and defend, gathering blessings for eternal prosperity.
Swiftly, swiftly, by the fiery decree of the Dipper *gang*!"*

**Method for Repelling Doors Closing on Their Own**
Assume the Flying Dipper Mudra, recite the incantation twelve times, harness northern *qi* to write the talisman, and burn it where the specter lingers. Affix another copy to the door—the specter will vanish, unable to cause harm, and the household will flourish with fortune and blessings.

**Incantation:**
*"The Star of Fortune shines brightly, the Three Luminaries illuminate clearly.
Radiant light pervades the eight directions, suppressing and sealing demonic spirits.
Disasters and misfortunes scatter—doors and gates become serene.
Myriad *qi* fill the defenses, naturally reviving prosperity.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Supreme Emperor commands!"*

**Method for Repelling Chickens Flying and Crowing Abnormally**
Inscribe the talisman on cypress wood and nail it to the east. Assume the Dipper Mudra to face the *gang* and harness *qi*, recite the incantation, and spray water—the specter will vanish, transforming misfortune into prosperity.

**Incantation:**
*"Before the sun rises, the golden rooster does not crow.
If it crows, it becomes a specter, harming my living spirits.
The Supreme has decreed to restrain and subdue demonic spirits.
Drive the specter ten thousand *li* away, dispelling misfortune and pacifying the mind.
All is auspicious, the human path is at peace.
I uphold the radiant canopy of the Dipper’s decree!"*

**Method for Repelling Serpent Specters**
Assume the Dipper Mudra, face the *gang* to write the talisman. If the specter appears as a human-faced being crouching on the wall, spray water to command it. Burn the talisman where the specter lingers, and have the afflicted person wear another copy. Write another on a brick and bury it beneath the local earth god’s shrine—great fortune will ensue, transforming calamity into blessing.

**Incantation:**
*"Hasten, hasten! Ten-thousand-*zhang* flying serpents—
Restrain and subdue disaster and peril; those who see you come to no harm.
Those who harm me—hasten to drive them away!
You are a lowly specter—dare not trouble me.
Those who violate my talisman shall be dismembered.
Forever mirror this auspicious ground, securely restrained without mishap.
Swiftly, swiftly, as commanded—by the blazing fire of Heaven’s might!"*

**Method for Repelling Rat Specters**
Assume the *zi* Mudra, harness northern *qi* to write the talisman, and hang it on a bamboo pole at the *zi* position—greatly auspicious.

**Incantation:**
*"Wu-su, seize! Yu-su, seize!
O parents of the vaulted heavens, with a thousand hundred kin—
I now recognize your specter and command it to cease.
I order you to restrain your specter and prevent it from acting.
Should you act recklessly, the Celestial Stem shall execute you.
I uphold the decree of the Dark Heavenly Emperor!"*

**Daily Talismans for Warding Off Specters and Repelling Evil**
Prepare twenty-two talismans, inscribing the day and branch on front and back according to the date. For example, if a specter appears on the *jiazi* day, write the *jia* talisman on the front and the *zi* talisman on the back, then carry it on your person.

**General Principles of Talisman-Writing**

All talismans must be inscribed with the Dipper Mudra, *gang qi*, and cinnabar ink. Have the afflicted person wear it to avert misfortune and attract auspicious omens. After inscribing the talisman, recite the *Great Exorcism Mantra* seven times to consecrate it.

**Mantra:**
*With the Sword Mudra, seven times—sprinkle water upon the afflicted.*
*"August Heaven births me, Heaven is my father.
August Earth bears me, Earth is my mother.
Sun and Moon harmonize in aid, above and below the Dipper shines.
The Northern Dipper’s *Kui Gang* slays evil in ten thousand directions.
Demons shall not become specters, evil shall not bring calamity.
Those who violate this talisman shall die; those who defy it shall perish.
Mysterious Yellow generates *qi*, universally bestowing good fortune.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Northern Dipper’s Seven Stars—destroy demons, slay specters—by decree!"*

**Additional Mantra:**
Before reciting, first direct the *qi* of the Three Lights to envelop the afflicted in a net of radiance. Then chant the mantra seven times, commanding the afflicted to retreat nine steps. Point the Dipper’s handle at them, summon them before you, and sprinkle water thrice. Affix the talisman to their person, and all specters shall forever cease their mischief.
*"The Most High issues the decree: slay ghosts, eliminate harm.
Heaven is my canopy, Earth is my foundation.
The Northern Dipper’s starlight is my raiment.
Left *Gang*, right Fire—banish and restrain inauspicious forces.
Return misfortune to fortune, dispel disaster and repel harm.
No evil shall invade; specters and demons shall retreat.
See the specter yet not be alarmed—its power shall crumble.
*Yuan Heng Li Zhen*—ten thousand years of prosperity.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the True Fire of the Crimson Heaven—by decree!"*

**Chapter Ten: Expelling Evil and Upholding Righteousness**

The Master said: *"Harmonizing the upright *qi* of Heaven and Earth is called a talisman. Humans receive the proper balance of yin and yang to be born—this is the Three Lights. Whenever cold, heat, wind, or summer heat transgress and cause injury, the transgression deviates from the upright; deviation from the upright becomes evil—not merely a curse, but a fundamental disorder. It must be remedied with the *qi* of the Three Lights. Thus it is said: Harmonizing the upright *qi* of Heaven and Earth is called a talisman. The Three Lights are how Heaven enacts transformations and governs spirits and demons. Therefore: the Sun is the essence of all yang; the stars are the essence of all yin; the Moon receives yang to shine. Where the Three Lights illuminate, rain, snow, and gloom dissipate without obstruction; fox demons and monstrous birds scatter without provocation. The sages and revered masters, borrowing the truth of divine incantations, looked upward to draw the essence of the Three Lights. We, too, harmonize them with sincerity, and the talisman unites with their numinous power. When yin evil encroaches upon a person—becoming a specter, a monstrosity, an illness, or a plague—it is like rain and snow manifesting, like fox demons and monstrous birds encountering broad daylight: it need not be driven away to vanish without a trace. Though talismanic scripts are many, which surpass the Five Lights? Thus, the Three Lights are placed first."*

**Talisman of the Three Lights**
This is the *Ancestral Talisman of the Three Lights*, the origin of all methods and the honor of the Three Realms. It annihilates all evil, preserves and harmonizes true *qi*, and its virtues cannot be fully described. A hundred thousand myriad transformations all emerge from this talisman, so its application is simple yet it is the foundation of all methods. Inscribe it in cinnabar on a square inch of lightweight paper, prepare three copies, and swallow them with jujube decoction. It cures all demonic afflictions and is called the *Talisman for Subduing Curses and Curing Evil*.

The Master said: *"Uprightness does not become evil. Thus, the method that destroys evil is the upright method. There is no need to curry favor with ghosts and spirits—it rests solely with the ritual master. Cultivate the Three Realms in the mind, ingest the Three Lights, and when inner cultivation is full, external evil will naturally submit."*

**Talisman of the Heavenly Canopy and Golden-Browed Lord Lao’s Transformation**
First visualize a golden light within the crown of the head. Lord Lao’s brows respond, his face golden. The practitioner silently recites the *Heavenly Canopy’s* original mantra once, twice, thrice, and beholds the Golden-Browed Lord Lao ascending into the void, transforming into the true form of the Heavenly Canopy. Recite the original mantra, then inscribe the talisman’s *qi*-slaying form with the brush. With a single stroke of the divine blade, write the Sword Talisman, followed by the command characters. *"Hastily obey the Northern Emperor’s decree!"* Use the Northern Emperor’s Mudra, inscribe on yellow paper with cinnabar, one foot and six inches in length, and fumigate the afflicted.

**Talisman of the Dipper’s *Kui* and Great Virtue’s Fire**
First visualize the Seven Stars of the Dipper in the sky, the *Gang* star pointing forward. Step into the Dipper, absorb *qi* into the abdomen, and feel warmth. Then begin writing, exhaling *gang qi* to guide the brush. Inscribe the talisman.

**Three Primordials’ Ding-Jia Response Talisman**
When inscribing this talisman, step into the Dipper to greet the *Gang*, visualize the Celestial *Gang* on the red paper, grind cinnabar facing the sun, grasp the *Gang* Mudra, and inscribe with a single breath. When dispatching the talisman, burn gold coins and *Jia* horses beforehand.

**Seven Slayings Talisman**
This talisman possesses great power, subduing fierce evil, destroying malevolent shrines, and eliciting divine responses—its wonders cannot be fully described. Step into the Dipper, grasp the Dipper Mudra, inscribe with *qi*, paper, and ink, face the *Gang*, exhale fire to activate it, and burn it in the central courtyard. This talisman has been corrected by the Three Heavens and proclaimed to ancestral altars, with extraordinary efficacy.

The Master said: *"The Seven Slayings Talisman has been transmitted through the ages, but its talismanic script was unclear, and many uses failed. Now, with the rise of the Teaching Master and the flourishing of the Great Teaching, all Northern Pole talismans and documents from the Jade Altar have been requested, decreed, and bestowed here. Scattered, its form is wondrously subtle; gathered, its form is mighty and brave."*

**Dipper-*Gang* Talisman**
This talisman is simple yet divinely efficacious, requiring no embellishment or elaborate application. Formed into pills, it can be ingested or fumigated; when worn, *Gang* fire spans the heavens, and ghosts and spirits dare not approach. Use the Dipper Mudra and northern *qi*.

**Talisman Summoning and Commanding Mantra**
*"Riding the *Kui*, opposing the *Gang*, blazing with dragon fire.
Above Heaven, below Earth—annihilate inauspicious forces.
Should any dare resist, they shall be reduced to flying ash.
Plunge ten thousand fathoms into the earth, follow the talisman’s path—never to return for ten thousand kalpas.
Solemnly summon the Heavenly Generals within the talisman to accompany and guard it.
Those who violate the talisman’s command shall be shattered by thunderbolts.
Fire decree, fire decree—by the Emperor’s command, act!
Flowing fire for ten thousand miles—no ghost shall escape its form.
Swiftly, swiftly, by decree!"*

*Concluding Volume Eight of the* Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method.
*Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
*Scripture Title:* Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method.

Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty fascicles.
Source text: *Zhengtong Daoist Canon*, Dongzhen Section, Methods Category.

*Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Fascicle Nine*
*Chapter Eleven: Summoning and Subjugation of the Nether Prison*

The Master said: For those mountain specters lingering through kalpas, water spirits haunting for years, celestial demons and heterodox ways, blood-feasting deities, the Five Penetrations beneath trees, vengeful ghosts of execution and violent death—those who gather in bands, cling to ancient shrines, usurp imperial titles and call themselves kings, or presume to style themselves Grand Marshals; those who extort temple construction, drag forth village festivals, debauch women, occupy towers, drip blood and hurl bricks, manifest forms and set fires, afflict people with malignant illness, and swiftly seize living souls—such monstrous harms are beyond remedy by ordinary methods. In our great teaching, there is the method of the Nine Springs Nether Prison to govern them.

The establishment of the prison must not be undertaken lightly. First, one must receive a petition, then issue talismans to drive and govern the offender, and dispatch proclamations to announce the decree. If they fear the law and flee, permit them to reform and renew themselves, and there is no need to proceed with subjugation—only that the human realm may be at peace. But if the demonic spirits are defiant, resisting the true method and unafraid of talismans, then this method must be employed to govern them.

The Master said: To establish the prison, first memorialize the Supreme Emperor and the Northern Dipper Mansion’s Sagely Masters, dispatching celestial soldiers and officials to descend to the designated place, build the Nether Prison, and apprehend the demonic thieves. At night, select a clean chamber and use lime to delineate the prison’s boundaries. Then post proclamations, talismanic scripts, and notices. First, divide the sections and dispatch generals and officials to pursue and capture the demonic thieves, as well as to restrain the local earth gods, city gods, and subordinate spirit officials, all bound by the Middle Punishment Talisman. Set a time limit for their capture. Next, recite the *Spell for Capturing Ghosts* and patrol the prison. Place one lamp in each prison. At dawn the following day, the ritual master burns incense and performs the rites as before. Observe their traces, and if necessary, issue talismans to hasten the capture. If the demonic band is not fully apprehended, perform the rites again at night as before. During this time, on certain nights, one may hear the sounds of interrogation and punishment—be reverent and respectful. If after one or two days no traces are found, and it is the celestial demons or heterodox ways clinging to evil, one must again memorialize the Celestial Masters to urge the dispatch of officials, who will then surely appear. After seven days, the prison may be dismantled. If among them there are truly unforgivable demonic ghosts, those whose forms are to be destroyed must have a separate *Great Mystery Demon-Slaying Altar* constructed.

**Method for Establishing the Nine Springs Prison**
The Master said: The Nine Springs are the Nether Springs of Fengdu in the Northern Capital, a prison for the wicked. This matter concerns the Celestial Court and must not be undertaken lightly. Thus, Fengdu is the office of all the world’s ghosts and spirits, wielding the authority to restrain and control demonic and malevolent forces. No proclamation of might is greater than this.

The prison consists of nine divisions:
1. **Feng Spring Command Prison**
2. **Heavy Spring Decapitation Prison**
3. **Yellow Spring Pursuit Prison**
4. **Cold Spring Poison Harm Prison**
5. **Yin Spring Dark Night Prison**
6. **Nether Spring Slaying Prison**
7. **Lower Spring Eternal Night Prison**
8. **Bitter Spring Massacre Prison**
9. **Drowning Spring Interrogation and Burning Prison**

Each of the nine prisons has its designated jurisdiction:
1. The first prison governs celestial demons.
2. The second prison governs negligent temple officials.
3. The third prison governs mountain specters and goblins.
4. The fourth prison governs river and lake water spirits.
5. The fifth prison governs blood-feasting evil deities.
6. The sixth prison governs the tree-dwelling Five Penetrations.
7. The seventh prison governs corpses hidden in ancient tombs.
8. The eighth prison governs sorcerers and rebellious ghosts.
9. The ninth prison governs those who died by execution or violent death.

Before each prison, arrange Dipper Lamps, each one foot two inches in diameter, with a two-foot-four-inch *qi* path. Before each of the nine prisons, hang a *Talisman for Pursuing Ghosts*, and within, hang a *Heavy Punishment Talisman*. At the prison gate, suspend a bamboo pole three feet long, bearing the *Proclamation for Pursuing Ghosts*. At the main gate, hang the *Talisman for Blocking Ghost Roads*. Thrice daily, at the three periods, offer incense and perform the rites. At dawn, observe the traces to discern the nature of the ghost. For minor offenses, bind and restrain them; for greater offenses, condemn them to the Three Paths of heavy labor; for the gravest offenses, erase their traces and destroy their forms.

**Talismans:**
1. **Talisman for Blocking Ghost Roads** – Can subdue all evil, restrain and pacify the myriad demons. When placed in a residence, no evil shall intrude.
   Write it with the *Northern Emperor’s Seal Script*.

**Prison Talismans:**
1. **First Talisman**
2. **Middle Punishment Talisman**
3. **Lower Punishment Talisman**
   Use three talismans, written with the *Northern Emperor’s Seal Script*. Hang one in the prison, and use one to pursue ghosts. In ordinary times, they may also be used to guard residences—ghosts and spirits dare not look upon them directly, and those who do shall be bound and shackled.

**Great Mystery Demon-Slaying Altar**
The Master said: The establishment of the *Great Mystery Demon-Slaying Altar* is the pivot of celestial punishment, subduing all flying and earthbound demonic spirits and malevolent beings, truly eradicating the ferocious deities of mountains, forests, temples, and shrines. This is not for those who have not truly violated our teaching’s laws—it must not be undertaken lightly.

**Method for Establishing the Altar:**
Use floating sand to draw a three-tiered altar. The top tier is one *zhang* wide, the middle tier two *zhang*, and the lower tier three *zhang*. If the space is confined, adjust as needed. On the top tier, arrange the Celestial Masters and the Four Saints. On the middle tier, outside the Heavenly Gate, array the various generals, and before the Heavenly Gate, place the demon-slaying generals and officials, surrounding them with spirit talismans. At the four corners, establish gates, beginning from the *Qian* position:
1. **Qi of Expelling Corpses and Sweeping Away Wrongs** – Gate for the descent and summoning of celestial generals.
2. **Qi of Drowning and Clarity**
3. **Gate of Orthodox Unity for Driving Away Evil**
4. **Qi of Primordial Green Yang Brightness**
5. **Qi of Severing Ghosts and Cutting Off Demons** – Gate for the merging of immortals and entry into sagehood.
6. **Qi of Red Brightness and Cavern Yang**
7. **Qi of Longevity and Tranquility** – Gate for the entry and exit of living spirits.

Eight: **Qi of Unyielding Rectitude and Stern Clarity**—Gate for the invocation of celestial generals.

At the Heavenly Gate, set up an incense table to summon and receive the descent of celestial generals. The Earthly Portal shall remain sealed to all passage, the ghostly paths forever closed, with only the Human Gate left open for transit. On the lower tier, array troops and cavalry in full encirclement, burning talismans morning and night. When the rite is performed with clarity for one or two days, the ghosts will perish of themselves, or one may hear the sound of wailing and weeping, or blood may be spilt upon the altar—all signs of its efficacy.

This method is not to be employed lightly, but reserved solely for cases of formidable demonic hordes, tangible apparitions, or monstrous anomalies that defy all other remedies.

**Altar Design**
The Master says: Ghosts formed from the Five Phases and spirits attached to mountains and rivers do not rely on human souls to attain sentience. Objects crafted by human hands, if imbued with even fleeting potency, may over time become haunted, capable of shifting form and assuming guises to harm people and disrupt the world—often more pernicious than ordinary ghosts. Thus, the Most High established this singular method to subdue them.

When erecting a demon-slaying altar, burn talismans at the Ghost Gate thrice daily, each time reciting the *Tianpeng* incantation and spraying the breath upon them. Within three days, profound responses will manifest.

This is a matter personally overseen by the Northern Dipper, of grave import—far beyond the scope of ordinary talismanic arts. It must never be invoked except in the face of the most extreme demonic infestations, lest severe retribution be incurred. Exercise utmost caution.

**Talisman of the Northern Emperor for Slaying Mountain and Stone Spirits**
This talisman subdues mountain spirits, stone spirits, millennia-old steles, stone Buddhas, stone figures, stone beasts, stone tortoises, and stone dragons. Inscribe it in black ink on black paper and deliver it to the afflicted, then burn it at the site of the haunting.

If the spirit appears in human form, consorting with women or seducing men and women, await its arrival and burn this talisman upon its approach.

**Talisman of the Northern Emperor for Slaying Wood Spirits**
This talisman subdues tree spirits, woodwights, millennia-old pine-dwelling ghosts, locust tree deities, wooden idols, wooden beasts, withered trees, and hollow trees that harbor spirits. Inscribe it in cinnabar on a slip of catalpa or cypress, then drive it into the tree, which will wither and die.

If the spirit manifests to harm the people, inscribe the talisman on yellow paper and burn it—the spirit will be violently destroyed.

**Talisman of the Northern Emperor for Subduing Metal Spirits**
This talisman governs spirits of gold, silver, copper, and iron, including millennia-old bronze Buddhas and statues. If the day of their casting coincided with inauspicious or malevolent influences, true numen will not descend, and demonic forces will attach themselves instead.

Inscribe this talisman in cinnabar on an iron plaque and secretly bury it beneath the statue—the ghostly spirit will flee, and the haunting will cease, regardless of whether the statue is later destroyed.

**Talisman of the Northern Emperor for Slaying Water Spirits**
This talisman subdues all water spirits, including those dwelling in rivers, seas, lakes, marshes, deep pools, springs, and wells—such as jiao, shen, serpents, pythons, and wayward dragons—whose forms vary but all possess the power to stir winds and waves, capsize boats, and claim lives.

If they assume shapes to consort with women or seduce the living, burn this talisman, and the spirits will perish utterly. Inscribe it on yellow paper, affix it to an iron tablet, and cast it into the water before burning.

**Talisman of the Northern Emperor for Subduing Ape and Spectral Spirits**
This talisman subdues all ape spirits—gibbons, macaques, foxes, wild boars—and spectral entities such as corpse-possessing dogs, oxen, horses, and other beasts with intact remains, collectively termed *xiao*.

For those afflicted by such spirits where other remedies fail, inscribe the talisman in cinnabar on blue-green paper, then wear it, affix it, or burn it—the spirit will die of itself.

**Talisman of the Northern Emperor for Slaying Blood-Consuming Demons**
This talisman subdues all blood-consuming demons inhabiting shrines, temples dedicated to ancient worthies, abandoned estates, empty halls, pavilions, and gardens—where malevolent ghosts gather in bands, usurping scenic sites, seizing dwellings, snatching souls, seducing women, invading dreams with feasts and songs, or possessing mediums to demand temples and sacrifices, committing myriad transgressions.

Inscribe this talisman in cinnabar on catalpa wood and drive it into the site. Then deliver another copy to the afflicted household to be nailed in the central hall—the demonic activity will cease.

Though these six talismans govern distinct afflictions, their application is uniform. When inscribing them, visualize oneself as Tianpeng. When deploying them, do likewise. Apart from distributing talismans to households or nailing them in place, burn them thrice daily at the demon-slaying altar while reciting the *Tianpeng* incantation.

To execute a spirit, cut its talisman in two at the Ghost Gate—the entity will perish. Great omens will follow: wailing in the void, blood upon the altar—all signs of its efficacy.

Here ends *Scroll Nine of the Supreme Mystery of the Three Heavens and the Jade Hall of the Great Dao*.

**Supreme Mystery of the Three Heavens and the Jade Hall of the Great Dao**
*Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.*
*Source: Zhengtong Daoist Canon, Dongzhen Section, Methods Category.*

**Scroll Ten of the Supreme Mystery of the Three Heavens and the Jade Hall of the Great Dao**
**Chapter Twelve: Expelling, Purging, Exorcising, and Averting Calamities**

The Master said: To expel and dispel malign forces is called *gua*. To eliminate inauspicious and malevolent influences is called *fu*. To sever demonic bonds and break curses is called *guai*. To suppress misfortune and dissolve disasters is called *rang*. Though these four bear different names, their use in aiding the world yields the same benefit.

All who dwell between Heaven and Earth are bound within the Five Phases, and few escape their cycles of generation and destruction. Thus fortune and misfortune arise, and success or ruin, prosperity or decline, cannot be foreseen. Without the secrets of exorcism and averting calamities, how can one ensure enduring good fortune? For this reason, this chapter expounds upon these methods in detail.

**Method for Subduing the Earth Duke and Earthbound Spirits**
The Master said: Since the Three Powers were divided and the Five Phases separated, the interplay of generation and destruction has given rise to fortune and misfortune. In all actions, regret and adversity follow—such is the work of the Earth Duke’s spirits, ever causing peril. When households construct dwellings, dig ponds, relocate mountains, or seal tombs, the deities govern every corner and direction. Should one violate their norms, disaster swiftly follows. Thus, the Most High has devised methods to subdue and pacify them, ensuring each remains in its proper place and no longer harms the living or invites calamity. The treatment is uniform; the methods are listed below.

**Talisman for Pacifying Earth and Ensuring Safety**
This talisman is addressed to [Name], the Year Star of the *jiazi* cycle, and all deities under the Tai Sui. By command of the Most High, you are to comply: as [Household Name] undertakes construction, disturbing the spirits and baleful forces, upon receipt of this talisman, return to guard your respective directions, each resuming its rightful place. Avert misfortune, dissolve disaster, and bestow eternal good fortune. As decreed.

**Talisman for Dispelling Earth Qi**
This talisman is specifically for subduing the Earth Duke and severing the one hundred and twenty baleful influences. When inscribing it, transform into the Heavenly Master, infuse the brush with *qi* of the Dipper, and blow upon it while writing. Inscribe in cinnabar on yellow paper and affix it to the central courtyard.

The Master said: For the method of subduing *fulian*, first arrange the Dipper’s image in a purified chamber, offer sacrifices to the *fulian* deities, and then have the household wear the talisman.

**Talisman of the Most High for Severing *Fulian***
This talisman severs the male and female baleful forces. Place it in a crimson pouch and wear it.

**Talisman for Prohibiting Mourning Visits and *Fulian***
Seal the corners with yellow paper, inscribe in cinnabar, and announce its burning to the Tai Sui’s direction—auspiciousness will flourish.

This talisman is addressed to the Tai Sui, baleful deities, malevolent forces, male and female baleful influences, *Sangmen*, *Diaoke*, and all such spirits. By this talismanic command, return to your original positions and cease allowing baleful influences to harm the living. As this decree takes effect, depart swiftly without delay. As decreed.

**Talisman for Prohibiting Tomb Litigation**

**Breaking *Zhu* in the East, Refining Corpses in the South, Expelling Calamities in the West, Repelling Disasters in the North, and Severing Corpses in the Center**

The Azure Mystery and Supreme Mystery Woman Azure *Duan Zhu* Talisman is addressed to the spirit officials of the Eastern One-Nine Bureau. It opens the path for so-and-so, stabilizes their physical form, and nourishes their *ying* and *wei* protective qi, preventing the Earth Officials from driving or pressing upon them. As decreed by Woman Azure.

The Master says: In cases of tomb litigation, the household of descendants will not prosper, and misfortunes will frequently arise. It is fitting to employ this method to deliver the deceased ancestors, so that blessings may extend to descendants, and the afflictions of *yang zhu* will be forever dispelled.

The Master says: Take a fine stone, two feet and four inches in length and one foot and two inches in width. Engrave upon it the Five Talismans and bury it within the tomb, approximately thirty paces from the burial site, at a depth of three feet, in a pit three feet square. Each time a talisman is buried, recite the middle chapter of the *Divine Book*, perform the Yu Step to the *Kan* position, and inter it. This method can transcend and subdue yin corpses, extend blessings to descendants, bring prosperity to the household, and forever eliminate the afflictions of tomb litigation and *yang zhu*.

**Method for Dispelling Curses**

The Master says: Those afflicted by curses will suffer from inverted hun and shen, scattered essence and po, external illnesses that linger, and may even meet their demise—truly pitiable. Some harbor private grudges and practice their malevolent arts in spirit halls or unorthodox temples, extending misfortune to descendants. There exists a method to exorcise such afflictions.

**Eastern Azure Emperor’s Talisman for Dispelling Curses**
**Southern Vermilion Emperor’s Talisman for Dispelling Curses**
**Western White Emperor’s Talisman for Dispelling Curses**
**Northern Black Emperor’s Talisman for Dispelling Curses**
**Central Yellow Emperor’s Talisman for Dispelling Curses**

**General Petition Formula for the Five Directions**
Inscribe on yellow paper with cinnabar, perform the offering ritual, and then it shall be auspicious.

This talisman is addressed to the Eastern Curse Spirit Bureau to dispel the curses afflicting so-and-so’s household, the entanglements of vengeful oaths upon the clan, or self-inflicted curses that bring misfortune. By this talismanic command, swiftly depart to another direction. As decreed.

**Method for Ensuring Progeny and Continuing the Lineage**

The Master says: When descendants are difficult to obtain, whether due to prolonged infertility, miscarriage, failure to thrive, or lack of intelligence, it is often because the feng shui of previous generations has unknowingly violated *guansha*, severing the generative qi. One should perform an offering to the Six Jia Direct Talismans, beseeching the issuance of a talismanic command to nurture the primordial qi, foster the growth of the spiritual root, and ensure the flourishing of descendants.

**Talisman for Conception**
This talisman is for women who are barren or unable to conceive. It is fitting to establish a Six Jia ritual arena, inscribe the talisman facing the direction of the recipient’s life destiny, and have her wear it. Results will manifest within one hundred and twenty days.

**Talisman for Protecting the Fetus**
Inscribe this talisman on yellow paper with cinnabar and have the pregnant woman wear it—it shall be auspicious.

**Talisman for Securing the Birthing Chamber**
Inscribe three talismans on yellow paper with cinnabar and hang them in the birthing chamber, on the bed curtains, or where the mother rests. This will ensure no difficulties in childbirth.

All the aforementioned talismans should be inscribed while holding the Dipper Mudra, facing the direction of the prosperous *qi* of the *Gang*. Their efficacy will be as swift as an echo.

**The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Scroll Ten—Concluded**

**The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method**
**Title:** *The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.
Source: *Daoist Canon*, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category.

**The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Scroll Eleven**
**Chapter Thirteen: Extending Life and Delivering from Calamity**

The Master says: Alas! Those of shallow learning lose their minds in the realm of worldly toil, while officials in the marketplace bury their heads in the pursuit of profit and rank. They desire to prolong life but have no means to extend it; they wish to escape calamity but have no method to deliver themselves. Thus, fate is determined by destiny, and misfortunes arise from tangible causes. For all disasters and dangers, one should rely on exorcism and thanksgiving rituals.

Yet the ritual gates are vast, and the Daoist methods numerous. Their efficacy varies in depth, and their effects differ in speed. Only the teachings of the Jade Hall’s Orthodox Unity, passed down through the ages, open the gate to exorcising disasters and atoning for transgressions, revealing the secrets of preserving life and extending longevity. They enable the people to avoid premature death, each safeguarding their allotted years. Truly, they serve as a bridge to transcend the world and a refuge for humanity and the heavens—how could their merit be but a small contribution?

The Master says: For men or women suffering from deep calamities or grave misfortunes, afflicted by chronic illnesses and confined to bed, or entangled in official litigation with years of household unrest, it is fitting to purify the mind and perform an offering to the Northern Dipper. Follow the ancient method to arrange the altar: lay out four clean mats around the perimeter. Choose a secluded courtyard or quiet chamber, a place undisturbed by others, where one may concentrate the spirit and sincerely invoke a response.

Place the true image against the northern wall, spread the altar before it, and position the Seven Primordial Lamps at the center. Arrange the offerings around the perimeter. Select auspicious days such as the Three Primordials, Eight Nodes, one’s life destiny birthday, the Northern Dipper’s Descending Day, the Five La Festivals, the Two She Festivals, *Gengshen* or *Jiazi* days—provided they do not conflict with the Emperor’s Harsh Days—to ensure the ritual’s efficacy.

The method for petitioning the Dipper requires submitting the memorial a day in advance and also invoking the Two Immortals, Qing and Tuo, to descend and inspect the altar site. When the night deepens, perform the ritual according to the prescribed rites. Do not let the mind wander or the proceedings falter—surely, a favorable response will manifest.

**Required Items**
None may be omitted. As for the altar’s stabilizing offering, it may vary according to one’s means—presence or absence is not an issue, and thus it is not specified here.
Four mats.
Nine candles.

Two catties of sesame oil. Nine portions of seasonal fruits. One catty of *jiangzhen* incense. Three taels of agarwood. Half a tael of frankincense. One tael of blended incense. Half a tael of borneol. One catty of *maoxiang* grass. One tael of cinnabar. One tael of vermilion. Twenty sheets of yellow paper. Two *ge* of light fermented soybeans, soaked. Ninety oil cakes. Half a tael of ginseng. Half a tael of *fuling* (poria). One *ge* each of glutinous rice, broomcorn millet, foxtail millet, wheat, and red beans. Forty-nine stalks of *suanzi* grass. Nine brushes. Twenty-four feet of yellow *Dao* silk. Twenty sheets of memorial paper.

The master instructs: The ritual master shall proceed to the altar site during the *xu* and *hai* hours. Beneath the mats, spread white cogon grass. The ritual table shall be placed one *zhang* away from the mats. First, ingest the *Entering the Chamber* talisman. Prepare the *Altar Diagram* and the *Bright Lamp* talisman. The lamp bowls—whether large or small—must contain the same amount of oil and wicks; no additions or subtractions are permitted, nor may the wicks be adjusted beforehand. The ritual master shall light them with paper tapers. In spring and summer, begin from [omitted character]; in autumn and winter, begin from [omitted character]. Hold the breath, then place the talismans into the lamps in the prescribed order. Beneath each lamp, hang seven talismans on banners.

*Talisman for Beneath the Lamp*
*Talisman for Within the Lamp*

**Upper Terrace Preservation-Spirit Talisman**
**Middle Terrace Pacification-Soul Talisman**
**Lower Terrace Summoning-Corporeal-Soul Talisman**

Once the Seven Stars shine clearly, recite the incantation:

*"Heaven is profound, earth is shallow,
Sun and moon revolve in turn.
The Five Stars course eternally,
Moving my celestial image above.
I establish this altar—
Ten thousand ghosts all submit.
With one stroke of the divine blade,
Ten thousand ghosts scatter in flight.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by law and command!"*

Next, circumambulate the distant lamps three times, reciting:

*"Bright lamps seize the light,
Wandering spirits do not flee.
The seven corporeal souls rest in place,
All spirits return in submission.
Like the sun at midday,
Ever abide in radiance.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by law and command!"*

Recite again:

*"Following the *gang* to erect the Dipper,
The ritual torch illuminates the celestial stars.
The Seven Sovereigns descend—
Primordial, prosperous, advantageous, steadfast.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by law and command!"*

**First: Longevity-Extending Talisman**
Stand facing forward; burn one talisman per lamp.

**Second: Calamity-Averting Talisman**
**Third: Life-Preserving Talisman**
**Fourth: Lifespan-Augmenting Talisman**
**Fifth: Disaster-Dispelling Talisman**
**Sixth: Misfortune-Dispersing Talisman**
**Seventh: Decline-Supporting Talisman**

Next, stand at the center and invoke:

*"Reverently summon the Wealth Star Lamp of the Chu division—surnamed Rao, named Li—clad in white, descend now.
Reverently summon the Longevity Star Lamp of the Jin division—surnamed Wang, named Yin—clad in purple, descend now.
Reverently summon the Fortune Star Lamp of the Zhao division—surnamed Xu, named Gai—clad in blue-green, descend now.
Reverently summon the Destiny Star Lamp of the Zeng division—surnamed Fan, named Zheng—clad in black, descend now.
Reverently summon the Male and Female Star Lamp of the Zheng division—surnamed Sima, named Lu—clad in crimson, descend now.
Reverently summon the Wife Star Lamp of the Wei division—surnamed Ji, named Qian—clad in crimson, descend now.
Reverently summon the Blessing Star Lamp of the Yan division—surnamed Long, named Deng—clad in crimson, descend now."*

Next, offer incense, bow three times before each lamp, and observe the lamps.

Circumambulate the distant lamps three times, silently reciting the incantation forty-nine times, then divine fortune or misfortune by the lamp’s light.

*"Reverently summon the Seven Perfected to descend and receive this petition and proclamation.
By the lamp’s brightness or dimness, know fortune or misfortune.
By the power of the majestic spirits,
Ten thousand wishes all comply."*

When divining by the lamps, observe with a pure heart.
If the lamp burns brightly, it is auspicious.
If dim, it is inauspicious.
If it flickers repeatedly, it is inauspicious and unfavorable; one must earnestly perform expiatory rites.
For unclear omens, base the interpretation on the affairs governed by the respective star.

If the lamp’s light does not return, prepare in advance a black robe, black bellyband, and black headwrap, each inscribed with a talisman, and wear them—let no one see, and if asked, do not answer. This may also be done before sleep at night.

If a lamp’s flame is blue-green: it indicates a dormant corpse.
If red: wandering baleful lights, blood taboos, or malevolent ghosts.
If white: legal disputes at the household gate, or illness that will not heal.
If black: illness or inauspiciousness.
If yellow: affliction by earthly pestilence.
If bright then dim, dim then bright: ghosts and spirits cause disorder.
If it fails to light at first, or the oil bowl is overturned: *xiao* ghosts swarm, laboring insects fly and crouch, and the sick will not recover.

In such cases, proceed as with the garments above.
If the Fortune or Longevity Star’s lamp dims, it likewise requires expiation with black headgear.

The Master says: *"For divining household affairs, use the seven lamps collectively, regardless of the specific matter at hand.
One must avoid the presence of sparrow hawks, dogs, cats, monks, nuns, or women, for their defilement will pollute the altar, preventing the descent of the lofty Perfected and instead inviting transgression."*

**Expiatory Lamp Talisman for Resolving and Dispelling Inauspiciousness**
Write the talisman while reciting the incantation;

**Northern Emperor’s Incantation**
Inscribe upon black garments or write on yellow paper and place within the garments.
Recite the incantation:
*"Supreme divine talisman,
resolves and dispels inauspiciousness.
Radiant light preserves life,
averts calamity and prolongs existence.
Alter form, change attire,
black baleful forces remove misfortune.
Encircling the floral canopy,
clothed in the light of the Dipper.
Evil cannot harm,
ghosts cannot injure.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

**Seven Talismans for the Offering Ritual**
Recite the incantation:
*"Zǐ Xīn, Primordial Lady,
governs and manifests the soul.
Luminous splendor curves and reflects,
illuminating the dark and obscure.
Grant your majestic radiance,
true qi unites with the soul.
Master’s body and mind,
where spirit and qi converge,
bestow longevity.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

Recite the incantation:
*"Sacred spirit within Zǐ,
radiance and light preserve the true.
Jade brilliance scatters mist,
sun and moon race as one.
Uphold this servant’s fate,
nurture the spleen’s hun-soul.
Master’s hun-soul and spirit,
where spirit and qi converge,
bestow peace and tranquility.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

Recite the incantation:
*"Zǐ Huì, Great Sage,
luminous and mystically penetrating.
Divine perfection, jade majesty,
ascends to the dark heavens.
May this servant’s name in the register of fate
endure eternally without end.
Master’s essence and spirit,
infused through the hundred passages,
nurture qi and pacify the spirit.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

Recite the incantation:
*"Zǐ Zhèng, Scribe of Destiny,
broadly delivers the multitudes.
The people’s fortune and misfortune
all belong to the azure vault.
Bestow reversal of ill fortune,
preserve life and extend its span.
Guard the human spirit and soul,
protect life and increase its years,
qi attains peace and tranquility.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

Recite the incantation:
*"Zǐ Tōng, Master of the Yin,
let this servant’s emotions flow freely.
Three measures drift into the vast,
the body enters the mysterious numen.
Life is preserved naturally,
bestow longevity.
Irrigate the bodily form,
inscribe merit and conduct,
master joy and harmony.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

*"Zǐ Chōng, Black Emperor of the North,
let the command enter the subtle and profound.
This servant prays to the Dao/Way,
the mandate aligns with the mysterious mechanism.
Merit reaches the wondrous extreme,
ascending to ride the cloudy regalia.
Majesty subdues Heaven and Earth,
the master attains long life,
greatly bestowed with numinous power.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

Recite the incantation:
*"Zǐ Cháng, Breaker of Armies,
numinous power is most revered.
Radiant light spouts flames,
greatly bestowed with majestic spirit.
Grant long life,
eternal peace for the soul.
Majesty subdues ghosts and spirits,
sever and eradicate malevolent ghosts,
the Dipper’s calculations bind the numinous.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance."*

For the talisman and incantation: burn one talisman, recite the incantation once, and bow. Combine this with the Mudra of the Northern Emperor. Upon completion of the recitation, pace the Dipper to the altar and present the memorial.

**Oral Instructions:**
The master says: First, concentrate the spirit and stabilize the will, pace the Dipper and bow nine times. Then, emerge as an official, pace the Dipper again, visualize the primordial qi of the Mysterious and Yellow, and imagine the body seated at the Dipper’s mouth. The five viscera emit their original-colored qi, coalescing into a precious cloud, a golden bridge ascending to the Central Heaven. Next, together with the officials and clerks, carry the memorial up the bridge. Midway, encounter an emissary in embroidered robes, who receives the memorial and departs. In a moment, the petitioner is led to the Stellar Palace. After the audience concludes, after a long while, golden light ten thousand fathoms long emanates as the Nine Sovereigns emerge from their palace. Flying rays like cinnabar enter the petitioner’s crown. One sees the light penetrating the hundred bones, senses the body suffused with warmth and radiance, the light ascending through the crown and reddening the face—this is true yang nurturing the form, and the prayer will surely be answered.

The master says: The Northern Dipper is the Central Dipper. The Great Chief of the Central Dipper oversees all spirits; it is the revered Northern Dipper, to which the myriad numina of the Three Realms, celestial gods, and earthly deities all submit. Moreover, the lives of ordinary people belong entirely to the Northern Dipper. When faced with calamity or adversity, how can one not contemplate means of supplication and exorcism? This section on extending life is uniquely detailed in the memorial to the Dipper. Those who study this may regard it as a treasure for saving the world. Revere it, revere it.

*Thus concludes Volume Eleven of the* Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method.
*Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
**Scripture Title:** *Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty volumes.
Source edition: *Daoist Canon of the Zhengtong Era*, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category.

*Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Volume Twelve*
*Chapter Fourteen: Augmenting Blessings and Longevity*

The Master said: The scriptures state that the Southern Dipper governs the Li Palace, its name shared with the sun, and the spirit it bestows upon humans is called the *hun*. It presides over the yang offices, administering the Fire Emperor, and in its dynamic application, no virtue surpasses it. Together with the Northern Dipper’s Seven Governors, it shares the duty of governance. In times of urgent peril, one should perform rites of thanksgiving to the Southern Dipper, arranging torches and bright lamps as in the Northern Dipper’s method. Now, the Northern Dipper’s rites include both supplication and requital, for it holds life and death in particular gravity—hence its methods are especially detailed. The Southern Dipper, however, is the office of life’s augmentation, governing blessings and longevity, and thus concerns itself solely with the entreaty of grace. Without talismans, one cannot summon its response; without incantations, one cannot unite with its numen. Therefore, this section again sets forth the ritual method, appending the Dipper’s lamps, banners, and talismans below.

**Talisman of the Heavenly Mansion’s Director of Destinies, Supreme General and True Lord Who Guards the Realm**
*Incantation:*
Director of Destinies, True Lord,
Preserve my long life.
Let no calamity assail me,
Let my nine orifices shine with light.
May you descend true *qi*,
And unite with this talisman.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman of the Heavenly Appearance’s Registrar of Records, Supreme Minister and True Lord Who Guards the Peaks**
*Incantation:*
Registrar of Records, True Lord,
Preserve my thousand years.
Let ten thousand *qi* shine with light,
Guard my true form.
May you descend true *qi*,
And preserve me in spontaneity.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman of the Heavenly Beam’s Prolonger of Life, True Lord Who Protects Destiny**
*Incantation:*
Protector of Destiny, True Lord,
Guard my *hun* and essence.
Sever the roots of death,
Restore my *qi* to its primal origin.
May you descend life-*qi*,
And unite with your servant in numinous union.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman of the Heavenly Uniformity’s Increaser of Years, True Lord Who Preserves Life**
*Incantation:*
Bestower of Life, True Lord,
Augment my years of longevity.
Let harmonious true *qi* flow,
Nurturing the spirit with refinement.
May you descend upright *qi*,
To preserve my life and truth.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman of the Heavenly Pivot’s Deliverer from Adversity, True Lord of Literary Florescence Who Refines the *Hun***
*Incantation:*
Refiner of the *Hun*, True Lord,
Cultivate and forge living beings.
Transform the yin corpse through refinement,
Transmute mortals into immortals.
May you descend life-*qi*,
And let my destiny soar in cycles.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

**Talisman of the Heavenly Mechanism’s Supervisor of Life, Grand Minister and True Lord of Great Principle**
*Incantation:*
True Lord of Great Principle,
Prolong life and deliver destiny.
Shield the body, preserve life,
Dispel misfortune and scatter calamity.
May you descend life-*qi*,
That I may pass through kalpas unscathed.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

For each, visualize the star’s radiance and grasp the corresponding hand seal:
*Midnight, Ox, Midday, Lake, Fire, Horse.*
Inscribe banners on yellow silk with cinnabar, and suspend them beneath each lamp’s position. Further, inscribe on yellow paper with cinnabar, then burn and scatter the talismans into each lamp’s bowl.

The Master said: When presenting offerings to the Southern Dipper, arrange six lamps and torches. At the time of the rite, further dispatch six talismans, inscribed on red paper with yellow ink, using the same hand seals as before:
1. Talisman of the Director of Destinies
2. Talisman of the Registrar of Records
3. Talisman of the Prolonger of Life (Talisman of the Protector of Destiny)
4. Talisman of the Preserver of Life
5. Talisman of the Refiner of the *Hun*
6. Talisman of the Grand Minister

**Talisman of the Six True Lords’ Vermilion Chariot and Jade Conveyance**
*Incantation:*
The heavens possess radiance,
The Southern True Lords’ jade brilliance.
Shed light to protect destiny,
Deliver from adversity and avert wrongdoing.
Today is most auspicious,
As we behold the numinous presence.
Descend with the lamps’ glow,
Dispelling darkness with splendor.
Augment my years of longevity,
Grant me the immortal’s term.
Release me from suffering,
Sever my Three Corpses.
May I attain long life spontaneously,
Chewing the mysterious fungus.
Swiftly descend in cloud-borne chariots,
To attend the imperial chariot.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!*

Visualize each star’s blazing, molten *qi*—neither purple nor white, neither gold nor jade, but its natural hue—descending into the lamps to seek numinous verification. If the adept wishes to entreat the recording of years, circumambulate the lamps three times, silently recite the incantation, and burn the talisman in requital. If the lamp’s flame grows by an inch, one has obtained the sign of long life.

**Talisman for Prolonging Life by Entreaty to the Lamps**
Circumambulate these six lamps, burn six talismans, and regard brightness as auspicious. If the flames grow long and red, one has received the proof of long life.

*Thus concludes Volume Twelve of the* Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method.
