**Compiled by:** Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty
**Thirty Scrolls**
**Source:** *Daoist Canon of the Zhengtong Era*, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category

**Scroll Thirteen of the** *Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
**Chapter Fifteen: Severing Pestilence and Cutting Off Epidemics**

The Master said: People born into this world recklessly muddy body and mind, deluded by desires and cravings, unable to circulate and nurture their *qi*. Thus, wind, cold, summerheat, and dampness injure them from without, while excess and exhaustion deplete them from within. This causes the four great elements of the body to scatter and *qi* to wane, weakening strength and wearying the spirit.

When essence and *qi* falter, primordial *qi* is no longer secure, and epidemics arise. Yet if one regulates daily life to avoid cold and heat, moderates diet to nourish the transient body, and severs lustful thoughts to secure primordial essence, then true *qi* will not scatter, blood and *qi* will circulate freely, and one will enter the Dao and commune with the real. How then could one suffer from malignant diseases or seek methods to subdue them?

Thus the *Medical Classic* states: *"If one does not fall ill with pestilence in spring, it is because one stored essence in winter."* This is the meaning.

Now, out of compassion, the Most High establishes methods of subjugation to save the people of the latter age, that they may avoid untimely death and be spared from violent demise, ascending to benevolence and longevity—this is the Most High’s fundamental heart of cherishing life.

The scriptures say: In times past, people were benevolent, righteous, and pure, free from malice, untouched by untimely death, and ghosts did not harm them wantonly. But in this latter age, the era is degenerate, human hearts are corrupted, the five emotions are in chaos, and doubts multiply. People act at will, distrusting proper teachings and embracing perverse conduct. They turn from truth to falsehood, abandon the Dao and benevolence, defy heaven and earth, slaughter living beings, are disloyal and unfilial, devoid of love and compassion. They harm lives and accumulate karmic adversaries, inviting calamities to spread, families to suffer epidemics, and bodies to endure toxic *qi*, bringing illness and death to all.

For this, the *qi* of the Six Heavens, the Lord of Northern Fengdu, the marshals of the ghost legions, the generals of the human realm, and the deities of the Five Peaks traverse the world, bearing the burden of their transgressions. They release toxic *qi* to slay the wicked.

Thus the Most High established methods of control. The *Laws of Lady Green* states: *"If one knows the names of the pestilence ghosts, they dare not cause harm. Call their names thrice, and the ghosts will perish of themselves."*

**Eastern Green Pestilence Ghost:** Liu Yuanda, essence of Wood, leading ten thousand ghosts to spread diseases of malign wind.
**Southern Red Pestilence Ghost:** Zhang Yuanbo, essence of Fire, leading ten thousand ghosts to spread diseases of heat toxin.
**Western White Pestilence Ghost:** Zhao Gongming, essence of Metal, leading ten thousand ghosts to spread diseases of black flux.
**Northern Black Pestilence Ghost:** Zhong Shiji, essence of Water, leading ten thousand ghosts to spread diseases of malignant toxin.
**Central Yellow Pestilence Ghost:** Shi Wenye, essence of Earth, leading ten thousand ghosts to spread malignant sores and swellings.

**Eastern Pestilence Ghost:** Jiu Da
**Southern Pestilence Ghost:** Shi Yan
**Western Pestilence Ghost:** Yao
**Northern Pestilence Ghost:** Tian Xia
**Central Pestilence Ghost:** Da Huangnu
**Sixth Pestilence Ghost:** Zhu Nü
**Seventh Pestilence Ghost:** Bo Ling

**Pestilence Ghosts’ Paternal Grandfather:** Liang Zhou
**Pestilence Ghosts’ Paternal Grandmother:** Jiao Cheng
**Pestilence Ghosts’ Father:** Yan Nian
**Pestilence Ghosts’ Mother:** Chu Zhong

The five directional pestilence ghosts, seven brothers in all, together with their grandparents and parents, total eleven forms. They fly and move, spreading toxins with the moon to harm the wicked. Yet the Most High, in cherishing life, has talismanic methods to control them, so they cannot cause harm.

**Pestilence Ghosts by Month:**
**First Month:** Wei
**Second Month:** Zhong (also called Xing)
**Third Month:** Liu
**Fourth Month:** Cun
**Fifth Month:** Lei (pronounced *qi*)
**Sixth Month:** Mou (also called □)
**Seventh Month:** Xing
**Eighth Month:** Huai
**Ninth Month:** Chen
**Tenth Month:** Bei
**Eleventh Month:** Ying
**Twelfth Month:** Jian

**Pestilence Ghosts by Day:**
**Zi Day:** Gen
**Chou Day:** Dang
**Yin Day:** Yi
**Mao Day:** Yi
**Chen Day:** E
**Si Day:** Ai
**Wu Day:** Wu
**Wei Day:** Nu Chang
**Shen Day:** Mu
**You Day:** Shi
**Xu Day:** Zhi
**Hai Day:** You

These pestilence ghosts preside over their respective months and days, following Liu Yuanda and the others to release toxins and cause harm. All people of the five phases who do not practice the Dao and its precepts, who are disloyal and unfilial, unbenevolent and unrighteous, will suffer their misfortunes. Yet those who practice the Dao and follow its teachings, knowing their names, will subdue them. Those who should depart will flee far away; those who remain will repel their evil factions. They will bind one another, refraining from harming the good. Call their names thrice, and they will hide in terror.

**Gu Toxin Ghosts:**
**First Gu Toxin Ghost:** Han Qu
**Second Gu Toxin Ghost:** Jiu
**Third Gu Toxin Ghost:** Li Jiu
**Fourth Gu Toxin Ghost:** Cheng Yan
**Fifth Gu Toxin Ghost:** Bu Shi
**Sixth Gu Toxin Ghost:** Wu Wu
**Seventh Gu Toxin Ghost:** Yuan Zhi
**Eighth Gu Toxin Ghost:** Shi Gan
**Ninth Gu Toxin Ghost:** Yu Yi

These nine ghosts spread evil and disorder across the world, acting alongside the pestilence ghost Da Huangnu to disseminate perverse toxins. All are controlled by talismans.

**Heavenly Master’s Pestilence-Expelling Talisman**
Inscribed in cinnabar on yellow silk, with incantations as hidden language. Dispatch the Heavenly Ding warriors to release the *qi* of the Three Luminaries and expel the *qi* of perverse spirits.

**Method for Expelling Pestilence with Cypress Tablets**
Use cypress tablets inscribed in cinnabar. The incantation reads:

*"Hark! Ghosts of the Six Jia and Six Yi, bearing afflictions—depart swiftly to the Six Bing and Six Ding! I know your names; flee a thousand leagues without delay. Linger but a moment, and I shall dispatch the Great Spirit, towering a thousand fathoms high, with five eyes blazing, wielding iron chains to seize your form. With mighty pincers, I shall tear out your tongue and devour your flesh. Once your form is destroyed, you shall languish in the dark abyss for ten thousand kalpas. Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the Lord Lao’s statutes!"*

The Master says: *"In years of plague and calamity, when ghosts and demons roam unchecked, those who seek deliverance must recite this divine incantation with utmost sincerity, thrice daily. They may then share a bed and meals with the afflicted, fearing no harm, and shall remain unscathed, their minds at peace. Call the ghost’s name thrice, and it shall perish of its own accord."*

The incantation reads:
*"I wear the Vermilion Bird upon my crown, tread the Dark Warrior beneath my feet. To my left, the Azure Dragon; to my right, the White Tiger. Before me, a cauldron of boiling oil; behind me, the Tiger’s Might and Heavenly Wrath. The celestial soldiers stand guard at my front and rear. Ghost of Huangnu, flee ten thousand leagues from me—or the Emperor shall sever your form. Swiftly, swiftly, as the statutes command!"*

Another incantation reads:
*"Hark! Pestilence ghosts of the Five Directions—I know your names and the seasons you spread your blight. My head bears the heavens, my feet tread the earth; my tiger’s roar shakes the mountains, my divine sword cleaves the Yangtze’s flow. Above, I cast the Heavenly Net; below, the Earthly Snare. I command a general named Zali, who feasts on yakshas and devours specters. Let the pestilence ghosts hear his name and flee a thousand leagues! Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the Lord Emperor’s statutes!"*

**Lord Lao’s Great Pestilence-Expelling Talisman**
Inscribed in cinnabar on yellow silk, then burned in a large censer. It may also be worn on the person. This great talisman records the sacred method by which the Perfected Master subdued ghosts and vanquished demons in Shu.

The incantation reads:
*"Celestial Talisman of the Most High, the Supreme Clarity, Lord Lao—commander of the Five Divisions of Ghost Kings. Liu Yuanda, Zhang Yuanbo, Zhao Gongming, Zhong Shiji, Shi Wenye, and the five *gu* spirits wielding a hundred toxins—along with Huangnu, Bojie, Zasu, and the ghosts of the Six Ding—slay the living and spread harm. They shall be cut down at the waist without mercy for past sins. Swiftly, as the mandate commands, let wind and fire obey!"*

**Swiftly, as the statutes and decrees command!**

**The Most High’s Talismans for Slaying Evil, Severing Pestilence, and Dispelling Epidemics**
Hold the three talismans in the Dipper Mudra and inscribe them with *qi* along the *gang* (celestial stem). Hang them in the central hall and at the doors of rooms to forever sever the afflictions of malevolent ghosts and pestilential epidemics.

**Two Additional Talismans**
**The Most High’s Merciful Talisman for Deliverance from Suffering, Ensuring Shared Rest Without Contagion**
Inscribe the talisman with the *qi* of the Three Lights, then swallow it with well water. Wear it by day, bind it in your topknot by night, and ingest the Three Lights Talisman according to the prescribed method.

**The Most High’s Talisman for Halting Contagion and Slaying Pestilence Ghosts**
Inscribe it with *qi* using the Dipper Mudra and the revolving *gang*, then swallow it with well-flower water to forever prevent contagious illness. If one ingests it at the year’s dawn, they shall remain free from all afflictions. This is the decree of the Most High’s Northern Emperor, the Pestilence-Quelling King—revere it.

Recite the *Tianpeng* incantation thirty-six times in practice.

The Master said: To subdue pestilential demons, first focus the eyes, visualize the five viscera each inhabited by its respective spirit, and knock the teeth together thirty-six times, followed by a single clack of the jaws. For those possessed by ghosts, if this method is applied thrice, their eyes will fester and they will die. Should a mortal practice this diligently, they shall attain the Dao of immortality. This incantation is the *Tianpeng* incantation; if recited carelessly, one will surely fall into evil destinies. Thus, superior practitioners ought to practice it diligently. The incantation contains the secrets of slaying ghosts—its words must not be spoken lightly. Upon reciting it ten thousand times, its merit shall be immeasurable.

**Fire-Bell and Flowing-Metal Incantation for Slaying Pestilence**
*"Divine spirit of the Most High, essence of the Flame Emperor.
Lightning flashes in radiant glory, illuminating the Three Clarities.
Fire flows for ten thousand *li*—ghosts cannot escape their forms.
With one descent of the sacred talisman, demonic spirits are reduced to ashes.
Generals of the Three and Five, officers and soldiers of the *Huoluo*.
They level heaven and strike earth, ceaselessly slaying ghosts.
Flying talismans and moving seals, their heads bear the Seven Stars.
Hurl fire to slay in advance, the demonic essences of the Six Heavens.
Pestilential ghosts and thieves are delivered to the divine *Ding*.
The Five Numinous True Elders are my original masters.
Unobstructed divine power—all spirits return in unity.
The Five Pestilences and Seven Afflictions—I can slay them all.
What ghost dares defy? In Fengdu, their forms are executed;
the Northern Dipper severs their corpses.
With one descent of the sacred talisman, ten thousand ghosts scatter in terror.
Swiftly, as the statutes and decrees of the Supreme Lord Emperor command!"*

**Spring Talisman for Warding Off Pestilence**
Four talismans, each corresponding to a direction and color, inscribed in cinnabar and hung in the central hall to repel the inauspicious *qi* of the four seasons and usher in auspiciousness.

**Summer Talisman for Warding Off Pestilence**
**Autumn Talisman for Warding Off Pestilence**
**Winter Talisman for Warding Off Pestilence**

**Talisman for Repelling Pestilence from the Eastern Neighbor** (left side for east)
**Talisman for Repelling Pestilence from the Western Neighbor** (right side for west)

**Talisman for Suppression and Posting**
Inscribe in cinnabar on yellow paper and post according to direction. Use the Northern Emperor’s Mudra, transform and ride the *gang*, point to the direction, and spray water—it shall be efficacious.

**The Unsurpassed Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Scroll Thirteen** *(conclusion)*

**The Unsurpassed Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method**
*Title:* The Unsurpassed Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.
*Source text:* Zhengtong Daoist Canon, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category.

---

**The Unsurpassed Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Scroll Fourteen**
**Chapter Sixteen: Wisdom-Light Illuminating the Obscure**

The Master said: When celestial perfection prevails, *yin* wanes and *yang* waxes—this is the way of immortals. For ordinary people, *yin* waxes and *yang* wanes—this is the way of ghosts. Thus, the scriptures say: ghosts lurk in obscurity, belonging to the *yin* kind. The multitude of the netherworld, the spirits of the departed, endure sorrow and bitterness, having lost their original luminosity and entered the nameless darkness. Therefore, the Most High established these rites, employing lamplight to convey *yang* *qi* and entrusting true *qi* to sacred talismans. Relying on the radiance of the Dharma torch, it disperses the blind redemption of the nether paths. In the eternal night of the Yellow Springs, all shall behold the light of *yang*. This is the Most High’s profound grace, a merciful absolution for the lower ghosts—how could one not revere it?

The Master said: In the primordial chaos before the beginning, heaven and earth were unformed, the sun and moon unborn—thus, the boundless expanse was devoid of light. When the One *qi* divided into Two, and the Two *qi* divided into Three, heaven and earth took their places, the sun and moon came into being, and light penetrated the obscure, giving rise to the myriad transformations. Therefore, at the inception of a ritual for delivering beings, one emulates the luminosity of heaven, earth, sun, and moon—using lamps to dispel darkness and *yang* to scatter *yin*. First, visualize the *qi* of one’s cinnabar field and sea of primordial *qi* glowing like a millet grain. Next, visualize the *qi* entering the heart, then ascending to the *Niwan* (mud-palace). Distribute the light of the sun, moon, and stars to universally illuminate the ten directions. Above heaven and below heaven, no obscurity remains—all is bathed in light. The spirits of the departed ride this luminosity, leaving the darkness behind.

**The Dharma Master’s Method for Dividing Lamps and Transforming the Three Luminaries Diagram**
**Moon Wheel Manifesting Auspicious Jade Talisman**
Use the Moon Sovereign’s Mudra, gather *qi*, and entrust it to the talisman. When dividing the lamps, ignite paper as a bright candle and visualize the process according to the method.

The incantation reads:
*"True water settles in mysterious clarity, the primordial *qi* just beginning to arise.
The white soul shines upon the diagram’s scene—Lady Nuanxiao is her name.
Flowing light pervades the obscure alleys; the Jade Hare bears the Silver Toad.
Radiant splendor of the two poles, interreflecting the distant Jade Towers.
Gathering *qi* to part the eternal gloom, divine light dances in *yang*’s flourish."*

**Sun Luminance Illuminating the Golden Talisman**
Use the Sun Sovereign’s Mudra, gather *qi*, and entrust it to the talisman. When dividing the lamps, ignite paper as a bright candle and visualize the process according to the method.

The incantation reads:
*"Golden Crow scatters crimson light, *yang* *qi* permeates the ten directions.
Great brilliance blazes in the central heaven; the Three Realms pay homage to the Primordial Emperor.
The Five Thearchs guide the *yang* essence; the vermilion radiance soars in the Flowery Chamber.
All *yin* has already dissipated; the true scene refines the primordial net.
Illuminating the Eternal Spring realm, it naturally connects to the Emperor’s land."*

**Star-Splendor Radiating the Luminous Treasure Talisman**
Use the Dipper Mudra.

The incantation reads:
*"Starlight is heaven’s embryo, weaving *qi* to unfold divine radiance.
The Dipper’s bowl turns the central heaven; the pivot mechanism revolves the Primordial Emperor.
Below, it shines upon the ten-directional realms—even the obscure night is filled with light.
The souls of the departed leave the dark night, riding the light to refine true *yang*."*

**Jade Capital’s Universal Light Dispelling Darkness Treasure Talisman**

**Incantation:**

*"The Primordial One *qi* gives rise to the Three Clarities.
The Three *qi* set the turning in motion; the Three Lights unfold brilliance.
The sunlight shines downward, scattering *yin* across the Three Realms.
The moonlight glows radiant, bringing spring to the long night.
The Dipper’s light descends, illuminating heaven and earth.
Above, it reaches the Summit of Existence—all heavens bow to its splendor.
Below, it shines through the Nine Ramparts, its light piercing the Yellow Springs.
At its center, it illumines the Earth Prison, dissolving karmic paths into clarity.
Beneath the Nine Heavens, every place is filled with light.
*Yin* is broken by *yang*; darkness is broken by light.
Heaven’s light descends—earth’s darkness vanishes.
Heaven’s light is born—earth’s *yin* perishes.
Merciful radiance shines forth, delivering boundless salvation."*

**The Nine Dark Hells’ Lamps**
The Master says: *"Draw upon the *qi* of the upper heavens to subdue the souls of the Nine Heavens. Thus, we borrow the talisman and infuse it with *qi*, riding the light downward into the Earth Prison—whereupon the imprisoned souls depart."*

Now, *yang* is an odd number: from one to three, from three to five, from five through seven, reaching nine—all are *yang* numbers.
First, arrange nine lamps in order before the Master. Invoke the *Nine Heavens’ True Yang Jade Light Dispelling Darkness Talisman* to the lamp’s location, then burn the talisman and proclaim the ritual.
Next, beginning in the east, light one lamp and recite the incantation, guiding its light to illuminate the Wind-Thunder Hell.
Before each hell’s lamp, inscribe the celestial realm of its corresponding direction—for the east, write *Infinite Heaven*—then cover it with the hell’s enclosure.
When closing the lamp, remove the enclosure and burn it with the talisman, whereupon the hell transforms into a celestial realm.
Proceed with the south in the same manner.
When all nine hells are completed, they are wholly transmuted into heaven.

**Nine Heavens’ True Yang Jade Light Dispelling Darkness Golden Talisman**
The Master says: *"This talisman is inscribed in cinnabar on yellow silk, traced with sunlight and moonlight. Burn it before lighting the lamps to invoke the wisdom-light, then break open the hells."*

**Incantation:**
*"The Three Lights’ true wisdom, their radiance merging in splendor.
The ten directions respond to their transformation, universally descending in majesty.
Fire-toxins dissolve the haze; the frigid pools grow bright.
The dark gates shine clear; the gloomy prisons gleam.
Great compassion descends; the exalted saints show mercy.
Imprisoned souls ascend, soaring to the celestial courts.
Swift as a command!"*

**Diagram of the Nine Hells’ Lamps**

**Talisman for the Merciful Sovereign Opening the Dark Prisons**
Use the *Jade Clarity Mudra*.
First, visualize the Merciful Sovereign of Grand Unity within the sun, emanating light. Then, bow in reverence, recite the *Sutra of Salvation* once, and draw the sun’s Merciful Sovereign into your mouth to empower the brush as you write nine talismans.
When breaking open the hells, cast one talisman into each direction, then proclaim the talisman’s decree.
The decree is a layered talisman found in the *Chapter on Salvation by Sound*.
Outside the circular image, within the halo of light, Grand Unity sits upon a lion, sprinkling water.
For each use, prepare a talisman on light yellow paper, eight inches long and five inches wide. Grind cinnabar facing the sun and inscribe it as before.
Cast one talisman per hell.
When casting, visualize yourself as the Merciful Sovereign, facing the dark prison. Guide the talisman’s light to shatter it, forgetting your own form—seeing only that you are the Heavenly Worthy.
Thus, with focused intent, the nine hells will resonate, and the ritual proclamations will be announced.

**Incantation for Salvation from the Wind-Thunder Hell of the East**
When breaking the hell, use the *Jade Clarity Mudra*, face east, and part the hair with the *Gui Mao* mudra. Visualize the blue *qi* within your body, riding the talisman’s light as you transform into the Heavenly Worthy, entering the dark prison to save the suffering souls. The other directions follow this pattern.

*"Blue *yang* generates *qi*, its light illuminating the Mystic Terrace.
The Primordial Worthy’s great compassion descends upon the Wind-Thunder Hell.
Flying spears scatter; tortures and interrogations cease.
The Most High swiftly pardons—souls ascend to Jade Clarity."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Fire-Haze Hell of the South**
Face south with the *Gui Wu* mudra.

*"Three *qi* of cinnabar blossoms illuminate the south.
The Fire-Haze Hell naturally cools.
Flying sweet dew and dharma rain flow with fragrance.
Spirit-souls are at ease, ascending to the land of blessings."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Vajra Hell of the West**
Face west with the *Gui You* mudra.

*"The Heavenly Worthy commands pardon, shining down upon the Vajra Hell.
Ghost-officials obey the decree; souls ride the light.
Dark prisons end their trials; tortures cease their bitterness.
Departing the hells, they stride toward the immortal realms."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Dark-Cold Hell of the North**
Face north with the *Gui Zi* mudra.

*"*Yang* radiance shines downward; the hells return to spring.
The Dark-Cold’s frigid night is wholly dispelled by light.
Bitterness scatters; punishments and crimes dissolve.
Riding this talisman’s light, they escape the dark gates."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Cauldron-Boiling Hell of the Northeast**
Face northeast with the *Gui Yin* mudra.

*"True light of jade brilliance opens the night’s cold glow.
Cauldron flames subside; scorching torments turn to ice.
Wisdom’s moisture soaks; divine winds extinguish the blaze.
Spirit-souls are at ease, riding the light in flight."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Bronze-Pillar Hell of the Southeast**
Face southeast with the *Gui Si* mudra.

*"The true light of jade commands; ghost-officials receive grace.
Bronze pillars collapse; the crooked pardon sinful souls.
Black records vanish; golden light delivers souls.
Jade radiance ascends—beholding the Merciful Sovereign."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Slaughter Hell of the Southwest**
Face southwest with the *Gui Shen* mudra.

*"The golden talisman descends with the celestial decree; the Most High proclaims mercy.
The Slaughter Hell’s knives and swords dissolve to dust.
Broken souls restore their nature; sins and karma are erased.
Riding the light from darkness, they escape the kalpic age."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Fire-Chariot Hell of the Northwest**
Face northwest with the *Gui Hai* mudra.

*"A hundred treasures’ auspicious splendor, within which dwells the Primordial Worthy.
Pouring sweet dew, washing away the flames’ affliction.
Fire-chariots halt their tracks; swords and halberds shatter their suffering.
Ghost-officials obey the pardon, drawing out the ghost-souls."*

**Incantation for Salvation from the Universal Torment Hell of the Center**
Face the center, burn the talisman, then use the *Jade Clarity Mudra* to conclude.

*"Mystic radiance arises naturally, pardoning the depths of the Yellow Springs.
Grace extends universally; sins and sufferings are absolved.
Ghost-officials depart; soul-spirits ascend as immortals."*

Visualize the three-colored cloud-*qi* atop your crown, with Grand Unity the Merciful Sovereign seated above, radiating a hundred treasures’ light to shine upon the Yellow Springs’ curves. In each hell, the Merciful Sovereign appears, emanating light to dispel darkness. Sinful souls ride the light upward, whereupon you prod them with your staff.

*Thus concludes the Fourteenth Scroll of the Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method.*

**Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method**

**Scripture Title:** *Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.
Source text: *Daoist Canon of the Zhengtong Era*, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category.

**Scroll Fifteen of the Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method**
**Chapter Seventeen: Seeking Sound to Deliver from Suffering**

The Master said: The Yellow Register delivers the living; the Azure Mystery rescues the suffering. Wisdom’s light dispels darkness; talismanic commands reach the hidden realms. They retrieve sunken, stagnant souls, raising them to swift joy. Such merit is truly not insignificant. Yet those who practice it—how could they regard it as easy to behold?

The altar must be solemnly arrayed, bells and chimes resonant. Though outwardly adorned with majestic ritual forms, inwardly it relies solely upon virtue and conduct. If one takes seals as life-essence, or now employs written summons for control, yet does not inwardly cultivate the self, not only will it be of no benefit—it may even lead astray.

The transmission of talismans for the hidden and nether realms has long prioritized deliverance from suffering and longevity. Thus, the talismans for deliverance from suffering are placed first.

**Explanation of the Original Deliverance-from-Suffering Talisman and the Longevity Talisman**

The Master said: This level talisman is fully recorded in the *Scripture of the Nine Nether Realms*, all conforming to the true. Later incorporated into the *Lingbao* methods, distinctions were forcibly imposed, establishing various grades, scattered forms, and hierarchies of nobility, each with its own gradations.

When heaven and earth divided, humanity was placed between them. Having attained human form, one encounters the gates of life and death, and the distinctions of noble and base—such is the natural order of the world. Yet how could heaven treat the people below with disparate degrees? There is only the One.

Thus, the *Scripture of the Mysterious Numinous* states: Though ranks differ in honor, the allotment of life is without distinction. If there is no distinction, how could talismanic forms differ? Yet their terminology varies, sowing confusion.

The Master continued: Within the treasure-pearl, the primordial script was simple, but later ages made it elaborate. Now, I establish the Deliverance-from-Suffering as a single category, placing these two talismans at the forefront. Future inheritors of the teaching should follow and practice this, comprehending its truth.

**First: True Deliverance-from-Suffering Talisman**
**Second: Transforming-Reed Dragon Talisman**
Use yellow paper, two feet and four inches in length, inscribed in cinnabar. Suspend it in the mouth of the reed dragon. Recite the *Jade Clarity* and *Azure Mystery qi* incantations nine times, then write the talisman.

**Incantation:**
The Dao is attuned to the heart; delusion relies on illusion to take form.
Sever delusion with illusion; transform the false into the true.
Bind reeds into a dragon, its brows and eyes distinct.
Bear my talismanic command, descend into the cold courts.
From this day forth, incinerate and transform, flying ceaselessly.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance.

**Additional Incantation:**
Compassionate light delivers from suffering; the Most High is merciful.
Human life is benighted; sins and sufferings lead astray.
Five sufferings, five burdens—karmic retribution is never lacking.
Today is a great celebration; celestial light descends.
Deliver from the realms of suffering; karmic debts dissolve.
Ascend my altar, undergo refinement, and be reborn.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance.

**Longevity Numinous Talisman**

**Golden Dragon Transformation Talisman**
Use yellow paper two feet and four inches in length, inscribed in cinnabar. Place it into the dragon’s mouth as before. Perform the Yuqing mudra, invoke the Dongyang qi, and recite the incantation nine times before inscribing the talisman.

**Incantation:**
The Dao is known through the heart; delusion takes form through illusion.
Sever delusion with illusion; transform the false into the true.
Shape the image into a dragon, transmuting into a golden dragon’s form.
All transformations arise from fire; all changes depend on the heart.
Transformation lies within me, refining and smelting the hidden yin.
The cinnabar heavens’ true fire burns away the Feng courts to ashes.
Refined by fire, it ascends naturally to the Vermilion Mound.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance.

**Additional Incantation:**
Crimson qi flows as fire, blazing upon the Vermilion Mound.
The three qi of the cinnabar heavens smelt and refine the Golden Court.
Attain longevity and deathlessness, return the bones to their original truth.
Within it dwells the Immortal Elder, clad in crimson robes and fiery skirts.
Han Jun enacts transformation; Sima gives birth to spirits.
Forging the po, molding the hun, refining yin with yang.
The corpse and po disperse, transforming into the true form.
Merge with the Three Clarities, unite with the Pure, and ascend.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and ordinance.

**Supreme Spontaneous Compassionate Sin-Reducing Talisman**
Perform the Yuqing mudra, bow twice toward the northeast, and draw the talisman while invoking the Great Crimson Qi. Before submitting any talismans, first present this talisman to reduce sins, then submit the Prison-Transferring Talisman.

**Supreme and Spontaneous, compassionate in reducing sins.**
The jade talisman is proclaimed below to the Northern Yin of the Earth Prison, the Wuji World.
To Dengdu, the Great Emperor, and the Six Heavenly Ghost Kings:
Wherever this talismanic command arrives, the dark night is illuminated.
Obey the Dao’s decree, and notify the Three Officials, Nine Bureaus, One Hundred Twenty Offices, Thirty-Six Prisons, Nine Dark Hells, Twenty-Four Prisons, the Great and Small Iron Enclosure Hells, the Avīci Hell, the officials of the Underworld, and the spirits of the Earth Prison.
By the grace of this talismanic command, through the compassion of the Most High, reduce and erase the sins and transgressions of the departed soul of so-and-so in life, and the grievances after death.
By this talismanic command, diminish and cut away sins and offenses, release from Feng punishment, and reconcile transgressions.
By the merit of this sin-reducing talismanic command, do not delay.
All as proclaimed.
Proclaimed on an auspicious day, month, and year of the Tai Sui.

**Incantation:**
Primordial compassionate light coalesces into Brahma qi.
Shining upon the hidden darkness, it reduces and removes sins and offenses.
Proclaimed from the golden mouth, no record remains in the Black Register.
The divine treasure’s merciful light is revered by a thousand spirits.
Swiftly obey and execute; ghostly officials must not delay.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the Statutes and Ordinances for Deliverance.

**Qingxuan Emperor’s Qi-Absorbing and Scripture-Holding Mudra**
The adept enters the chamber, arranges their robes, and sits upright. Light incense toward the stove, free the mind of all distractions, and abide in undisturbed singularity.
Visualize the qi from one’s own liver emerging as blue-green mist.
The blue-green clouds pass through the ears and nose, gradually increasing until they fill the entire chamber, extending outward so that blue-green clouds are seen everywhere.
Within the blue-green clouds, behold the Qingxuan Emperor seated upon a lion throne, holding a willow branch and a lapis lazuli vessel.
To his left and right stand two perfected beings and eighty-one spirit officials in attendance.
See only the August One within golden light, piercing the blue-green clouds and pervading the ten directions.
The adept petitions for the wisdom-light sweet dew.
After a long while, the August One bestows the sweet dew upon the perfected beings to drink, and the adept’s five viscera feel cool and refreshed.
From the crown of the August One’s head, golden light descends upon the adept’s fontanel, illuminating their body. The adept senses their entire being suffused with golden light, entering the mouth like honey.
Next, silently recite the *Sutra of Salvation from Suffering* once, then gather the golden light and clouds, allowing them to enter through the subtle gate.
Swallow the saliva nine times, bow nine times, and retreat.
Perform this nine times, and what is practiced will be efficacious, what is delivered will be saved, and extraordinary proofs will manifest.
Keep this secret.

The *Nine Yang Perfected Salvation-from-Suffering Jade Talisman*
Jade Clarity Incantation: From the hours of *hai* and *zi* to *yin*, inscribe the talisman with great crimson *qi*.

Once this talisman is proclaimed, then proclaim the *Cessation-of-Suffering Talisman*.
When the *Nine Yang Perfected Salvation-from-Suffering Jade Talisman* is proclaimed, its radiance shines upon the Northern Yin’s Boundless Realm, the Fengdu August Emperor, the Six Heavenly Demon Kings, the Thirty-Six Hells, the Twenty-Four Hells, the great and small Iron Enclosures, and the hells of Intermittent and Uninterrupted Torment. Where the talisman’s light reaches, the dark prisons gleam.
By the grace of the Most High’s decree, swiftly pardon without delay. Remove and deliver the deceased, so-and-so, their form and soul, along with all the suffering shades of the netherworld. Upon beholding this light, may they ascend by this deliverance.
The merit of the talisman’s pardon must not be obstructed.
As proclaimed, so let it be.

Proclaimed on an auspicious day, month, and year of the Great Year, at a propitious hour.

**Incantation:**
The Nine Clarities’ talismanic command descends to illumine the deepest yin.
Dark dungeons and black prisons all behold the light.
Ox-Head shows compassion, ghostly fires grow clear and cool.
Remove and deliver the sinful shades—they must not linger long.
Ghostly emperors obey the command, demon kings reverently comply.
As proclaimed, so let it be.

*The Purple Tenuity Upper Palace Deliverance Talisman for Cessation of Suffering in the Lower Realm*
When the *Purple Tenuity Upper Palace Deliverance Talisman for Cessation of Suffering in the Lower Realm* is proclaimed, its radiance shines upon the Northern Yin’s Boundless Realm, the Fengdu August Emperor, and the Six Heavenly Demon Kings. Where the talisman’s light reaches, the darkest nights brighten. All receive the talismanic command, which is universally proclaimed to the Three Offices and Nine Bureaus, the One Hundred Twenty Courts, the Thirty-Six Hells, the Nine Nether Hells, the Twenty-Four Hells, the great and small Iron Enclosures, and the hells of Intermittent and Uninterrupted Torment, along with their wardens and officials. Each shall act in accordance with the talismanic command: cease suffering, halt punishments, and deliver the soul of the deceased, so-and-so, along with all the suffering shades of the netherworld. May the winds and thunder grow still, the karma-fires clear. May the icy waters warm, and all punishments be universally lifted.
Sever with compassion, and let swords transform into forests of *jian* trees.

The bronze pillars shatter and collapse, the vajra walls crumble and topple. Cauldrons of boiling liquid become tranquil pools, and the wheels of searing flames cease their turning. No suffering is endured, and evil roots are extinguished. By the merit of this Purple Tenuity talismanic command, none may delay or detain. Let it be proclaimed as decreed, transmitted swiftly as wind and fire.

Proclaimed on an auspicious day, month, and year of the Great Year, at a propitious hour.

**Incantation:**
The Jade Steps petition mercy,
the precious talisman penetrates the hidden.
Pardons descend to the nether courts,
rescuing the suffering and halting imprisonment.
Shackles and restraints fall away,
tortures and trials bring no sorrow.
By the authority of the talismanic pardon,
depart from the dark and hidden.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the Celestial Emperor’s decree for the salvation of the living!*

Jade Clarity mudra, Heavenly Gate *qi*, written in vermilion.

**The Master says:** These are the Three Talismans—of Sin-Reduction, Prison-Transfer, and Suffering-Cessation—granted by the Most High’s merciful pardon. In all ritual fasts and supplications, these three talismans must first be proclaimed before the Talisman of Salvation from Suffering.

**The Method of Salvation from Suffering in the Nine Nether Hells**
**The Master says:** Heaven’s halls are all within me; hell is not apart from the mind. If one lives in the world, and all actions accord with principle, then at death, how could there be karmic debt? Without karmic debt, there is no sin. Without sin, how can there be hell?

Yet when the minds of worldly people grow deluded, the Six Dusts defile all. They slander the sages and transcendents, betray their lords and fathers, kill living beings, steal, owe lives, and squander wealth. A lifetime of deceit, treachery, and unbridled vice—after death, their souls are bound for hell. It is like a foolish person, wearied in mind and spirit: by day, their spirit wanders; by night, their soul takes flight. As they act, so do evil visions manifest. Only upon waking do they realize it was but a dream. Hell is no different from such delusion.

All the causes sown in life, and the sufferings endured after death—hell arises from sin, and sin originates in the mind. If the mind’s dharmas are empty, how can sin exist? Yet hell, though unreal, is hard to refute in form; the mind’s dharmas, though formless, are hard to grasp in appearance. To stabilize the mind, first sever delusion. Once delusion is cut, sin vanishes without form, and hell is shattered.

For heaven is yang and thus bright; earth is yin and thus dark. Darkness brings suffering, suffering brings confinement—this is hell. To shatter hell, first mobilize the light of heaven. Borrow the talisman to convey *qi*, and borrow *qi* to spread light. With brightness shatter darkness, with yang overcome yin, with truth dispel delusion—this is called shattering hell.

Yet the superior adept awakens without doubt, while the inferior adept cannot yet comprehend. The Dao’s mystery is unfathomable; the mind’s dharmas are inexhaustible.

The profound and wondrous principles need not be expounded at length.

**Method for Shattering Hell**
The Master said: The method for shattering hell involves striking the prison gates with a ritual staff. The use of such a staff pertains to the Three Caverns Masters. There are those who wield swords to shatter hell—these are the Orthodox Unity Masters. In recent times, some have taken up axes to break open hell, citing the unorthodox claim of "using iron axes to cleave all hells." Later generations, unaware of the origins and traditions, mistakenly attribute the ritual staff to the Numinous Treasure Masters, while the Heavenly Master’s lineage is said to employ axes. These are all vulgar interpretations, failing to grasp the true essence and confounding the correct Dao. In our tradition, only those who have received the Central Alliance Great Cavern Register may use the ritual staff; others hold the Alliance威 Register. Swords and wooden axes are most disruptive to the Dao. When ascending the altar, such acts differ little from theatrical performance. They profane the sacred and true, and their transgression is grave. Thus, the practice of wielding axes is expressly abolished.

**True Talisman of the Three Qi and Nine Yang Jade Light to Shatter Hell**
With the Jade Clarity mudra, inscribe the *qi* of the Three Heavens, Nine Yang, and Three Lights. The True Talisman of the Void-Origin Three *Qi* and Nine Yang Jade Light to Shatter Hell is proclaimed below to the Underworld’s Curved Springs and the Northern Capital of Luo Deng:

"May the yang light penetrate and illuminate, opening the iron prisons. May the gloom of the netherworld disperse, the blades and halberds shatter. May the flames of the fire pools subside, the karmic realms know no wind. May the night gates and dark palaces all transform into heaven. May the departed souls emerge, bowing before the golden countenance. As this decree is issued, let it be swiftly conveyed by wind and fire."

Proclaimed on an auspicious day, month, and year of the Great Year.

**Method for Inscribing Talismans**
By the decree of the Three Great Emperors of Jade Clarity, Highest Clarity, and Grand Clarity, absolve and deliver the ten directions. May the Numinous Treasure Savior from Suffering Heavenly Worthy, the Vermilion Numinosity Emperor, the Vermilion Numinosity Lord, the Southern Culmen Longevity Great Emperor, and the Nine Heavens Life-Monitoring Great Spirits deliver the soul of the departed, so-and-so.

Upon reaching the character "decree," visualize the golden light of the Three Treasures of the Three Heavens.

**Incantation:**
"The Jade Emperor decrees, receiving the mandate of Jade Clarity. Absolve the sins of the ten directions; let fragrant incense fill the court.
*Oṃ hūṃ halu svāhā*, swiftly as the decree commands."

**Concealed Transmission of the Duplicate Talisman**
Inscribe one talisman for each hell, performing the rites in advance, then use the duplicate talisman as verification. On yang days, add one stroke.

When summoning souls from the underworld, this talisman may also be reprinted on the directional envelope, and the earthly officials will promptly comply. When shattering hell, this talisman may be inscribed on yellow paper and placed in each direction as a token of its use. This is the talisman of the Six Jia yin-yang spirits, which may also be overlaid on the duplicate talisman.

**Method for Inscribing the Savior from Suffering Talisman and the Like**
The Master said: Before inscribing talismans, first purify the mind, restraining and sealing all worldly distractions. Face east in the cross-legged posture, visualizing the head as a circular light divided into blue, white, and yellow hues, with the Great One Compassionate Venerable seated upon a lion within the light. Then, within the radiance of a hundred treasures, emit a hundredfold brilliance, illuminating the ten directions. In each beam of light, behold the compassionate visage of the Great One Heavenly Worthy. Next, visualize the body as Mount Kunlun, drawing the compassionate light of the Great One to shine upon the Underworld’s Curved Springs, where every hell is bathed in light. Withdraw the *qi* of the Azure Mystery to infuse the brush and inscribe the talisman.

**Method for Proclaiming the Savior from Suffering Talisman and the Like**
The Master said: When reciting the proclamation, visualize the body as the Great One Savior from Suffering Heavenly Worthy. Then, from the crown of the head, emanate the Great One Savior from Suffering Heavenly Worthy ascending through the wondrous gate. From the eastern realm, the Great One Savior from Suffering Heavenly Worthy arrives upon a lion throne, merging with the Heavenly Worthy emanated from the crown. Then, unite with the Heavenly Worthy transformed from the body. At this moment, the three bodies become one. Open the eyes, seated within white light, the self now the form of the Great One.

Draw the nine *qi* of the east to irrigate the liver, transforming the hall into a dragon that wields the talisman to summon souls.

**Incantation:**
"Nine *qi* surge forth, irrigating my liver meridian. Ten thousand golden rays transform into nine dragons.
Pierce the dark and break the gloom, descending twice into the Northern Feng.
May sinful souls be free, roaming the vast heavens.
Swiftly as the Dharma commands."

Next, visualize the liver *qi* transforming into a dragon, emerging from the left ear, then dispatch the talismanic dragon.

**Method for Inscribing the Longevity Talisman**
The Master said: When inscribing the Longevity Talisman, proceed as with the Savior from Suffering Talisman—calm the mind, free from distractions. Then, visualize the head as the blazing sun, within which the Great Lord of Longevity wears a hibiscus crown, seated amidst crimson clouds, radiating great light. Next, visualize the body as Kunlun, the heart as the Fire Palace. Draw *qi* to infuse the brush and inscribe the talisman.

**Method for Proclaiming the Longevity Talisman**
The Master said: When proclaiming the talisman, visualize the body as the jade form of the Great Lord of Longevity. Then, from the crown of the head, emanate the Emperor of Longevity ascending through the wondrous gate. From within the cinnabar fire light, the Emperor of Longevity rides a three-*qi* fire dragon, merging with the form emanated from the crown. Then, unite with the body. At this moment, the three bodies become one. Open the eyes, standing within fire light, the self now the Great Lord of Longevity.

Draw the three *qi* of the southern heavens into the liver, transforming into a golden dragon that emerges from the left ear.

**Incantation:**
"*Qi* of the Cinnabar Heaven, radiant jade light.
Irrigate my spirit palace; four golden dragons manifest.
Bearing the talisman and token, ascend to Southern Prosperity.
Refine the yin haze, transform and circulate pure yang.
Swiftly as the Dharma commands."

Next, visualize the liver *qi* transforming into a golden dragon, emerging from the left ear. Then, with clear vision, dispatch the golden dragon.

**The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Scroll Fifteen, Concludes**

**The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method**
Title: *The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.

**Source Text:** *Zhengtong Daoist Canon*, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category.

**The Supreme Mystery and Primordial Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method, Scroll Sixteen**
**Chapter Eighteen: Salvation of the Netherworld**

The Master said: To deliver the netherworld is to awaken the illusory through the real.
All beings, while alive, stray from the true; in death, they lose it entirely. Once the One True [nature] is lost, delusive thoughts arise, manifesting as suffering and retribution. The sagely masters established teachings for no other purpose than to awaken the illusory through the real.
When the human heart strays from its true origin and enters the dark realm, even a thousand sages find it difficult to intervene. Only by deploying the One True to shatter the One Delusion can benighted souls attain purity, clearly escape their suffering, and be freed from entanglements—this is the original intent of the Most High’s compassionate teachings.
If practitioners fail to grasp this principle, clinging instead to mere documents and summonses as their practice, or upholding ritual decorum as merit, chanting through the night and exhausting themselves by day, they will ultimately bring no benefit to the deceased.
Thus, this chapter on salvation is established, that one may devote oneself wholly to the netherworld and not be distracted by external affairs.
When the mind’s realm becomes clear and luminous, and the nature of heaven shines brightly, beyond this truth there is no other teaching.
To liberate those sunk in darkness from the realms of suffering—such merit is immeasurable.

The Master said: The Six *Jia* refer to *Jiazi*, *Jiayin*, *Jiachen*, *Jiawu*, *Jiashen*, and *Jiaxu*. *Jia* is the generative *qi* of the East, the Great Benevolence of life.
Thus, the South refines with fire, the West hardens with metal, the North obstructs with water, and the four intermediate directions are not aligned with the true *qi*. Without the deities of the Six *Jia* arrayed in the eight directions, the ethereal and corporeal souls would not perceive life.
The true [essence] of life is difficult to reach the altar; therefore, in this great teaching, the Six *Jia* messengers are first dispatched to guide the way.

**Six Jia Opening Talisman**
This talisman, when proclaimed, shall illuminate the nine springs’ dark paths and the gloom of ghostly realms.
The Three Lights dispel obscurity; the Six *Jia* penetrate the yin.
Ghostly souls receive amnesty and behold the light.
Spirit officials shall not conceal; the Golden Horse Post transmits.
As this decree commands, the Wind-Fire Post conveys.
Proclaimed on an auspicious day, month, and year of the *Tai Sui*.

The Master said: The Six *Jia* Opening Talisman is the benevolent pledge that opens the dark paths. It must be proclaimed before summoning and gathering [the souls]. It is written in cinnabar on yellow paper, sealed at the corners, and dispatched.

The Master said: Alas! The people of the world, benighted and unaware, do not awaken in life.
Their hearts traverse perilous paths; in death, they enter the netherway. Naturally obstructed, without the Most High’s compassionate light, they cannot reach the altar. Only with this talisman will the dark paths brighten, the nether roads become smooth, and the departed souls know no peril.

**True Talisman of the Vermilion Radiance and Three Lights Opening the Nether Path**
This talisman, when proclaimed, commands the mountain, water, and celestial boundary deities along the paths of Mount Tai to swiftly open the nether roads, illuminate the dark journey, and guide the departed soul of so-and-so to follow the talisman’s light and swiftly reach the altar.
Let no obstruction or hindrance arise; may the soul’s consciousness be at peace.
Those who violate this decree shall be punished without delay.

As the decree is proclaimed, let it be transmitted by wind and fire couriers. On an auspicious day and hour of the year, month, and day under the reign of the Great Year Star, the decree is issued.

The Master declares: This is the method of the *Talisman Command for Opening the Nether Path*. Write it in vermilion on blue paper, fold the corners, seal with an imprint, and place it upon the altar before summoning the soul. When the Master guides the departed soul, with this talisman, the dark paths shall be smoothly traversed without obstruction.

**Method of Transformation**
For opening the nether path, first circulate one’s own Three Lights to merge with the Three Lights of Heaven, naturally illuminating the path so that the nether roads shine brightly, free from stagnation or hindrance. One will then perceive the soul’s consciousness abiding within this radiance, seeing no other hues.

Next, visualize the Most High Compassionate Venerable One holding a willow branch of empty azure, sprinkling the nether realm with its dew. In silent contemplation, recite the incantation:
*"The Three Lights gleam bright,
The Nine Nether realms lie deep.
Night’s haze disperses, dawn’s clarity arises,
Beholding the Compassionate Venerable’s form,
Sweet dew flows cool.
Let the soul’s consciousness return,
Smoothly traverse the dark journey.
Hearing the sutras and the Dharma,
Roam freely in the Upper Clarity."*

After the incantation, draw the talisman while guiding the *qi*.

**Method of Ablution**
The Master declares: Worldly toil and defilement are why the minds of mortals remain uncleansed. Not only is the mind tainted—all six senses bear dust, the six dusts bear consciousness, and the six consciousnesses bear filth. Thus, in death, one sinks even deeper, as if mired in mud, unable to purify oneself.

This ablution does not merely wash away conscious defilement. For the dark soul, burdened by sin, ignorance, and delusion, is like a body caked in grime. Therefore, with the pure and compassionate Dharma-water, each drop sprinkled and each touch cleansed, the nape and heart become clear, the *po* soul is restored, sins dissolve, and filth vanishes—this is what is meant by ablution.

**Talisman of the Immortal’s Corpse-Cleansing**
Incantation:
*"The Flower Pool nourishes and bathes,
Form and soul become one in purity.
The six dusts are without stain,
Karmic grime is wholly clarified.
The Three Fields glow full,
The Nine Orifices open bright.
Washed and irrigated, the root of life,
The dead soul returns to infancy.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the law!"*

**Jade Talisman of the Numinous Source’s Irrigation**
Incantation:
*"Fragrant clouds congeal as dew,
Dripping and sprinkling, cool and pure.
The celestial source’s dark waves
Moisten and irrigate the nether realms.
Corpse-filth is stilled,
Karmic dust instantly clears.
Refine all delusions,
Scour away ignorance.
The Three Hun return to truth,
Withered and decayed regain form.
Entering and exiting the void,
Coming and going in profound darkness.
No stain of sin or filth,
Ten thousand kalpas’ dust cleansed.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the law!"*

**Talisman for Scouring Worldly Toil**
Incantation:
*"Heaven’s filth becomes clouds,
The Three Lights sweep them clean.
Human filth of the six dusts,
Dharma-words scour the passions.
Earth’s filth of corpse-impurity,
Dharma-water clarifies all.
Human filth does not arise,
Corpse-filth is pacified.
Earth’s filth is dispelled,
All immortals unite as one.
The Three Qi intermingle,
Merging with the Dao in truth.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the law!"*

**Method of the Celestial Physician’s Whole-Form Restoration**
The Master declares: The ghostly consciousness lacks form, scattered and ungathered, like *qi* dwelling in the wind, without fixed shape. Yet its deluded thoughts persist, and the pains of illness or injury suffered in life continue to afflict it in death. Without the method of whole-form restoration, the soul’s form remains fragmented, unable to coalesce. Thus, those who die of illness have their souls worn away and cannot be made whole. Those who die from harm have their souls damaged and cannot be restored. Those who die by the blade have their souls dispersed and cannot be reunited. Therefore, the Most High, in compassion, established the *Method of the Celestial Physician’s Whole-Form Restoration*.

**Talisman of the Three Sections and Eight Sceneries Communicating with the True**
**True Talisman of the Celestial Physician’s Original Qi for Healing**
Incantation:
*"Heaven’s *qi* clarifies,
Earth’s sceneries open bright.
The Nine Treasures arrayed,
The Three Passes flourish.
The yin corpse returns to substance,
True *qi* remains ever pure.
Dense yin reverts to yang,
Softness returns to hardness.
Shatter the Six Caverns,
Dispel the yin’s stagnation.
The true scene guards within,
The *po* corpse regains form.
The Nine Elders’ ancestral *qi*,
Transmutes to immortal and becomes human.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the law!"*

**Method of the Life-Monitoring Purification**

The Master said: The karmic debts of the Blood Lake arise fundamentally from women. When desires burn fiercely and karmic bonds run deep, they congeal into retributive encounters. Yet if the foul and bloody impurities remain unsettled, the departed soul does not forget its attachments from the former life, and so its spectral spirit continues to suffer pain. Whether mother and child remain unsevered or the blood corpse is not yet purified, without the power of the method, how can they ascend and transcend? Therefore, this method is specially prepared to rescue those who perish in childbirth.

**Talisman for Dispelling the Impurities of the Blood Lake**
Incantation:
*"Great Brahma of the Nine Heavens,
Flying Mystery of the Three Caverns.
Unbind your fetal knots,
Open and clear the womb’s origin.
All karmic ties are severed,
The roots of death and grievances dissolved.
The Blood Lake is purified,
The prison wardens hold no dominion.
The Primordial Lady regains form,
The Celestial Overseer and Life-Monitor attend.
The Eight Sceneries are complete,
The ten-month gestation is fulfilled.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the Most High’s law!"*

**Talisman for Restoring Form and Severing the Fetal Bond**
Incantation:
*"Nine Elders of the Immortal Capital,
Jade Light coalesces into truth.
Fetal knots unravel of themselves,
The dead soul returns as an infant.
Great Spirit of the Life-Monitor,
Divine Lord of Parted Birth.
Descend with the talisman’s *qi*,
Sever the roots of death.
Dissolve the stains of sin,
Separate mother and child in form.
Wash away the foul and bloody,
Come to behold the Jade Court.
Receive the talisman and undergo refinement,
Transcend to the Vermilion Mound.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the law!"*

**Talisman of the Transmigration Banner**
Using the solar mudra, draw in the sun’s *qi*, and inscribe it according to the method. When raising the banner, circulate one’s own solar essence upon it, recite the Solar Lord’s incantation, and lift it aloft, visualizing the radiant sun blazing in the heavens, its light penetrating the depths of the Yellow Springs.

**Talisman of the Returning Yellow Banner**
Using the lunar mudra, draw in the moon’s *qi*, and inscribe it according to the method. When raising the banner, circulate one’s own lunar essence upon the banner, invoke the Lunar Lord’s incantation, and lift it aloft, visualizing the moon’s light filling the heavens, illuminating the darkest nights.

The Master said: The Transmigration Banner is made of crimson silk to symbolize the sun. The Returning Yellow Banner for Liberation is made of yellow silk to symbolize the moon. Each is twelve feet in length.

**Talisman for Universal Offerings to the Three Luminaries of the Celestial Kitchen**
Incantation:

Within the Three Realms and Six Paths,
All beings are ever hungry with delusive thoughts.
The Three Luminaries gather numinous essence,
And the dharma-food bestows sweetness and richness.
Above, it reaches the myriad gods of heaven;
Below, it extends to the Iron Hell of Mud.
A single offering nourishes all,
Joyfully attaining the subtle and serene.

*Concluding* **Scroll Sixteen of the Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Rites**
*Beginning* **Scroll Seventeen of the Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Rites**

**Chapter Nineteen: The Divine Tiger’s Pursuit and Summoning**

The Master said: The Dipper governs the souls and spirits of the world, hence its profound and hidden mysteries serve as the foundation for pursuit and summoning. Yet scholars, though familiar with its forms and frequent in its practice, seldom witness its efficacy—often reducing it to mere paperwork. Therefore, in this flourishing age of the Great Teaching, a dedicated chapter on pursuit and summoning is established, ensuring that responses to talismanic invocation are swift as echoes and shadows—not merely for ornamental display.

The talismanic script of the Divine Tiger’s Jade Tablet is widely known and thus not reproduced here. Instead, this text records the secret methods, for their subtlety transcends worldly understanding.

The Master said: Should one ask what the Divine Tiger’s rite entails?
The Master answered: The sages employ the Divine Tiger for summoning because the *yin* direction is the Ghost Gate, and its guardian is the tiger. The act of summoning from this direction is thus profoundly meaningful. Today’s lineage masters appoint altar officials to oversee the Tiger Bureau—this is the principle.

The Master said: In the art of summoning, without knowledge of the inner secrets of the Dark Mystery, the netherworld remains obscured, the Three Realms indistinct, and ghosts reluctant to appear, while the courts of the underworld delay compliance. Mastery of this method differs vastly from the practices commonly seen today.

**Register of the Divine Tiger’s Dark Mystery Inner Bureau Officials and Generals**

The Master said: The registers of daily altar attendants pertain to routine affairs. The officials of the Dark Mystery Inner Bureau, however, constitute a separate office, not bound to daily duties. Thus, their names are appended to this chapter on pursuit and summoning.

Divine Tiger’s Inverted Life Dark Bureau Jade Maiden: Jiang Renkui
Divine Tiger’s Purple Origin Lady, Dark Mystery Pursuit and Summoning Inner Bureau Jade Maiden: Wei Ziran
Dark Mystery Pursuit and Summoning Inner Bureau Spirit Officer: Cui Hao
Divine Tiger’s Left Male Jade Ministry Chief Scribe: He [ ]
Divine Tiger’s Right Female Martial Phoenix Chief Scribe: Qiao [ ]
Divine Tiger’s Inner Bureau Pursuit-Soul Register-Keeper Spirit Officer: Li Youjun
Dark Mystery Inner Bureau Heavenly Path Pursuit-Soul Envoy: Gao Long
Dark Mystery Inner Bureau Human Path Pursuit-Soul Envoy: Ma Zheng
Dark Mystery Inner Bureau Spirit Path Pursuit-Soul Envoy: Xue Yan

By imperial decree, descend from the Mystic Capital.

And receive the celestial talisman.
Swiftly execute the order,
And drive forth in pursuit of the soul.
I now summon you—
Hasten from the hidden paths!
*Oṃ hūṃ hūṃ*, come swiftly!

Write with black ink on black paper, inscribe the names in vermilion, and hold the Dipper Mudra while writing. Before any summoning, first use this talisman to call forth the generals, then issue the official document.

**Divine Tiger’s Dark and Hidden Inner Bureau Pursuit-Soul Bureau**
The right-hand ash altar is the Divine Tiger’s Prison.
This altar is for inner, secret use.

**Divine Verification Method**:
Use two *dou* and four *sheng* of slaked lime, arranged according to the prescribed pattern. Next, during the day, apply the talisman, then summon the soul at the Ghost Gate. Plant the soul banner in the center, and arrange the talismans to its left and right.

**Pursuit-Soul Incantation**
With the Dipper Mudra, recite nine times, and draw nine breaths of *qi* from the northeast to spread across the altar. Next, nine breaths from the east, three from the south, seven from the west, five from the north, and one from the center—all to be dispersed upon the altar. After burning the talismans, when a tinkling wind stirs within the bureau, the soul has arrived.

The essence of Heaven and Earth,
The gathering of yin and yang spirits.
With numinous *qi*, bind your form and soul—
Scattered, yet reunited; dim, yet bright.
From nothingness, signs emerge; from emptiness, truth appears.
Swiftly return to the numinous banner, merge with the radiant truth!
The Purple Origin’s talisman and summons descend to the Yellow Springs,
The Great One’s pursuit-soul command arrives in haste!
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the Dark and Hidden Inner Bureau’s Pursuit-Soul Statutes!

The Great One, by command, the Northern Dipper’s Divine Tiger—
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the Great One’s Soul-Summoning Statutes!

Use purple silk, two *chi* and six *cun* in length, one *chi* and two *cun* in height, inscribed in yellow, and enclose it in a square box as prescribed.

On an auspicious day, month, and year of the Great Year, at the appointed hour, proclaim below.
[Your] dharma rank and surname [are recorded here]. By imperial edict, [I] carry out the command.
The Three Heavens’ Great Sage, Celestial Master of the Great Dharma of All Heaven.

Write in vermilion on yellow paper, seal the corners as a document, and dispatch it alongside the golden document.

This altar, by order of the Great One’s Purple Origin Pursuit-Soul Golden Document, summons the deceased [Name], [their] years of life and death, and their true soul and spirit to appear before the bureau, receive deliverance, and be reborn. The pursuit and summoning must be executed as follows:

By imperial decree, command the Earth Bureau to seize the form and soul.

[Your] dharma rank and surname [seal].

The true talisman shines with jade light,
The Earth Prison opens its hidden yin.
The Seven Stars follow the *qi* of life,
The Three Luminaries scatter golden truth.
Soul, do not be startled or harmed;
Spirit, do not sink into perdition.

Refine your form and return to the Jade Flower.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by the statutes!

**Banner-Attaching Method**
The master says: When attaching the banner, first visualize the Divine Tiger’s hidden name, and the officials will arrive. Once the officials arrive, the soul may be drawn onto the banner. Visualize these two names emerging from the heart and kidneys, and the officials will come. Then attach the banner.

*(Secret names:)* □□□□□□□□
Hold the breath seven times, visualize the transmission of the river’s flow. Once the deceased’s soul arrives, it will manifest.

The master says: This bureau ensures full manifestation—seeing the brows and eyes as in life. Thus, it is especially secret and wondrous.

*(Secret names:)* □□□□□□□□□□□□□□
These fourteen characters are most secret. Hold the breath and recite twenty-one times, perform the Dipper Mudra, and spray water three times—then the soul will appear.

The radiance of the terrace arises here,
The hidden essence restores its form.

**Life-Command Mudra.**

The master says: This secret has not been transmitted for a thousand years. In former times, when Emperor Wu of Han’s Lady Li passed away, Master Shaojun performed this method to manifest the lady as in life, enabling her to speak with the emperor.

The method employs seven panels of raw silk, inscribed to form the Seven Stars. On the deceased’s natal star, burn through one star. Place the silk before the spirit table, extinguishing all lamps and candles on all sides to plunge the space into darkness. The dharma master recites the secret incantation and sprays water, while the mourners stand in a ring. From the burned spot, secretly peer within—then the deceased will appear as in life.

The manifestation curtain consists of seven panels of silk, arranged in a wooden-fence pattern on all sides.

The master says: This is the inner secret of the Divine Tiger, unknown to the world. Now that the Great Teaching flourishes, it is transmitted forth to be bestowed upon the lineage’s successors. Those of the Dao who obtain this should recognize its swift and responsive efficacy—unlike ordinary Divine Tiger summonings. Keep it secret.

The □□(ghost+chrysanthemum) □□□(ghost+kalpa) method: With the middle finger of the middle hand, visualize a blue-clad child descending from the Dipper with a single *qi*, then blow upon the banner seven times—whereupon it falls.

*The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*, Scroll Seventeen concludes.

---

*The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
**Title:** *The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.
**Source text:** *Daoist Canon*, *Dongzhen* section, Methods category.

*The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*, Scroll Eighteen
**Chapter Twenty: The Transmutation of Immortals into Human Form**

The master says: To refine the form into perfection is the work of divine transcendents. When the three fields of the adept shine with radiance, the four symbols merge in harmony, the yang fire and yin talisman fuse with the alchemy of creation, and the spirit is whole with its full complement of numbers—then one ascends at dawn in broad daylight. This is the Dao of refining the form to achieve deathlessness. Why, then, would one need to rely on talismans and incantations?

Yet the world’s people, deluded in life and unenlightened by the Dao, enter the gates of darkness at death. Their single nature scatters and flies away, forever without a path to rebirth. If not for borrowing the transformative power of our own cultivation, harnessing the mysterious workings of water and fire in their mutual refinement, employing incantations to deliver them and talismans to revive them—how could the fragmented be gathered into a whole soul, the corpse be refined into a yang substance, and liberation be attained in an instant? Thus, this method is also the esoteric secret for saving the souls of the dead. How could one fail to revere it?

**The Altar for Refining and Deliverance**
The master says: Our altar’s refining and deliverance derive from the marvel of true water and fire. The sun’s essence and the moon’s radiance are called true water and true fire. Thus, the Great Teaching takes the Three Luminaries as its foundation. Since the marvel of water and fire was first attained by us, what difficulty is there in delivering the dead? Though the Lingbao Nanchang refining and deliverance method exists, its water and fire emerge from our own sun and moon.

One must know that this altar is the progenitor of all methods—how much more so for refining and deliverance? The art of smelting and forging is only here that the orthodox transmission’s marvel is attained.

**The Water Pool, Fire Pit, and Lamp Method**
**Mobilizing the Refining and Deliverance Official Generals**
The master says: The transformations of our body follow the movement of thought, becoming the divided forms of our yang spirit’s official generals. Merging with the *qi* of Heaven, we mobilize our spirit, entrusting it to the talismanic form and borrowing the breath of ordinary water and fire.

Internally, unite with the Dao in truth. First, visualize within our body, between the kidneys, a point of light the size of a bean. After a long while, it grows and flies out upon the water’s waves. The officials upon the waves all wear dark robes. The Jade Maiden, riding the *qi* of water, stands at the right of our body. We entrust her to the side of the water pool.

Then visualize within the heart a pellet the size of a tangerine. After a long while, true fire bursts forth. The officials within the fire wear red robes. The Jade Youth, riding the light, stands at the left of our body. We entrust him to the side of the fire pit.

Thereafter, burn the *Plain Flower True Mysterious Jade Radiance Yellow Edict* and the *Original Yang Spontaneous Refining Soul Red Register* to summon true water.

**Transmutation and Refinement**
The master says: When burning the *Yellow Edict* and *Red Register*, visualize each of the celestial bodies—thus, the water pool becomes the moon, and the fire pit the sun. Riding the light, they enter our body, merging with our body’s water and fire, and together enter the pool. One sees only a dazzling radiance, no longer perceiving the mundane world. Only then proceed.

**Plain Flower True Mysterious Jade Radiance Yellow Edict**
**Incantation:**
True Official of the Mysterious Unity, Pure and Wondrous Primordial Sovereign,
Send down true water, descending into the altar courtyard.
Wash away yin defilements, retain the true and admit the pure.
The soul returns to *ren* and *gui*, the womb nurtures the essence-spirit.
Drink and absorb the mysterious flower, float upon the green bloom.
The dharma flows in a mixed outpouring, the body possesses radiant light.
After ten thousand kalpas, fulfillment is complete; the Three and Five respond in resonance.
By the mysterious imperial talismanic command, the Great Yin receives and obeys.
Thus, as the decree is proclaimed.

The Master says: This Yellow Edict is precisely the method for transforming true water. One should guide the moon’s rays to infuse the brush when inscribing it. When burning it, visualize the moon’s essence entering the mixed-water pool.

**Primordial Yang Naturally Refines the Soul’s Crimson Register**
**Incantation:**
Mixed *qi* crimson cinnabar, celestial radiance penetrates the Yang.
The crow advances swiftly, the golden rooster spreads wide.
The immortal furnace’s jade portal, the cavern descends with true light.
Flowing fire blazes fiercely, the yin corpse returns to hardness.
By the talismanic command of the Supreme, the true Yang jade decree.
Invoke and descend the fire *qi*, to shine with the sun’s brilliance.
By the borrowed talisman’s entrusted *qi*, transform and refine at Southern Prosperity.
Thus, as the decree is proclaimed.

The Master says: Having transformed the true water and fire, approach the water pool to perform the water-refining method, called "moon’s rays refining the corpse."

**Pure Yin True Water Forms the Lustrous Plain Flower Cavern-Yin Jade Talisman**
**Incantation:**
The Great Dao’s true center, the One as the primordial root.
The profoundly mysterious true One water emerges from the Gate of Longevity.
The hidden soul sinks through nine nights, creation’s transformation no longer exists.
Adrift on the bitter sea’s waves, submerged in the wind and waves’ depths.
Channel this primordial water to irrigate the foolish, decayed soul.
Vast and clear, suspended in the Great Void, this heart shines like a full wheel.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Yellow Flower’s law commands.

**Moon’s Essence Returns to True Jade Talisman**
Ten identical talismans, with ten rays of the method.
**Incantation:**
The primordial chaos blends with the celestial origin, jade liquid ripples on golden waves.
The lustrous essence descends as true water, pure and luminous *qi* abounds.
The numinous source overflows the empty cavern, densely emerging from the celestial river.
Fragrance fills the Yellow Court, the infant sings in response to the season.

The Master says: Circulate the Moon’s Auspicious Radiance Talisman, merging divine water to float upon the numinous pool. Bathe the soul-spirit in the clear, cold water, wash the soul in the moon’s radiant light. One then sees the soul’s form become an infant, riding white *qi* out of the water, and only then proceed to fire refinement.

**Infant Emerging from Water Diagram**
Channel the Heavenly One’s water, merging with the Great Yin to irrigate it. The moon resembles autumn, moon and water intertwine in splendor.

**Pure Li True Fire’s Flourishing Crimson Radiance Cavern-Yang Jade Talisman**
**Incantation:**
Flaming celestial sun above, resplendent spirit within the body.
Crimson light knows no decay, true *qi* blends with Yang essence.
Merging, the celestial gate opens, the Mysterious Woman visits the Plain Lord.
The Great Void’s form shines brilliantly, scorching and dispersing the hidden clouds.
The corpse’s *po* emerges from layered darkness, the cinnabar soul ascends to the jade dawn.
The infant nurtures the mysterious pearl, in vagueness forms golden blossoms.
Luminous, luminous, the gate of the Mysterious Supreme, never apart from the spirit within the body.
Nine refinements birth radiant scenes, shedding the dust-bound heart of kalpas.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the Yang-refining law commands.

**Sun’s Crystalline Refines the Soul, Attaining Oneness with the Spirit Jade Talisman**
Nine identical talismans, with nine rays of the method.
**Incantation:**
Resplendent and blazing, the Yang essence shines, molten gold casts fiery bells.
The Flourishing Crimson descends as true fire, refining yin to form the Yang spirit.
Bing and Ding’s fiery brilliance, blazing forth from the Vermilion Mound.
Refining the embryo returns to the original beginning, gazing upward to ascend in reverence.

Circulate the Sun’s Essence Yang Radiance Talisman, merging with the true fire’s blazing fiery pool, smelting the soul-spirit within the sun’s crystalline light. One then sees the infant riding the sun’s golden firelight, emerging from the flames to enter mutual refinement.

**Infant Emerging from Fire Diagram**
Channel the Earthly Two’s fire, merging with the Great Yang to smelt it. The fire resembles spring’s harmonious warmth.

**Mutual Refinement Method**
The Master says: The mutual refinement method’s transformations are especially wondrous, thus it fully seizes the marvel of creation’s mutual fusion. Borrowing the talismanic script’s operational efficacy, it achieves the union of water and fire, harmonizing soul and spirit. Yin diminishes as Yang grows, naturally perfecting the true—how could this be a minor dharmic power?

**Water and Fire United in Refinement, Forming the True Jade Talisman**
**Incantation:**
Flowing celestial Han essence, vast currents blend with Kun’s springs.
The Earth Mother covers the Heavenly Father, cold streams return to the true source.
The dragon ascends to reach the azure vault, Li and Bing intimately descend to the lower origin.
The azure sea births crimson flames, within fire bursts the celestial abyss.
The cock and hare nurture true essence, water and fire distinguish ugliness and beauty.
Purple clouds shroud the celestial valley, the mysterious pearl hangs in the center of heaven.
The Yellow Elder sings the cavern’s hymn, the dead soul regains the infant’s form.
Nine nines’ pure Yang complete, the Marshal stands rightly in the courtyard.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the water-fire mutual refinement law commands.

**Complete Perfection of the Dao, Returning Yang to Merge with the Body Great Talisman**
Visualize the sun and moon’s intertwined radiance, guiding the soul to stand at the center, then proceed to completion.
**Incantation:**
Heaven possesses the three wonders: sun, moon, and stars.
Earth possesses the three wonders: Yi, Bing, and Ding.
Humans possess the three wonders: essence, *qi*, and spirit.
Essence secured, *qi* complete, the primordial spirit is born.
Spirit united with *qi* sufficiency, only then is the true formed.
Jia water guards the soul to preserve a thousand years,
Geng metal restrains the *po* to form the peerless hero.
Bing and Ren, water and fire’s Yang essence,
Three fields coalesce into the celestial treasure vase.
Three *qi* return to One, reverting to the celestial root,
Beneath the Jade Capital Mountain, sun and moon shine.
Celestial light blends to illuminate Kunlun,
True water and true fire refine to form the true.
Ascending through the purple portal, emerging from darkness,
Transcending the three realms to pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the complete form’s deliverance and transformation law commands.

**Merging the Complete Form Talisman**

**Nine Heavens’ Immortal Refinement Method**
The Master says: The nine *qi* are heaven and earth’s honor, the root of all things. From the One undivided arise the three *qi*, and from the three *qi* are born the nine *qi*. Thus, the human body, receiving creation’s endowment to possess form, is guided by nothing other than the nine *qi*. Those who receive the nine *qi*’s Yang become human. Losing the nine *qi*’s Yang, they become ghosts. Cultivating the nine *qi*’s Yang, they become immortals. Therefore, in refinement and deliverance, Yang *qi* is used to deliver yin *po*. Thus, talismans are borrowed to aid it, incantations to invoke it. As the scripture says: "Hidden souls hear it and are delivered. Withered and decayed hear it and emit smoke. Dead souls attain this and regain their soul’s form." This is the work upon which both life and death depend—how could its benefit be small?

**First Yang Talisman**
**Second Yang Talisman**

**Third Yang Talisman**
**Fourth Yang Talisman**
**Fifth Yang Talisman**
**Sixth Yang Talisman**
