**Seventh Yang Talisman**
**Eighth Yang Talisman**
**Ninth Yang Talisman**

The Master said: The nine refinements begin from the Great Beginning’s formation of form. They are the method by which form is perfected, the body completed, and inner and outer made true. Without this method, the fetal womb becomes stagnant, and the dead *qi* solidifies at the root. Thus, the immortal refinement must be practiced.

It is said: When transmitting *qi*, one must rely on the *qi* of each respective direction to infuse it. The nine heavens distribute the eight directions and the center, each possessing the *qi* of its own direction. Applied to the human body’s creation, this means: The *Yu Shan Wu Liang* Heaven governs the *qi* of the East. All things arise from it, hence it is called "Beginning Azure"—rightly so.

When gathering into one, it is the *Huang Yan* *qi*. One is the beginning of numbers, and the color of the beginning is black, which transforms into yellow. *Yan* means "to flow through." Thus, the *qi* of *Huang Yan* is used to irrigate the fetal life, allowing the true *qi* to scour the yin of the corpse and open the fetal origin.

In practice, one visualizes the *qi* of the Eastern *Beginning Azure* Heaven, guiding it with the talisman into the crown of the deceased’s soul to infuse it. After a long while, the body becomes radiant. Next, the *Wu Liang* Heaven draws the *qi* of the South. The *Xu Yan* Heaven draws the *qi* of the West. The *Xiong Shu* Heaven draws the *qi* of the North. The *Bo Luo* Heaven draws the *qi* of the Northeast. The *Ying Sheng* Heaven draws the *qi* of the Southeast. The *Fan Fu* Heaven draws the *qi* of the Southwest. The *Gao Xu* Heaven draws the *qi* of the Northwest. The *Wu Xiang Wu Jie* Heaven draws the *qi* of the Central Heaven. Once the nine *qi* are complete, the Three Passes and Eight Sceneries are born. This is what is meant by "without enduring suffering, the body radiates light, and form and spirit are both wondrous."

The creative transformations of the nine heavens are all methods for scholars to refine the body and attain immortality. Thus, they are fully employed to deliver the deceased.

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Dong Ming Zi Hu*?
The Master said: The immortal embryo originally has no form; its likeness is cavernous, meaning it is indistinct between light and dark. When the first *qi* forms the womb and the second *qi* forms the fetus, there is as yet no clear or turbid. Within it is profound obscurity, but its mysterious gate is purely Yang, unadulterated. Purple is the color of Yang’s radiance, hence it is called the *Purple Gate*.

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Chang Ling Ming Xian*?
The Master said: With the third *qi*, the Mysterious Origin has already divided. Here, the spirit-soul is born. The *hun* is Yang. Cultivating it, one may attain long life and spiritual communion, radiance and penetrating clarity, and refine the body into an immortal.

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Dang Shi Ming Yan You*?
The Master said: There is Yin and Yang, life and death—this is the way of the world. The human body cannot be without Yin and Yang. Without cultivation, Yang diminishes and Yin prevails, and one dies to become a lowly ghost. Thus, *qi* belongs to the *po*, and the *po* belongs to Yin, its nature inclined to sinking and heaviness. Hence, *dang dang* refers to the stubbornness of stone, too heavy to ascend. When the *po* is strong, the *hun* dissipates. When the *hun* dissipates, the corpse becomes everlasting. One must circulate the Yang *qi* of the Four Great Elements to dissolve the path of the corpse’s *po*, merging it with the spirit-soul to refine and become an immortal.

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Wu Xian Zhong Ling*?
The Master said: The five *qi* complete the Five Phases. When the Five Phases are complete, the viscera are whole. Thus, when the Five Phases gather at the center, one may refine the immortal and attain spiritual communion. The viscera are not the lungs and kidneys as commonly understood, but rather the treasures within the body, fully preserved—this is called *zang*. Stored without dissipation, with a place to return, this is called *fu*. Thus, the scripture says: "When the Earth Treasury is opened, gold and jade reveal their form."

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Gao Zhen Chong Rong*?
The Master said: When the scholar has achieved success, the six transformations are no ordinary matter. The palaces within the body all attain spiritual communion in the highest realm. The work of becoming a true immortal is harmonious and fused, uniting with Heaven.

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Gao Xian Dong Ji*?
The Master said: The seventh *qi* is Lesser Yang. Here, the *qi* congeals into truth, returning to the primordial and highest realm. The work of verifying immortality is profound and subtle, beyond full comprehension. Those who enter its depths are called *Dong*. Its secrets are not revealed, hence it is called the *Xuan Shi*. Thus, the *Ji* and treasured texts are the dragon scripts of the *Daoist Canon*.

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Zhen Ling Hua Ning*?
The Master said: The eighth *qi* is when one is about to become a true immortal. This is what is meant by "a thousand times attaining spiritual communion, sitting in disappearance and standing in vanishing." Preserving the spirit and transcending transformation, guarding the One naturally, undispersed and unlost—this is called congealing. Thus, when the power of the Dao is complete, one may become true, attain spiritual communion, transcend transformation, and achieve firm congealment—all are the Way of long life.

Someone asked: What is the *qi* of the *Zi Ran Xuan Zhao*?
The Master said: When the nine Yang are complete, one ascends into formlessness, neither forced nor contrived, neither created nor fabricated—this is called *Xuan Zhao*. All are the gradual attainments of the diligent scholar, hence the subtle mysteries.

**Talismans for Receiving Transformation and Rebirth**
**Water Talisman for Refining the Womb and Nurturing Form**
Incantation:
*May the hun return to Ren and Gui,
May the po restrain the nine tombs.
Primal True Talisman,
Unfurl your light for ten thousand miles.
Command the breaking of dark obscurity,
Refine the hun with true water.
Bind the Yellow Flower of the Well Star,
May the Lady descend with sweet dew.
Great Mystery’s true aperture,
Return and restore essence and marrow.
Stir the turbid and lift the clear,
Enter life and exit death.*

**Fire Talisman for Refining the Embryo and Restoring Form**
Visualize the radiant light of the cinnabar field, knock the teeth twelve times, and form the Mudra of the Southern Dipper. Visualize the Primordial Beginning riding clouds above the crown. Write in red on yellow paper, infusing it with *qi*. Next, form the Mudra of the Northern Dipper, writing in black on yellow paper. When applying it, visualize nine phoenixes spraying flames and nine dragons spouting vast waters, the two *qi* intermingling within one’s own *qi*. Circulate them through nine cycles, and the Infant appears, its image following the body, golden light blazing brilliantly.

The incantation states:
The hidden and scattered return from afar,
The yin souls sink and fall.
Beyond the light of yang,
Iron walls seal them shut.
The wisdom sun halts its radiance,
The Southern Mound’s cinnabar fire.
The Primordial Beginning’s jade talisman,
Refines the embryo and scatters calamity.
The Northern Dipper revolves to the right,
The Southern Asterism abides to the left.
Return the embryo and transform the form,
All bones settle in harmony.
Escape the body through Heaven’s Pass,
Seated securely upon the golden lotus.

**Talisman and Incantation**
South *Li*, North *Kan*,
The tiger retreats, the dragon coils.
Counterflowing waters swirl,
Fiery flames refine and seethe.
The two blacks intertwine,
Yin and yang penetrate the passes.
Cultivate the hun and nurture the po,
Return to the golden elixir.
The numinous treasure serves as the *zi-wu* axis,
Circulating to merge with the true body.
Ten thousand disasters cannot invade,
Transcendence shapes the immortal.
Forever depart the ghostly bureaus,
The soul crosses the Cinnabar Mound.
Mounting the golden simurgh’s carriage,
Roam freely above.

**Granting the Golden Register to the Departed Soul**
The Most High grants life and delivers destiny,
The Golden Register of the Primordial Beginning’s Mysterious Cavern.
The root scripture of the *Numinous Treasure*,
Illuminating the Three Luminaries,
This is called the Heavenly Root.
The *Crimson Writ*’s jade characters,
Universally deliver heaven and humanity.
In the year of *Tai Sui* [X], the [X] month, [X] day, [X] hour,
By the Primordial Beginning’s talismanic decree,
Deliver [Name] to forever depart suffering,
Their name recorded in the Heavenly Court,
As commanded.

The **Register of Eternal Life**,
Having been inscribed and presented according to form at the Three Heavenly Gates,
Is granted in unison for the departed soul of [Name] to receive and uphold,
Ascending to the Cinnabar Bureau,
Refined and transformed into truth,
Form and spirit both wondrous.
Here the seal is applied,
Half retained for presentation above.

**The Celestial Bridge of the Supreme Heavenly Law**
The Register-Conferring Master, holding the dharma rank, your subject [Name].
The Register-Conferring Master, the Three Heavens’ Great Sage, the Heavenly Great Dharma Master of the Great Law.

The register is inscribed on silk,
Its reverse marked with a scroll,
And the frontispiece adorned as prescribed.
Written in gold powder and talismans,
Granted to the soul being delivered.
When sending the soul,
Present the talismanic decree toward the Heavenly Gate and the Bridge of Deliverance,
Burning it in fierce flames.

**The Teachings on the Three Paths and Five Sufferings**
The Master says:
The Three Paths and Five Sufferings,
Though their names differ, their retribution is one.
The toil of the Heavenly Path
Arises when the six senses are stained by the one center,
Thus at death, one receives the Heavenly Path’s toil.
The toil of the Earthly Path
Comes from laboring the body and wearing the form,
Hands moving, feet treading,
All dependent on earthly things,
At death, the familiar scenes are hard to forget,
Thus one receives the Earthly Path’s suffering.
The toil of the Watery Path
In life, through spring’s crookedness, ghostly cunning, and lust’s drowning of truth,
How much more in the sea of desire?
At death, thoughts cling unceasingly,
Thus one receives the Watery Path’s suffering.

The Five Sufferings, though their texts vary,
What are they?
Suffering of the heart, suffering of essence,
Suffering of form, suffering of spirit,
Suffering of the hun.
Together called the Eight Difficulties.
The scripture states:
*Forever deliver from the Three Paths, Five Sufferings, and Eight Difficulties,
Transcend the Three Realms.*
This speaks to the living.
If the living, within their mortal bodies,
Are not ensnared by desire’s defilements,
They forever depart the Five Sufferings and Three Paths,
Then may they transcend the Three Realms.
Now, those who practice the dharma,
Unable to deliver themselves from the Eight Difficulties,
Falsely establish Eight Gates,
Using talismans to deliver ghosts—this is mistaken.
The suffering of the heart:
Worldly people scheme and strategize,
Pursuing fame and sensuality,
All arising from the heart’s original purity,
Stained by desire—is this not the heart’s suffering?
Add to this lust and filth,
Yearning for feminine beauty—
This is called the suffering of essence.
When essence suffers, the body withers and strength fails,
Nearing the path of death.
If the body does not generate spirit,
The corpse’s po blazes fiercely.
Thus it is said: suffering of spirit.
When spirit departs, death is not far.
When the mortal body is lost,
The Dao-body unformed,
One becomes bleached bones in the wilds—
This is called the suffering of form.
When form suffers, one becomes a lowly ghost.
If the hun is incomplete,
Drifting as a scattered po,
Sinking and stagnating without return,
Only then is it the suffering of the hun.
The four sufferings—of heart, essence, spirit, and form—
Are the daily depletion in life,
Thus these sufferings arise.
The suffering of the hun
Comes only after death,
Then one receives its suffering.
The Five Sufferings were never meant to establish gates.
The Eight Difficulties also arise from the heart.
The heart is the master of the body;
When settled, the three karmas and six dusts are also settled.
When the heart is chaotic, myriad conditions arise.
If one wishes to burn talismans to deliver ghosts through the Eight Gates,
It would be better to deliver oneself from the Eight Difficulties.
Having failed to deliver oneself,
One cannot avoid death,
At death, the Eight Difficulties manifest as retribution.
At that time, relying on others to deliver oneself—
Is this not shameful?
Now, by the Master’s decree,
The Eight Difficulties’ gates are not established.
The gates that were established were later people’s fabrications.
Those who inherit the teachings
Should cultivate the body to deliver themselves,
Then rectify themselves before rectifying ghosts and spirits.
Therefore, the Three Paths and Five Sufferings’ talismans
Are no longer established,
Lest they delude the enlightened disciples of later generations.
Reflect on these teachings,
And do not practice false doctrines.

**The Departed Soul’s Holding of the Contract**
The Master says:
In the *Numinous Treasure* dharma,
There is a rite for the soul to hold the great contract in both hands
To enter the Three Heavenly Gates.
This is incorrect.
The formless and non-action
Take emptiness, stillness, and spontaneity as their root.
If holding a contract can enter the Heavenly Gates,
One is inevitably bound by form and attachment.
Bound by attachment, one does not attain the wondrous.
Thus the Teaching Master specifically removed the contract
And granted the Register of Eternal Life.

**The Essentials of Refining and Deliverance**
Following the *Crimson Clarity*’s decree to summon the generals,
Burn the talisman to summon the generals,
As in the method of transforming water and fire.
The officials and generals encircle the water pool and fire marsh,
The Emperor descends to his throne,
The Compassionate One witnesses the transformation,
The Nine Heavens spread their nets,
The Southern Asterism and Northern Dipper’s Imperial Lords stand in solemn array.
Summon the Water and Fire Lords to capture and transform the departed soul,
Refine the infant by burning the talisman,
Capture the infant and enter the water.
The water shines like autumn moonlight,
White and black blending,
The infant’s body gleams and glistens.
Capture and enter the fire for refinement,
The fire like spring’s warm qi,
Steaming and refining the infant to completion.
Within the golden orb,
A semblance of form appears,
Inter-refined within the purple-golden light.

The sun and moon conjoin their disks, guiding the soul into the *gan*-center,
The nine *qi* pour forth in irrigation, the golden light shines through.
After a long while, only countless golden orbs are seen—
What was known is now unknown.
The refinement and deliverance are complete.

---

*Wu Shang Xuan Yuan San Tian Yu Tang Da Fa*, Scroll Eighteen, concludes.

*Wu Shang Xuan Yuan San Tian Yu Tang Da Fa*
Text Title: *Wu Shang Xuan Yuan San Tian Yu Tang Da Fa*
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty
Thirty scrolls.
Source text: *Daoist Canon of the Zhengtong Era*, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category.

---

*Wu Shang Xuan Yuan San Tian Yu Tang Da Fa*, Scroll Nineteen
**Chapter Twenty-One: The Three-Five Step Pace**

The Master said: The secret of the three and five—how could it be easily known?
From one comes two, from two comes three,
And from three, the three luminaries divide and shine,
The three luminaries complete the three talents.
From the Great Ultimate come the Two Modes,
From the Two Modes come the Four Images,
The Four Images perfected, the Five Phases are whole.
The Five Phases whole, the five stars shine,
The five stars shining, the Five Peaks stand.
Thus, in the Dao, they are the Three Pure Ones;
In the world, they are the Three Talents;
In the divine, they are the Three Origins;
In man, they correspond to the three regions.
Again, in the Dao, they are the Five Elders;
In heaven, they are the five stars;
On earth, they are the Five Peaks;
In man, they are the five viscera.
Man possesses heaven and earth, form divided into yin and yang,
The Dao of *qi* complete within a single body.
If one cannot cause the Three Fields to gestate brilliance
And the five viscera to receive the numinous,
Then one begins to drift far from the Dao.
Those who cultivate it gather treasures in the Three Fields,
The five *qi* return to the origin,
The *po* is restrained, the *hun* is bound,
Spirit complete, *qi* full—
This is the immortal’s Way of honoring life.
Those who do not cultivate it allow the three *hun* to become the Three Corpses,
The five *qi* to become the Five Thieves,
The Five Thieves to become the Five Sufferings—
This is the ghostly Way of honoring death.
Thus, between heaven and earth, man is the spirit of the myriad things.
Therefore, every gesture of hand and step of foot
Must accord with the real—
The method of pacing the *gang* arises from this.
The pacing of the *gang* is the essence of flying heaven,
The numen of treading earth,
The true movement of man,
Causing the Three Talents to unite in virtue,
The nine *qi* to merge as one.
Ghosts and spirits revolve with heaven and earth,
Each step a pointing, each turn a revolution,
Perfected within the workings of creation,
The divine luminaries at the left.
Thus, one step symbolizes the Great Ultimate,
Two steps, the Two Modes,
Three steps, the Three Talents,
Four steps, the Four Seasons,
Five steps, the Five Phases;
Six steps, the Six Pitch Pipes,
Seven steps, the Seven Stars,
Eight steps, the Eight Trigrams,
Nine steps, the Nine Numinous Ones—
The ancestor of the myriad *gang*.

The Master said: The method of Yu’s Pace has lost its truth in the world.
Most can speak of it, but few attain it.
Those who attain it do not practice,
Those who practice do not focus—
Thus, it rarely proves efficacious.
The *Huoluo* Dipper practiced today is the pivotal essence of the Three-Five Yu Pace.
The interlocking numbers of the *River Chart*—
How could they be lightly dismissed?
Yet, due to common transmission errors,
They cannot transform and communicate with the numinous.
Now, I correct the errors and transmit the truth.

The Master said: One qi divides into three, named the Mysterious Origin. When the three qi divide and distinguish themselves, the Three Talents are established, mirrored in the human body. The forms of purity and turbidity separate into three sections. Each section has its spirit, also called the Three Fields. Each field contains treasure, thus one becomes two, two becomes three, and three becomes the myriad truths—together called the Three Origins. *Origin* means greatness, primacy. Thus, the *Book of Changes*’ *Qian* hexagram speaks of *origination, prosperity, fruition, and perseverance*, and so it is.

The Master said: The ancestral qi of the Five Phases is called the Five Elders. *Elder* is the model of beginnings, the ancestor. Drawing the essence of the Five Elders, they divide to become the Five Stars. The essence of the Five Stars stands firm as the Five Peaks, corresponding to the human body as the Five Viscera. Above, they align with the Five Stars; in the center, with the Five Peaks—thus the spirits reside within.

The Master said: The spirits of the Three and Five penetrate heaven and earth, yet all return to the single body. In their operation, there are methods of generation and restraint, of control and submission. For prayers, exorcisms, and offerings, the mutual generation and restraint apply. For driving away and curing, mutual conquest applies. Whenever treading the stars, first summon the spirits of the Three Origins and Five Phases, then proceed with the steps.

The Five Phases and Five Virtues generate one another:
Wood generates fire, fire generates earth, earth generates metal, metal generates water, water generates wood.

The Five Phases and Five Qi conquer one another:
Metal conquers wood, wood conquers earth, earth conquers water, water conquers fire, fire conquers metal.

The Upper Origin Pace belongs to heaven,
The Middle Origin Pace belongs to humanity,
The Lower Origin Pace belongs to earth.

**Incantation for the Upper Origin Pace:**
Step the essence of heaven, command the myriad spirits.
The Upper Origin conceals my body, General Tang Xiong.
Assist my true qi, repel and subdue demonic spirits.
Should any dare harm me, return it to their own person.
Let evil demons upon sight transform into fine dust.
Heavenly soldiers guard and protect—*hasten as the law commands!*

**Incantation for the Middle Origin Pace:**
Step the essence of humanity, strengthen yang and dispel yin.
Fortify my three hun-souls, extinguish ghosts and banish spirits.
Misfortune cannot reach me, calamity cannot touch me.
Harm cannot invade me—the Middle Origin hides my form.
General Ge Yong, lead a hundred thousand troops to guard my body—*hasten as the law commands!*

**Incantation for the Lower Origin Pace:**
Tread the numen of earth, secure the human path.
Heaven revolves, earth turns, above *Kui*, below *Qian*.
Yin closes, yang opens, true qi flows unceasing.
Ghosts cannot harm me, people cannot injure me.
Heaven is my canopy, earth my foundation.
Should any dare afflict me, seize them to *Kui* and *Gang*—the Lower Origin conceals my form.
General Zhou Wu, follow wherever I go, swiftly become my truth—*hasten as the law commands!*

The Master said: For subduing demons and evil, for overcoming calamities and dangers, first step the Upper Origin Pace. Once the sequence is complete, enter the Middle Origin Pace, then transform into the Lower Origin Pace. If subduing fierce evil, further transform to tread the Conquering Pace—then control heavenly dragons and ghostly spirits, responding to the heart’s call without fail. Guard this secret.

**The Conquering Pace of the Five Phases**
The Master said: For subduing fierce evil and overcoming calamities, tread this to subdue them. Water can extinguish fire, wood can conquer earth, fire can conquer metal, earth can conquer water, metal can conquer wood—thus apply the remedy in time. For example, to subdue fire’s misfortune, step metal and step water to restrain fire. The rest follow this pattern. If later students are unclear, simply follow the established form to complete the pace—do not add or omit.

**Incantation:**
The Five Phases mutually destroy, earth and water sever ties.
Water and fire annihilate, metal and wood do battle.
Ghosts and demons upon sight—behead and sever their feet.
Demon kings tremble in fear, shattered above and below.
Should any dare offend, forever sink into the dark abyss—*hasten as the law commands!*

The master said: This pace follows the sequence of metal conquering wood, wood conquering earth, earth conquering water, water conquering fire, and fire conquering metal. It is used for subduing and restraining. If seeking auspiciousness, reverse it to follow the mutual generation of the Five Phases.

**Pace of Mutual Generation of the Five Phases**
The master said: The pace of mutual generation follows wood generating fire, fire generating earth, earth generating metal, metal generating water, and water generating wood. Each generation and each restraint adhere to the sequence of water as one, fire as two, wood as three, metal as four, and earth as five—totaling fifteen steps, the Way of three and five.

**Incantation for Mutual Generation of the Five Phases:**
The Five Phases mutually generate, all affairs prosper.
Water and wood achieve, fire and earth unite.
Metal and water proceed together, misfortune transforms into fortune.
Ghosts cannot harm, people cannot encroach.
The dead revive, the withered flourish again.
*Hasten as the law commands!*

**Yu’s Pace of the Ninefold Numinous Dipper**
The master said: This is the Pace of the Vast Dipper, also called the Minor Three-Five Pace. Many in the world do not know its details, taking its common use for granted without understanding its profound subtleties. This pace can subdue wild evil, command ghosts and spirits, and dismantle temples—yet it is often used in reverse, so I now correct the error.

**Incantation:**
Sun and moon shine bright, heaven and earth pair.
I rise with Heavenly Peng into the celestial realm.
Passing lightly through the Celestial Balance, I meet the Assistant and retreat,
Returning to the Celestial Quail, facing the Heart.
The Dipper’s Way opens as the demonic path crumbles,
The Dipper’s essence wondrous, governing the twelve celestial stems.
Riding radiance, martial might arrays,
Qi ethereal, floating upon azure clouds.
Seven transformations stir, responding above to heaven,
Knowing change and transformation, fortune and misfortune arise.
The eight celestial lodges traverse the Celestial Pass,
Aligning with the six pitch-pipes, holding to Jia and Yi.
Treading the Celestial Flower, riding the Celestial Task,
Clear and cold abyss—yet one may walk upon the land.
Beside the Celestial Pillar, embracing the Celestial Heart,
From here I pass to ascend the Celestial Quail.
Leaning on the Celestial Assistant, gazing toward the Celestial Surge,
Entering the Celestial Inner, exiting through Heavenly Peng.
The Dipper’s Way opens, extending years and life,
Augmenting fortune and emolument, flowing to later generations.
Born in the netherworld for a thousand myriad years,
A thousand ghosts and ten thousand spirits naturally retreat.
*Hasten as the law commands!*

The master said: The pace currently practiced in the world reverses the sequence of exiting and entering the Dipper, rendering it ineffective. Now corrected, it can command ghosts and spirits and expel demonic paths. Guard this well, guard this well.

**The Wondrous and Supreme Three Heavens Jade Hall Canon, Scroll Nineteen—Concluded**

**The Wondrous and Supreme Three Heavens Jade Hall Canon**
*Title:* The Wondrous and Supreme Three Heavens Jade Hall Canon. Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.
*Source:* From the *Daoist Canon*, *Dongzhen* section, category of methods.

**The Wondrous and Supreme Three Heavens Jade Hall Canon, Scroll Twenty**
**Chapter Twenty-Two: Receiving Liberation in the Living Body**

The master said: The scriptures speak of receiving liberation in the living body, enduring through kalpas. This refers to those who cultivate in their present form. Later generations, unaware of self-cultivation, rely solely on ritual merit, seeking liberation before death—greatly missing the Dao. The "living body" here means the physical form in this present life. Those who "receive liberation" attain the Dao in their bodies, transcending the worldly net to become Perfected Ones. Thus, the body achieves immortality, enduring through kalpas without decay. Now, to liberate the body before death is to prepare the path for the time of dying—how can one know what is correct? This question is thus posed before the master.

The master said: This is because I do not approve of liberating the body before death in later generations. However, the Most High, in compassion for the world’s changes and humanity’s stubbornness—who can seek awakening?—realized that none could be liberated, and people would forever remain ignorant of the Dao. Thus, the precepts opened the method of liberation and transformation. Later students may cultivate their bodies and perfect their truth, freely entering the Golden Gate and roaming the Three Realms—what need would there be for this method?

The master said: Heaven generates the myriad beings, and humans are the most numinous. Yet their ranks vary: noble and base, worthy and foolish, rich and poor, long-lived and short-lived—all arise from different origins. What does this mean? Among the Six Paths, humans are the most numinous. Emerging from the Six Paths to become human is fitting. Those from the Heavenly Path are not malicious, their hearts always kind and benevolent. Those from the Spirit Path are secretly harmful, often wise and astute. Those from the Human Path know propriety and do not transgress, always following the correct principle. The rest from evil paths—such as hell, hungry ghosts, and beasts—are blind, deaf, mute, lowly, impoverished, stubborn, cruel, and lawless. Therefore, in liberating the living body, one must select whom to liberate.

Moreover, the world’s great nobles, kings, and dukes, and the immensely wealthy, their ranks and family resources—whether high or low, shallow or deep—all arise from worldly fortune. What does this mean? Those who in past lives believed in and followed the Dao and Buddhism, practiced rituals and expedient means, built roads and bridges, established baths and offered food, performed boundless good deeds, and personally received scriptural teachings yet failed to cultivate—such people, after death and rebirth, return to the human or heavenly realms, receiving retribution according to the magnitude of their merit. Having received their reward, if they act improperly along the way, upon death they must enter the dark gates. Thus, the Most High, in pity, specially bestowed this method of liberation, enabling them after death to bypass the earthly courts, erase their worldly transgressions, and become like Perfected Ones. The precepts have clear prohibitions, and people come to cultivate through these.

However, there are generals who command troops at the frontiers—these come from the ranks of deities and spirits. Though wealthy and noble, their names are entered in the Black Register, and they are tasked with killing. They are not suitable for liberation. Similarly, officials who administer punishments and interrogations, presiding over grievances and enmities, acting on their own judgment—these come from the earthly courts of the netherworld. They may be reborn in the Central Kingdom and attain nobility again, but they cannot be granted talismans for transcendence.

Those who inquire further may include scions of hereditary noble houses and heirs of immense wealth—young men of fleeting years who know nothing of the Three Honored Ones. These are the very sort haunted by the lewd and wandering ghosts that lurk beneath their eaves and gather at their gates. Though rich, they do not live long; though noble, they remain ignorant. Heaven’s overseers mark their deeds, and they perish swiftly. These, too, cannot be delivered.

Then there are those who carry meals along the roads—all the destitute and orphaned. In former lives, they accumulated karmic transgressions, and in this life, they endure the suffering of wailing and ceaseless toil, born as lowly men and dying as lesser ghosts. These, likewise, cannot be delivered.

Only elders of virtue, benevolent men, faithful laypeople, and nameless monks and Daoists who seek to return to the Great Dao, though unaware of its true source, may be delivered in this life so that, in death, they may follow the true path. For them, altars are regularly erected, and petitions are presented to the Three Heavens, notifying the courts of the netherworld to expunge their names from all records. Their names are then submitted to the celestial bureaus, inscribed upon jade tablets, and talismans are issued for them to wear. Half of each talisman is retained upon the body, while the other half is burned in offering. At the time of death, the talisman ascends with them.

All worldly people who hold no Daoist rank in life become lesser ghosts in death. During their time in the world, their names are bound to the registers of Mount Tai’s courts, interconnected across seventy-two case files, awaiting the opportunity for their records to be amended. To amend a record means that the registers of the earthly courts are linked to those of the celestial bureaus. Each case requires a brush, ink, paper, and an inkstone—whether made of paper or wood. These are burned along with the talisman for amending records.

The celestial overseers then sever and transfer the names from the earthly registers, issuing jade talismans for record amendment. These are inscribed on seventy-two slips of catalpa wood, written in cinnabar, and sealed with yellow paper before being dispatched. The talisman is sent down to the officials of the Eastern Marchmount’s netherworld courts, commanding them to expunge the transgressions of the named individual, wash away their karmic stains, and directly submit their names to the celestial bureaus to be inscribed upon jade tablets, awaiting the end of their allotted span so they may ascend to the divine realms of heaven. Let this command be carried out as decreed, transmitted by wind and fire couriers.

Issued on the [day] of the [month] in the year of the Great Year Star.

The Master says: For the faithful who receive deliverance, whose names are recorded in Fengdu, each is to be issued a talisman for the expungement of sins.

The True Talisman of the Most High for the Expungement of Sins and Love of Life:
Thirteen slips of cypress wood, inscribed in cinnabar, sealed in blue, and sent down.

This talisman is dispatched to the courts of the Yellow Springs, the Three Offices of Fengdu in the Northern Capital, the Nine Bureaus, and the Twelve River Sources, commanding the expungement of the named individual’s three lifetimes of submerged retributions and accumulated karmic transgressions, severing their records from the celestial bureaus and inscribing their names upon jade tablets. When their allotted span ends and their fate is exhausted, they shall ascend directly to the Vermilion Mound.

As commanded, transmitted by wind-and-fire courier.
In the cyclical year ____, month ____, on an auspicious day and hour, the decree is issued.

The Master declares: For the faithful who have received deliverance, whose names have departed the Northern Bureau, yet the Three Officials wield their brushes and the Four Departments scrutinize transgressions, it is now fitting to issue a decree to the Three Officials—the Jade Talisman for the Pardon of Transgressions.

**The Most High’s Jade Talisman for the Deliverance of Life and Pardon of Transgressions**
Three slips of cypress wood, inscribed in cinnabar; sealed in yellow and sent down.

This talisman is dispatched to the Three Primes, the Three Officials, the Nine Bureaus, and the One Hundred Twenty Offices, commanding them to comply with the Dao’s decree and talismanic grace, expunging the sin registers, inscribing names upon golden tablets, ensuring the yang spirit’s eternal life, and harmonizing with the Dao. Thus, when the named individual’s allotted span ends, they shall ascend directly to the Immortal Capital.
As commanded, transmitted by wind-and-fire courier.
In the cyclical year ____, month ____, on an auspicious day and hour, the decree is issued.

The Master declares: For the faithful who have received deliverance, whose names are now recorded in the celestial bureaus, it is fitting to assign divine protectors to guard their mortal forms, so that when their destined term concludes, their spirits shall ascend together.

**Great Protector of the Body, Mysterious True Guardian**
For the male official who has received deliverance, [Name],
Inscribed in cinnabar on yellow paper, issued to the recipient for safekeeping and wearing.
**Incantation:**
By the talismanic decree of the Mysterious Capital, the Mysterious True is summoned.
In accordance with the writ and command, they shield and guard the delivered body.
No calamity may assail, no misfortune may encroach.
For a hundred years they shall protect, and when life’s end comes, ascend together as one.

**Jade Maiden Xunying, Guardian**
For the female official who has received deliverance, [Name],
Inscribed in cinnabar on yellow paper, issued to the recipient for safekeeping and wearing.

The above-mentioned great spirits and jade maidens, with a retinue of a million, shall guard the talisman within the recipient’s body, awaiting the appointed end of their years, when the protective spirits shall soar and escort them.
As commanded.

The Master declares: For the faithful who have received deliverance, it is fitting to issue the talismanic precepts for pre-mortem cultivation.

**Register of Salvation Formula**
**The Most High’s Pre-Mortem Yellow Register for Salvation from Suffering**
This true talisman for salvation has been inscribed and presented at the Three Celestial Gates, petitioning for the eradication of sin’s roots, the severance of ties to the earthly prisons, and the inscription of names in the immortal bureaus.
Here, affix half the seal, with the other half placed upon the document in the earthly prisons.
When this is burned in the future, they shall forever depart the nether realms.

**Honorable Titles of Salvation:**
The Jade Treasure August Honored One delivers.
The Mysterious True Myriad Blessings Honored One delivers.
The Supreme Wondrous Honored One delivers.
The Mysterious August Jade Emperor delivers.
The Delivering Immortal August Sage delivers.
The Life-Loving Deliverer of Lives delivers.
The Supreme Numinous Void Emperor delivers.
The Boundless Great Florescence delivers.
The Jade Void Luminous Emperor delivers.
The True Emperor of the Grotto Spirits delivers.
The Seeking-Sound Savior from Suffering delivers.
The Deliverer from the Nine Hells delivers.
The Eraser of Sins and Remover of Transgressions delivers.
The Reconciler of Grievances delivers.
The Compassionate Welcomer delivers.
The Great Compassionate Savior from Suffering delivers.
The Great Compassionate and Great Benevolent delivers.
The Three Treasures and Nine Florescence delivers.
The Jade Hall and All Bureaus deliver.
The Orthodox Unity and All Bureaus deliver.

These Celestial Worthies are arrayed in three horizontal rows and inscribed accordingly.

**The Primordial Beginning’s Talismanic Decree: The White Slip of the Yellow Register for Salvation from Suffering**
Issued to the boundless worlds of the ten directions, the Three Officials and Nine Bureaus, the One Hundred Twenty Offices, the Five Thearchs’ Examiners, the Nine Hells of the Underworld, the Mighty Celestial Enforcers, the Punitive Divine Soldiers, the Officers of Life and Registers, the Officers of Merit and Destruction, the Ox-Headed Prison Guards, and the Great Demons of the Three Realms.
Pre-deliver the mortal form of [Name], expunge the sin registers, record their living name, dissolve all sins, reconcile all grievances, and by these nine wondrous precepts, bestow the merit of pre-deliverance, ascending to the celestial heavens.
As commanded.
In the cyclical year ____, month ____, on an auspicious day and hour, the decree is issued.
Holding the dharma rank, your servant [Name].

**The Great Celestial Master of the Three Heavens and the Great Dharma of the Capital of Heaven.**

**Register of Longevity Formula**
**The Supreme Pre-Mortem Golden Register of Longevity**
The Primordial Beginning’s Grotto Mystery, the Numinous Treasure’s Original Scripture.
The revelation of the Three Luminaries is called the Root of Heaven.
The delivered body receives salvation, enduring through kalpas without end.
In the cyclical year ____, month ____, on an auspicious day and hour, the Primordial Beginning’s talismanic decree is issued, pre-delivering [Name] to alter their fate in the earthly prisons, inscribing their name in the immortal bureaus, forever escaping suffering, and enlisting their name in the Three Heavens.

**The True Talisman of Longevity**
This talisman of numinous longevity has been inscribed and presented at the Three Celestial Gates, to be jointly acknowledged and issued to [Name] for safekeeping and wearing.
When the destined time of their passing arrives, they shall not pass through the earthly prisons but ascend directly to the Vermilion Palace.
Refined nine times to perfection, both form and spirit shall attain wondrousness.
Here, affix half the seal, with the other half retained on the memorial document.
When this is burned in the future, they shall forever depart the nether realms and ascend directly to the Vermilion Palace.

**The Bridge of the Supreme Longevity and Refinement of the True**
The Southern Culmen’s Lord of Longevity delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Deliverer of Lives delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Life-Loving Lord delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Celebrator of Life delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Officer of Life delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Officer of Records delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Extender of Lifespan delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Augmenter of Years delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Deliverer from Calamity delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Marshal delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Recorder of Life delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Disperser of Misfortune delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Dissolver of Disasters delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Recorder of Records delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Bestower of Blessings delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Examiner of Records delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Guardian of Life delivers.
The Southern Culmen’s Scribe of Goodness and Recorder of Merit delivers.
The Lord of the Vermilion Mound delivers.
The Divine Lord of the Vermilion Mound delivers.
These Lords are arrayed in three horizontal rows and inscribed.

**The Primordial Beginning’s Talismanic Decree: The White Slip of the Golden Register of Longevity**
Issued to the Vermilion Heaven World of the Southern Realm, the Vermilion Mound Fire Bureau of the Southern Prosperity Upper Palace, the Great Lord of Longevity, Marshal Han, the Officers of Life and Records, the Venerable Spirits of Lifespan Extension and Calamity Deliverance, the Great Spirits overseeing the resurrection of the deceased, and the supervisors of pre-mortem deliverance for [Name].
Inscribe their name upon the purple register, record their goodness in the golden annals.
Deliver them from calamity, extend their lifespan, and augment their years.
When their allotted span ends, they shall not pass through the earthly prisons but ascend directly to the Vermilion Heaven.
Refine their spirit into divine elixir, ascend as immortals, and attain the Dao.
As commanded.
In the cyclical year ____, month ____, on an auspicious day and hour, the decree is issued.
Holding the dharma rank, your servant [Name].

The Three Heavens’ Great Sage, Supreme Heavenly Great Dharma Celestial Master.

The two registers on the right shall be inscribed in gold on blue-green silk and adorned with yellow damask as prescribed.
The Ninefold Wondrous Precepts shall be written in vermilion on yellow paper and conferred upon the initiate.

The Supreme Pre-Death Cultivation Ninefold Wondrous Precepts.
According to the True Statutes: those who receive the Ninefold Wondrous Precepts and wear the Precious Register of Salvation and Longevity shall, in their lifetime, receive great blessings and enjoy long, unbroken years. When their allotted span ends, they shall not be subject to karmic rebirth but ascend directly to the Vermilion Heaven. This is for those who, as beginning celestial learners, gradually ascend to the ranks of immortals.

Now, the pre-death cultivator [Name] seeks to receive the Ninefold Wondrous Precepts, to restrain body and mind, and to pray for the protection of the True Ones.
The Heavenly Worthy declares:
1. Be filial and yielding, reverently supporting your parents.
2. Be diligent and loyal to your sovereign.
3. Do not kill; compassionately save all beings.
4. Do not commit adultery; maintain integrity in conduct.
5. Do not steal; promote righteousness and restrain the self.
6. Do not be reckless; do not oppress others with anger.
7. Do not deceive; do not harm the good with flattery.
8. Do not be arrogant; do not neglect the Perfect Truth.
9. Do not waver; uphold the precepts single-mindedly, and protect the Guardian Kings of the Precepts.

In the cyclical year ____, month ____, on an auspicious day and hour, the decree is issued.
Holding the dharma rank, your servant [Name].

The Three Heavens’ Great Sage, Supreme Heavenly Great Dharma Celestial Master.
The Master declares: When the faithful initiate approaches ordination, they shall shed the Three Calamities, transcend the Nine Perils, escape the Five Sufferings, then sever the roots of evil, dissolve the Black Register, extinguish the Three Corpses, and dispel the Yin Spirits—only then shall they become a disciple of the Dao.
If the Three Calamities remain unshed and the Nine Perils untranscended, illness and affliction shall still trouble them. If the roots of evil are not severed and the Black Register not dissolved, ascension to the True shall be difficult. If the Three Corpses remain unextinguished, desires shall multiply. If the Yin Spirits are not dispelled, one shall remain dull and unaware.
Now, purify and refine, wash away filth and polish the light. Let form and spirit become one in clarity, forever free from attachment.
If, after receiving the precepts, one indulges in wine and lust as before, unchanged—if anger, greed, and desire persist—then the Register of Pre-Death Cultivation shall be in vain, and one shall not escape the Register of Ghosts.

The Jade Talisman for the Eradication of the Three Calamities
At the time of ordination, have the initiate stand before the altar and receive the decree face-to-face.
Incantation:
The True Talisman descends, shining before the Stellar Palace.
The life-officer of [Name] dissolves misfortune and eradicates the Three Calamities.
Boundless blessings and protection attend this ordination.
Body and immortal become one.
As commanded.

The Talisman for Transcending Perils
Incantation:
The qi of the Dao flows; the qi of fortune circulates.
The Most High specially delivers the male initiate of pre-death cultivation.
Name inscribed in the Jade Calendar, calamities shall not arise.
Forever freed from peril, transgressions eradicated.
No disaster, no hindrance—peer to the True Immortals.
As commanded.

The Talisman for Eradicating the Three Corpses and Purifying the Seven Spirits
Before the altar, recite the incantation seven times over the initiate, then burn the talisman.
Incantation:
The Emperor’s salvation from the Mysterious Capital extends grace through the Jade Crucible.
Erase your sin-register, deliver your mortal frame.
Peng Shan, Peng Zhi, Peng Jiao, and Fu—
all transform and ascend as immortals, while the Corpse-Dog prostrates.
The Corpse-Sparrow devours Yin, banishing poison and malice.
Purify the foul lungs, open the gate of goodness.
The demonic gate is sealed; ascend to the Immortal Capital,
all transformed by the Mysterious Virtue.

The Master declares: Having eradicated the Three Calamities, transcended the Nine Perils, subdued the Three Corpses, and harmonized the Seven Spirits, one shall escape the Five Sufferings and proceed to cultivate the True.

The Talisman for Deliverance from the Suffering of Love and Attachment
Incantation:
The True Talisman delivers from suffering, clarifying your heart.
The heart’s spirit, the Cinnabar Origin, ever guards the central chamber.
No lust, no disorder—day and night, constant peace.
Freed from the suffering of attachment, turn the Great Dharma Wheel.
At life’s end, undisturbed, ascend into the Three Clarities.
As commanded.

The Master declares: At the altar, address the initiate thus: The heart is the abode of the spirit; keep it ever pure and undivided. If defiled, the heart is disordered and the spirit depleted, and one sinks into the ghostly realms. Now, this good man has turned his heart to the Great Dao and established pre-death cultivation. He must think little and desire less, avoiding exhausting thoughts. After ordination, let his heart be like the night moon—perfectly bright, clear, and pure. Thus shall ascension to immortality be effortless.

The Talisman for Deliverance from the Suffering of Greed and the Body’s Affliction
Incantation:
The Most High delivers the person, protecting the mortal body.
Body like a precious tree, undecaying, unharmed.
Neither aging nor depleting, its hue ever springlike.
Uphold the precepts against desire and disorder; sever greed and anger.
Cut off all movement, sweep away the Six Dusts.
Body at peace, form at ease—ascend with the immortals.
As commanded.

The Master declares: At the altar, address the initiate thus: The form is the body. Where there is a body, there is desire. Thus, the body is the mechanism of the Six Roots—eyes see, ears hear, and the body follows. Self-seeking, profit-chasing, and restless striving exhaust the form, causing the greatest harm. Now, having received ordination, cherish your body. Do not act recklessly, and you shall not suffer.

The Talisman for Deliverance from the Suffering of Lust and the Essence’s Affliction
Incantation:
The Most High delivers the person, the Jade Talisman protects the spirit.
Spirit undisturbed, essence-source unspilled.
Thus freed from desire, body and mind purified.
Receiving the talisman, refine and transform, clarifying the central chamber.
Primordial essence unmoved, forever attaining the Immortal True.
As commanded.

The Master declares: At the altar, address the initiate thus: Essence is the radiant essence of the entire body. Ordinary people, driven by desire, deplete their true essence, dissipating primordial harmony and withering their nature and life without awareness. Thus, excessive desire harms essence—this is called the suffering of essence. Therefore, the Sage said: “Do not agitate your essence, and you may attain long life.” After ordination, cultivate a pure heart and few desires. Guard and preserve your primordial essence; let it neither spill nor leak. Gradually, you shall enter the Immortal True.

The Talisman for Deliverance from the Suffering of Splendor and the Spirit’s Affliction
Incantation:

The Jade Talisman preserves the spirit; golden elixir refines the form.
Preserve your hun-soul’s essence, govern your po-soul’s numen.
When the hun is at peace and the po settled, the spirit-chamber becomes clear and serene.
The Three Passes and Nine Portals—each orifice radiant with light.
The spirit whole, without leakage, you shall ascend to the Upper Clarity.
As commanded.

The Master declares: The spirit is the master of the entire body. Ordinary people, driven by excessive desire and delusion, fail to guard their spirit-abode; their minds constantly stray outward, their bodies wither like rotting wood, the Nine Portals become obstructed, and the body ceases to generate spirit. Thus, *The Central Yellow Scripture* states: “Alas for the twelve towers of the Mysterious Palace—who knows they have become the dwelling of the Three Corpses?” Then the spirit is depleted. Therefore, the Celestial Master’s maxim declares: “When the mind is chaotic, the spirit naturally dissipates; when qi is exhausted, the form withers as well. Those who profane the Supreme Law of the Most High shall daily consort with ghosts.” Is this not the suffering of the spirit? After ordination, constantly guard the spirit-chamber, let no reckless thoughts arise, and both form and spirit shall attain subtlety, merging with the Dao in truth.

**Talisman for Deliverance from the Suffering of the Corporeal Soul**
Incantation:
The Jade Talisman preserves the spirit; the Jade Talisman connects to the True.
The talisman transforms primordial change; the talisman transfigures into true essence.
The spirit-heart unmoved, the numinous palace ever clear.
No greed, no desire, no chaos, no licentiousness.
The hun-soul serene and upright, the myriad qi eternally preserved.
Unburdened by suffering and affliction, the body radiates light.
The Three Realms attend as guards; the Five Emperors oversee the welcoming.
The myriad spirits pay homage; your name is inscribed in the Upper Clarity.
As commanded.

The Master declares: When the spirit abides constantly, the hun-soul remains ever at peace. When the spirit-chamber is in turmoil, the corpse-po delights in greed, anger, sorrow, thought, grief, joy, fine clothing, rich food, desire, and licentiousness—all the nature of the po. If one can guard the true and eliminate the reckless, purifying the spirit-chamber, then the hun-soul shall remain perpetually tranquil and unified. If one fails to guard the true, defiling the numinous orifices, the spirit perishes and the boundaries collapse, the po flourishes and the corpse rages—then the hun scatters and dwindles. Once the hun dissipates, one drifts far from immortality and draws near to ghosts. From this day of ordination onward, never forget devotion to the Dao, never exhaust the primordial spirit. When the spirit is not chaotic, the hun naturally finds peace, and only then may one receive the teachings of preparatory cultivation.

The Master declares: The ordained have already passed through the Five Gates of Suffering. Yet while the mortal form remains in this world, one must still guard against the defilements of transgressing precepts, lest one sink to the level of the common multitude. Though delivered from the suffering of the Corpse of Peng, this is merely a formal record. You must further uphold the Ten Precepts—matters commonly violated by worldly people. If you uphold them without transgression, you may remain free of blemish. If you cannot, relying solely on the register of preparatory cultivation to ascend directly in the future may not meet expectations. The ordained should diligently uphold and not violate them. The ordaining master, at the altar, should further instruct thus:

First, you must first honor the incense and flame of the Three Perfected. The Three Perfected are the Dao, the Scriptures, and the Master—also called the Three Honored Ones. As an ordained disciple, your name is now inscribed in the Jade Register; you must not newly serve base earthly spirits or heterodox deities. All blood sacrifices and offerings not arising from self-cultivation of the True are called demonic ghosts. From this day forward, if you have previously served gods or spirits before ordination, you may now ritually send them off. By “ritual,” I mean preparing incense, flowers, wine, fruit, and scriptures to dispatch them—never serve them again. If you have previously worshipped the Buddha before ordination, you must establish the altar of the Supreme Three Honored Ones above the Buddha’s position; you must not allow the Buddha to overshadow the position of the Most High.

Second, after ordination, you must diligently tend the incense and flame, strictly observe fasting and precepts, and practice reciting true scriptures. By “true scriptures,” I refer to texts such as the *Scripture of Salvation* and the *Chapter on Generating the Spirit*. As an ordained disciple, you should study the *Daoist Scriptures* to distinguish yourself for future ascension. If you persist in delusion and disbelief, rejecting the Dao, the Three Officials shall investigate and deduct twenty years from your lifespan.

Third, after ordination, you must cultivate a heart of kindness and compassion. You must not secretly scheme against the good, harbor envy toward the worthy and sagely, or sow discord and incite litigation. You yourself must not utter falsehoods or deceptions, devise plots to frame the innocent, amass excessive wealth, covet superficial gains, or swallow the possessions of the poor and weak to enrich yourself. If, after ordination, you do not reform past misdeeds, after receiving the precepts, the Guardian Spirit Kings shall report to the Three Officials, who will revoke your blessings.

Fourth, after ordination, you must purify body and mind, gradually distancing yourself from desire. You must not gaze upon the young and beautiful, indulge in brothels, or commit unlawful or improper acts. From this day forward, sever thoughts of spousal relations; there are also times of precept observance. Maintain regular practice, and ghosts and spirits shall hold you in awe—the ranks of immortals draw near.

Fifth, after ordination, you must cultivate frugality in diet. You must not arbitrarily slaughter the six livestock, indulging in rich and fatty foods, which disturb and disorder your true nature. If you can maintain a daily vegetarian diet, it is especially excellent. If you cannot yet abstain from meat, you should at least observe a morning vegetarian fast. If even this is not possible, you may fast on the Three Origins, Eight Nodes, Gengshen, Jiazi, and your own birthday. On the day before the fast, abstain from desire; on the fast day itself, abstain from meat; on the third day, act as you please. Practicing thus is quite manageable. If you cannot uphold these precepts, relying solely on this fasting practice as preparatory cultivation, expecting future ascension, may not meet expectations. Moreover, you risk punishment: the Three Officials shall investigate, and the cold night’s wind-knives shall become your burden.

Sixth, after ordination, in all matters, restrain the mind. Beyond clothing and food, follow nature without deliberate pursuit. If you seek the heavens to nourish beings, even birds and beasts are constantly provided for with insects and grains. How much more so for humans born between heaven and earth—how could there be no allotted blessings? Each has a destined portion; do not exhaust your mind and thoughts in vain.

Seventh, once ordained, let compassion and mercy guide your heart, and constantly practice hidden virtue. Hidden virtue means acting without others knowing—quietly performing acts of convenience as your strength allows. Where you can, do so: redress wrongs for the wronged; mediate conflicts for those in dispute; reconcile discord among kin; gently guide disobedient juniors with reason; feed the hungry and thirsty; heal the sick and suffering; clothe and nourish the cold and starving. If others wrong you, do not dwell on it; if you wrong others, reflect and repay them. Practicing thus, you may accumulate blessings for the human and heavenly realms. If you fail to do so, relying solely on preparatory cultivation to expect ascension may lead you astray—ponder this deeply.

Eighth, once ordained, if your ancestors remain in the netherworld while you seek ascension for yourself, have you not heard the scriptures say: *"Seven generations ascend, forever freed from the ghostly officials"*? And the *Three Invocations Hymn* states: *"Seven generations born in heavenly halls."* Thus, the ancients who cultivated the Dao first delivered their distant ancestors before attaining transcendence themselves. If those ancestors remain undelivered, the root of death persists, and you cannot ascend. To deliver them, must you forcibly expend gold and silk to perform the *Nine Netherworld Yellow Register* rites? Rather, the key is to broadly accumulate hidden merit, seeking to perform merit without cost. The most fitting method is the *Great Ultimate Refinement and Deliverance* of Master Ge Xianweng—a practice simple and easy, requiring little expense. If you cannot perform it yourself, engage a virtuous ritual master each month to conduct it on your behalf, accumulating hidden merit to deliver your ancestors. Then, when you ascend in the future, you will do so without shame.

Someone asked: *"If an ordained person has a relative who is a monk, and each month has them recite scriptures and confer the Netherworld Precepts to deliver the deceased, is this sufficient? Must one perform the Great Ultimate Refinement?"*

I replied: *"An ordained person is now a disciple of the Dao, having received the supreme grace of the Most High, registered in the Jade Calendar as a mortal destined for transcendence beyond the immortal realms. If you wish to deliver your ancestors, even the Buddha’s vehicle could liberate them—but as a Dao disciple, you should not follow another teaching. You must perform the Great Ultimate Refinement rites of your own tradition to be proper and correct. If you act ignorantly or mistakenly, the Nine Bureaus will investigate, the Four Offices will impose penalties. Who will bear the blame? Strive with diligence."*

Ninth: Having already received deliverance, one must treat all beings with equanimity. Regard all—whether foe or kin—as equal. Let no small grievance breed great enmity, nor private resentment obstruct public justice. Remember that this body is not your own, and balance both gratitude and resentment. Do not persist in delusion, lest you fall into the karmic consequences of this life. If you wish to deliver others, apply your thoughts with utmost care.

Tenth: All true immortals ascend to perfection only after cultivating practice and nurturing refinement. Now, though you have received deliverance, it is not through your own cultivation but by dedicating merit at the altar in advance, differing from those who, upon death, must pass through hell before ascending to the Cinnabar Heaven. While this may serve as a provisional means of deliverance, it is not as fitting as cultivating practice yourself. In self-cultivation, preserving authenticity and upholding integrity come first; reciting scriptures and maintaining a vegetarian diet follow. Yet the Daoist gate is vast, its methods manifold, and the entry point may prove arduous. Without innate spiritual capacity, even in old age, one may never encounter a perfected master’s guidance. Now, through this deliverance, I briefly outline the method of cultivation, lest you remain ignorant of the path and find yourself adrift before the boundless ocean of sagely attainment. It is better to withdraw the mind inward, observe within, and let no worldly affairs disturb you. Before engaging in any endeavor, collect the mind in silent sitting; stability and wisdom will arise naturally, and the Jade Clarity realm will appear in clarity. This is what is meant by the great stability of divine radiance. Through this, one may gradually transcend birth and death, escape the cycles of rebirth, and ascend naturally without need for further cultivation. If your roots are not firm and you hear this with doubt or hesitation, unable to maintain practice, then at least observe the precepts, wear the talismans of preemptive merit, and await future deliverance. Do you comprehend my words? Only after full understanding may you ascend the altar to receive deliverance.

From the severing of the corpse-soul onward, these instructions may be recorded in ritual manuals and recited at the altar to admonish those receiving deliverance to cultivate in advance. Once the recipient has been enlightened with the Ten Precepts and received the talismans for extinguishing evil roots, they may then enter the altar and undergo the refining through water and fire.

The master said: The water and fire preemptive refinement of the delivered refers to the formal procedure. The recipient is not a dead soul—how can they enter water and fire? Why is it called "refinement and deliverance"? They fail to consider that in ordinary people, the nine orifices are obstructed, the body does not generate spirit, and they merely inhabit a form, borrowing qi to move. This refinement does not temper the form but the spirit. Once the spirit within the body is smelted, the body naturally radiates light, and the golden tower and jade chamber generate spirit without fail. When spirit is generated, the corpse perishes and the po-soul falls away; the yang spirit remains whole, naturally free from calamity and demonic interference, able to ascend to the realm of transcendence. If the spirit is not refined, the hun-soul weakens while the po-soul flourishes, the corpse’s dust obscures clarity, illness arises easily, and death approaches swiftly, consigning one to the rank of lower ghosts. Even with preemptive merit, one cannot rely on it for transcendence. Practitioners must awaken to this truth.

**Method for Preemptive Refinement of the Delivered through Water and Fire**

The master said: For those who have accumulated preemptive merit, set up the refinement altar as usual. According to the method, guide the recipient to first enter the water pool, where talismans are burned and rituals performed. Then proceed to the fire pool, where talismans are burned and rituals performed. Only after both are completed are the Nine Perfected Wondrous Precepts conferred, along with the preemptive treasure talismans, before the altar is dismissed.

**True Water Talisman for Scouring Corpse-Dust**
*Incantation:*
Pure and cool jade liquid, sweet dew cascading.
Yellow blossoms flow forth, the jade body naturally fragrant.
Within cleansed, without purified, the po-soul refined, the hun-soul dissolved.
Scouring the filth of the heart, the five viscera cool.
A hundred passages unobstructed, refining into pure yang.

**Talisman for Bathing the Essence in the Water Pool**
*Incantation:*
Three barriers purified, a hundred joints freely flowing.
Bathing the true spirit, effulgent liquid merging.
Irrigating the womb’s stagnation, extinguishing demonic malevolence.
The flower pool overflows, suffusing the three palaces.
The true body sealed, ultimately achieving immortal attainment.

**Talisman for Irrigating the True Origin in the Water Pool**
*Incantation:*
Washing the womb, dispersing stagnation, untying knots, opening the heart.
Spirit complete, qi replete, the body radiant with light.
Myriad spirits pay homage, the name inscribed in the Upper Clarity.
No loss, no transmigration, ascending to the rank of immortal perfected.

**Talisman for Refining the Yin Corpse with Fire to Open Peace**
(This is the true fire of the Three Luminaries’ radiant clarity.)
*Incantation:*
With yang scouring yin, with qi merging spirit.
Spirit and qi inter-refined, naturally attaining perfection.
Light suffuses the three fields, the four limbs no longer yin.
Nine orifices freely flowing, a hundred joints at peace.
The sun’s qi brightens, the moon’s light gleams pure.
The two forces harmonize, the three luminaries shine as one.
Refining into spirit-yang, to fortify the mortal body.

**Talisman for Forging Yin Demons with Fire to Return Yang**
*Incantation:*
Cinnabar Heaven’s true fire, smelting spirit-yang.
Corpse and po-soul burned to ash, hun-soul strong, body healthy.
Myriad qi harmoniously surging, the body guarded by yang light.
With yang refining yin, yin wanes while yang flourishes.
With yang refining the true, the true is complete and qi returns.
Yang arises in the jade chamber, light penetrating the Hall of Clarity.
Qi returns to the root, steadfast and boundlessly efficacious.

**Talisman for Refining and Rebirth to Transform the Substance**
*Incantation:*
True fire blazing bright, illuminating the spirit chamber.
True qi surging and merging, wisdom’s sun radiant.
True fire refines the form, corpse and evil vanish.
The decaying corpse flees, the seven po-souls scatter.
The dharma-body, the true body, refined and reborn, the substance transformed.
Having received deliverance and refinement, ascending to receive the Jade Decree.

After the water and fire refinement, the recipient is first made to stand by the water and fire pools. The master performs the rituals, guiding them through the water pool, then the fire pool. Once refinement is complete, the corpse and po-soul are purified, the hun-soul and spirit are secure and strong. Thus, one may enjoy a century of blessings and partake in the preemptive merit of the retreat.

The master said: The faithful who receive deliverance shall be granted the talismans and precepts of preemptive cultivation.

Here ends the twentieth scroll of *The Great Law of the Supreme Mystery of the Jade Hall of the Three Heavens*.

*The Great Law of the Supreme Mystery of the Jade Hall of the Three Heavens*
**Title:** *The Great Law of the Supreme Mystery of the Jade Hall of the Three Heavens*
Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty. Thirty scrolls.
**Source Text:** *Daoist Canon of the Zhengtong Era*, *Dongzhen* Section, Methods Category.

**Scroll Twenty-One of *The Great Law of the Supreme Mystery of the Jade Hall of the Three Heavens***
**Chapter Twenty-Three: The Deployment of Generals and Officials**

The master said: The martial generals exist to manifest the intent of killing and conquest. The civil officials exist to preside over their respective duties. Together, they are called *shen* [spirits]. These spirits are not the dark and hidden ghosts of yin, but rather, those who inherit the teachings and cultivate without ceasing, their bones and form uniting with the immortal, their worldly toils utterly exhausted. In the Jade Hall and Golden Palace, none fail to generate spirits. Whatever the heart commands, all become generals and officials. Thus it is said: Heaven and earth unite with me, and I unite with heaven and earth. Spirits and humans assist me, and I assist spirits and humans. Essence and *qi* merge as one, swiftly guarding my true self. This is the meaning.

If one wishes to know the spirits within one’s own body, one must gather the spirit and sit in stillness. Once the celestial vault is settled and human desires are undisturbed, at that very moment, the true generals will appear before you. Thus, when the perfected masters speak of ascending immortals and transcendent numina, they refer to the transformation wrought by the two *qi* within the body.

The Twelve Hundred Official Lords of the Jade Steps of Great Clarity.
The Twelve Thousand Official Lords of the Jade Hall of the Three Heavens.
The Twelve Hundred Officials and Clerks of the Solar Palace of Yang Radiance.
The Twelve Hundred Jade Radiance Youthful Lords of the Lunar Palace.
The Thirty Million Hosts of the Three Yuan Generals.
The Three Hundred Sixty Thousand Hosts of the Seven Kings of the Northern Dipper.
The Two Hundred Thousand Hosts of the Black-Clad Soldiers and Horses of the Northern Emperor.

All the above officials and generals were born of the essence of water and fire at the dawn of the Primordial Kalpa of Vermilion Brightness. In heaven, each day, three spirit-generals follow the body’s *shen*:

The general who never leaves the body, named Ziying.
The general who never leaves the heart, named Xuanpin.
The general who never leaves the spirit, named Changxian.

Their attendant officials and soldiers are innumerable. The above three generals were transformed from the three *qi* prior to the Dragon Han era. The Three Treasures divide into three *qi*, and the three generals descend as spirits into the wondrous gate of the human body—the Gate of the Eyebrows.

Each day, the jade maidens on duty in attendance:
The Jade Maiden of Serene Harmony, Xuanyi.
The Jade Maiden of Longevity, Xianzhi.
The Jade Maiden of Transmitting Words, Daocheng.
The Jade Maiden of the Three Lights, Chiming.
The Jade Maiden of Slaying Demons, Miegao.
The Jade Maiden of Attending Incense, Xinzhen.
The Jade Maiden of Primordial Unity, Yiqi.
The Jade Maiden of Communing with the Real, Zhengxin.

The above eight jade maidens and generals, three at a time, totaling twenty-four, descend into the body’s Purple Chamber of Jasper.

Each day, the thirty-six duty *gongcao* [functionaries]:
The Three-Five *Gongcao*, Guarding the Upright.
The Orthodox Unity *Gongcao*, Balancing *Qi*.
The Descending Perfection *Gongcao*, Rectifying Heaven.
The Slaying Evils *Gongcao*, Beheading Demons.
The Direct Memorial *Gongcao*, Communing with the Mysterious.
The Attending Perfection *Gongcao*, Consolidating the Real.
The Curing Illness *Gongcao* and the Red Talisman *Gongcao*, Single-Minded.
The Yellow Register *Gongcao*, Delivering the Hidden.

The above nine ranks of *gongcao*, four per rank, totaling thirty-six, descend into the body’s Jade Treasury at the hairline.

Each day, the celestial clerks on duty:
The Yin Spirit Central Clerk.
The Yang Spirit Secondary Clerk.
The Left Tiger-Rushing Clerk.
The Right Tiger-Rushing Clerk.
The Left Celestial Physician Clerk.
The Right Celestial Physician Clerk.
The Left Demon-Slaying Clerk.
The Right Demon-Slaying Clerk.
The Black-Clad Demon-Capturing Clerk.
The Embroidered-Clad Demon-Capturing Clerk.
The Red-Clad Demon-Capturing Clerk.
The Cloud-Within Demon-Beheading Clerk.
The Five Directions Demon-Beheading Clerk.
The Three Origins and Four Beginnings Clerk.
The Memorial-Transmitting Clerk.
The Disaster-Dispelling and Calamity-Delivering Clerk.

The above celestial clerks, twenty-four each, encamp at the left and right of the body’s portents.

**Talisman for Deploying Officials**
**Incantation:**
The mudra is formed at the *chou* [second earthly branch] and traced to *wu* [seventh earthly branch] as it issues forth.
Golden chambers merge in chaos, the Jade Hall stands majestic.
Light penetrates the boundless, wondrously pervading the Great Canopy.
The left officials, ascending immortals, clad in radiant light and girded with rosy clouds.
The right officials, transcendent numina, illuminating the mysterious splendor.
The gate of wondrous mystery soars without error.
Communing with the real and the Mysterious Female, this is my immortal family.
Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!

The master said: Deploying officials is the method of moving the spirit. When the heart moves the spirit, the spirit soars without limit—this cannot be fully expressed by mouth or ear, but only grasped by the heart. Thus it is called the method of moving the spirit.

**Talisman for Receiving Officials**
**Incantation:**
The mudra is formed at *wu* and *si* [sixth and seventh earthly branches] and traced to *zi* [first earthly branch] as it issues forth.
Heavenly essence has descended, earthly *po* silently disperses.
The yang spirit is turned back, entering my celestial bridge.
The two *qi* of the immortal and the numinous stretch far across the celestial river.
Light returns to the Mysterious Pass, neither drifting nor scattering.
The eight gates are tranquil, the heavenly *qi* pays homage within.
Longevity and enduring vision, the inner landscape roams free.
Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!

**Jade Maiden Talisman**
**Gongcao Talisman**
**Celestial Clerk Talisman**
**Generals’ Talismans**
**Generals’ Talismans**

**Purple Yang Union of Light Talisman for Summoning the Deities of the Three Realms**

For the talisman on the right: whenever inscribing any talisman, perform the Dipper Step and, in accordance with the method, visualize and circulate the *qi*. When summoning generals, soldiers, or clerks, inscribe their names beneath the talisman. When summoning deities, inscribe the name of the god and call forth by name. When dispatching generals, attach the talisman to the front of the memorial. In all applications, proceed as the intention directs. The practitioner must achieve inner comprehension and guard against attachment.

**Incantation:**
Great Generals of the Celestial Origin, left and right clerks and soldiers,
Six Jia and Six Ding, celestial generals and gods,
Hasten to the altar’s base, tarry not.
By the primordial talismanic command, descend as the Primal Unity.
The Orthodox Unity receives and upholds, empowering me with authority.
Divine marshals of the Dharma Division, gods of the Divine Division, celestial immortals,
Attendant clerks and direct talismans, heed my decree.
Where incense smoke arises, swiftly come before the altar.
By the Most High’s talismanic command, hasten without delay.
Should you disobey, you shall be punished in the Dark Springs.
Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!

**Talisman for Summoning the Twelve Thousand Official Lords of the Jade Hall**

For all exorcisms, deliverances, or subduing acts, summon according to the matter at hand, and the response shall be as an echo.

**Incantation:**
By the Jade Decree of the Mysterious Capital, proclaim to the heavens below.
The altar’s radiance shines, a thousand officials hasten forth.
Clouds race, steeds gallop, descending *qi* connects with the immortals.
As the heart directs, the Three Realms are made manifest.
Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances!

**Method for Gathering the Spirit and Nurturing Within**

The Master said: When the heart wanders and the mind strays, the spirit does not abide in the body. Though one may not yet have heard the supreme Dao, one should at least understand the method for gathering the spirit. The human spirit is inherently numinous; if it is not, desires have muddied it. The spirit is inherently visible; if it is not seen, delusions have veiled it. Those who would follow the teaching must sever all delusions. As for social interactions and worldly affairs, though they may not be entirely eliminated, they should be reduced. Have you not seen how worldly people, ignorant of their true origin, chase after external realms and willingly enter death? For they heedlessly lose their true nature, unaware and unknowing, and do not believe that the body can attain the immortal rank. Those who follow the teaching must act contrary to worldly people, not drifting aimlessly entangled in the web of karma. Thus, Master Huan said: *Abiding in the vastness of the Great Void, I do not mingle with the multitude of beings.* For one must not blend with worldly people as one among them.

If you wish to see your spirit, first stabilize your heart. When your heart is stable, delusions too will stabilize. When delusions are stable, the heart remains ever clear. Throughout the twelve hours, apart from eating, maintain subtle mindfulness, burn incense, regulate the breath, close the eyes and contemplate emptiness. Nurture the breath continuously, embrace the light in silence. Practice this regularly, and delusive thoughts will not arise. The celestial true ones will return to the body, and within stillness, the heart will be seen—the spirit will manifest of itself. Though this method may not yet lead to true attainment, it serves as a means for disciples to gather the spirit, preventing entanglement in deliberate action and fruitless toil. Take heed, do not neglect it.

**Method for Deploying Generals with the Red Talisman**

The Master said: Immortals and Daoists whose yang spirit and *qi* are abundant respond as they are directed, thus they command without commanding, are numinous without being numinous. Worldly Daoists, entangled in the web of the mundane, have not yet attained communion with the immortals and must rely on visualization to seek response. When dispatching generals or circulating the spirit, first close the breath and stabilize the heart. Do not speak to others, nor glance back. Visualize your heart as a red sun, within which resides a certain general, fully robed and capped, the size of a bean. Presently, they ascend upon golden light, growing to about three inches. Then they emerge from the mouth, standing beside the body, gradually expanding to human size.

Then they grow to a hundred *zhang* in height, their majesty awe-inspiring. Dispatch them as the matter requires, and when the talisman is sent forth, it too transforms into the general’s form.

Now, the heart is the convergence of human spirit. Among the five organs, it is called the "Lord," its station most exalted, its function vast. Thus it governs fire and corresponds to the southern direction. The ritual master unites with the heart, hence the name "Red Talisman." Comprehend this union.

**The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Rites, Scroll Twenty-One Concludes**

---

**The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Rites**
*Scripture Title: The Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Rites*
