---
**Volume 24 of the *Supreme Mystery of the Three Heavens and Jade Hall Great Method* Concludes**
**Volume 25 of the *Supreme Mystery of the Three Heavens and Jade Hall Great Method*: The Chapter on Preserving and Controlling the Kalpic Turns**

The Master said: The Great Dao generates the Prenatal; the Prenatal generates the Supreme Ultimate; the Supreme Ultimate generates the Two Modes; the Two Modes generate the Five Phases; the Five Phases divide into the Eight Trigrams; the Eight Trigrams divide into the Nine Palaces. All arise from the mutual generation and conquest of the Five Phases, through which form and *qi* are conceived and nurtured.

Thus, Heaven holds the yang above, and the Three Luminaries shine forth. Earth holds the yin below, and the Five Peaks stand in majesty. Humanity receives the numinous within, and the myriad transformations are complete—thereby establishing the Three Powers and setting the axis of the cosmos.

Yet where there is destiny, there is turn; where there is form, there is kalpa. Inevitably, the kalpa brings calamity, for the Five Phases never cease, and the cycles of generation and destruction, mutual conquest and harm, follow in their wake.

Heaven’s body is pure and void, serene and without trace, enduring myriad kalpas without decay. Earth’s mass is heavy and turbid, ever subject to change. The stars’ benevolence or malevolence cannot escape their contrary courses. When water and fire clash, floods arise. When metal and wood contend, strife ensues. The wind-wheel sustains the earth; the water-*qi* floats the heavens. The Four Great Elements harmonize, and the Five Phases restrain one another. Should any deviate, omens of fortune or misfortune arise, causing Heaven to alter its form above, Earth to shift its form below, stars to entangle, floods and droughts to vie, and warfare to erupt in season.

Such are the destinies, such are the calamities. Therefore, our Great Peace Teaching spreads its teachings below. To preserve Heaven’s enduring existence, one must first preserve and control the kalpic turns. This chapter is established to weave the warp of Heaven and the weft of Earth, safeguarding the state and pacifying the household, delivering people from the disasters of the *yang*-nine, and ushering them into the era of Great Peace—how auspicious!

**Method for Dispelling Comets and Invoking Blessings**

The Master said: This talisman is the pivotal essence of the Red Heaven’s star-subduing art. One must pace the repelling star *Ding*, visualize transforming into the Black Baleful True Lord, then proceed with the flying steps to sever and annihilate.

Before inscribing the talisman, recite the *Supreme Black Edict for Slaying Ghosts* and intone the talisman incantation:

*Incantation:*
*"Om Hum Hum! All spirits bow their heads;
Demons and deviants return to rectitude.
Should any dare act perversely,
Let them be reduced to dust.
Hasten! Upon receipt of this edict, act accordingly."*

**Incantation for Pacing the *Ding***
*"I am the Great One True Lord of the Grotto,
Head crowned with the Seven Stars, pacing the Four Wheels.
Grasping the Dragon Sword, I stand in the *Xun* position,
Then traverse *Li* until reaching *Kun*.
At *Zhen*, *Dui*, and *Gen*, I seal the boundaries—
No demonic vapors may lurk within.
With Yu’s steps and the *Kui Ding* facing *Qian* and *Hai*,
I approach the Celestial Gate to pay homage to the Emperor.
Again, I ride the five-colored ascending clouds,
My true form wrathful, shaking the Gate of Heaven.
Entering the Azure Palace, I fill with generative *qi*,
Then mount the Azure Dragon into *Bing* and *Ding*.
The great radiance of the Red Heaven flames through the Three Realms;
The pure essence of baleful *qi* arrays its blades.
Returning to the *Zhen* position in *Qian*,
I tread the Seven Stars to extinguish the monstrous star.
With one celestial talisman, the baleful star retreats;
With one celestial halberd, Heaven and Earth are cleansed.
Returning, I report my merit to the Sagely Lord.
Om Ma! Summon the heavenly demons!
Hum Hum! Comply with the Emperor’s command!"*

**Talisman for Summoning the Black Baleful True Form**

*Edict Incantation:*
*"Dark Heaven of the North, profound and distant Spirit Lords,
Utterly shatter the demonic hosts!
All baleful stars and malevolent specters,
Be seized and delivered beneath the Dipper’s *Kui* to meet your death!
Om Hum Hum! All spirits bow their heads.
Hasten! Act accordingly!"*

**Method of Practice**
The Master said: When a comet or any baleful star appears as an omen, one should bow and recite the *Prayer for Dispelling Stars* to beseech peace. Next, submit a petition to the Northern Culmen Great Emperor, entreating the suppression of the baleful star. Then, establish an altar and set up a ritual feast, lighting lamps for the Eleven Luminaries and the Northern and Southern Dippers. At dawn, present a memorial, and summon the Black Baleful Great Spirit—who is the Sagely One of the New Moon. The practice must be executed with utmost sincerity.

After the morning audience, recite the *Jade Purity Scripture for Dispelling Disasters and Subduing Demons*. At noon, bow and recite the *Prayer for Dispelling Stars*, visualizing its application in tandem with the *Prayer for Severing Pestilence*. After the audience, recite the *Scripture on Salvation*. At dusk, pace the *Ding*, visualizing the Variegated Sage patrolling the eight directions to execute the punitive method.

For dispelling, both sides remain unharmed, each secure in its place. For conquest, one side must face peril—for this is not the transformative benevolence of the Supreme. Those who inherit this teaching must comprehend this truth.

**Method for Dispelling Fire Disasters**

The Master said: Among the Five Phases and Four Great Elements, water and fire are without sentiment. To control fire, first mobilize the virtue of water. Establish an altar and set up a ritual feast according to the prescribed form:

At dawn, pace the *Ding* of Water Virtue and issue the Water Star talisman command. Hang the banner of the Water Virtue Mysterious Standard. The Daoist assembly recites the *Supreme Yin Dark and Abysmal Incantation*.

At noon, display the *Mysterious Talisman for Suppressing Fire* and the *Talisman for Extinguishing the Might of the Fire Spirit*.

At dusk, bow and recite the *Prayer for Dispelling Fire*, then distribute and affix the talismans.

**Water Star Command for Controlling Fire**

**Supreme Yin Dark Incantation**
*"Supreme Yin, Dark and Abysmal,
Essence of the singular *qi*.
Pure yin coalesces and transforms,
The radiance of yang extinguished in form.
Black *qi* fills the vast expanse;
Red light returns to yin.
Within it dwells a spirit,
Black-bodied, in the Water Court.
Able to extinguish the fire’s ugliness,
The Prenatal Lord.
The abyssal springs churn waves,
*Jia Shen* manifests its brightness.
Roaring and howling, vast and mighty,
Dragons shriek, sand spirits tremble.
The four seas surge in waves,
The *Tu Bo Yi Zhen* arise.
Heavenly fire’s flames cease,
The Emperor commands the weary spirits.
A thousand eyes scatter water;
Poisoned lips unite in terror.
Hasten! As the statutes of the Supreme Yin, Dark and Abysmal, decree!"*

**Water Virtue Banner**
**Five Bushels of Yin Splendor Mysterious Register for Suppressing Fire**

This talisman is inscribed in yellow on black silk, one *zhang* and two *chi* in length, adding one *cun* in a leap year. Display it on the ritual table at dawn, and burn it with the talisman at dusk.

**Method for Exorcising Earthquakes**

The scriptures state: *Heaven moves while earth remains still.*
For heaven revolves above and earth rests below—this is the constant principle of Yin and Yang.
If earth assumes the movement of heaven and trembles, it is because Yin and Yang have lost their order.
This method should be employed to exorcise such calamities.

**Procedure for Conducting the Ritual:**
First, construct an altar and set up a sacrifice to the Ninefold August Lords.
Use a shared altar for the Three Realms.
As prescribed: At dawn, present the Jade Tablet for Pacifying the Spirits and burn it in the southwest.
Prepare records for each officiant, and have the Daoist assembly recite the *Vermilion Script of Jade Characters*.
At noon, recite the *Vermilion Script of Jade Characters* again, and bury the Jade Tablet for Suppressing *Kun* in the earth.
Conclude by prostrating before the *Chapter on Earthquakes* and dispersing the altar.

**Method for Exorcising Solar Eclipses**

The master says: *The sun is the symbol of the ruler and also the symbol of the Middle Kingdom.*
When the Great Yang is at its zenith, it illuminates the lands below,
Causing all under heaven to turn like sunflowers and bow like grass, revering the celestial light.
If the sun is eclipsed, it signifies the loss of virtue in Yang’s radiance, resulting in disaster and misfortune.
This method should be employed to suppress and exorcise, praying for blessings and protection.

**Ritual for Dispelling Locust Plagues**

The master says: The calamity of locusts arises when winter snow fails to fall, and yin breeds monstrosities. Borne by the fire of the southern direction, they sprout wings and become insects, thus able to devour seedlings and ruin crops. For the seeds of these pests lie everywhere. A single encounter with the qi of snow drives them three *chi* into the earth. Within one year, three encounters with snow’s qi bury them nine *chi* deep. In two years, two *zhang*. But if snow fails for a year, they emerge three *chi* from the ground. Should snow remain absent for three consecutive years, the accumulated plague of locusts will manifest.

The method of suppression and exorcism: Erect an altar and set up the offering ritual as prescribed. At dawn, dispatch a memorial to the Spirit Who Captures Locusts. Next, memorialize the City God and the Earth God, commanding them to summon winds to blow the locusts into clusters. The talisman leads the way. At noon, perform the memorial ritual as prescribed. At dusk, recite the incantation according to the method.

**Southern Vermilion Phoenix, Flame Clouds.**

**Ritual for Dispelling Drought**

The master says: When prolonged drought persists despite prayers, only those who approach with utmost sincerity, having widely aroused boundless compassion and received petitions for rain, may inscribe and employ the talisman. First, submit memorials to the Three Heavenly Gates, to the Heavenly Master’s court, and file reports to the Three Officials, the River and Sea Bureaus, the Tai Mountain Prefecture, the Dragon Lords of the Four Waterways and Five Lakes, the Immortals of the Grotto-Heavens of Famous Mountains, the Wind Earl and Rain Master, and the Earth God. Only then proceed with pacing the altar and reciting the incantation. Perform the three-day ritual upon the altar as prescribed. If rain falls sufficiently, do not cast the talisman further. If insufficient, next employ an iron plaque, one *chi* and two *cun* in length, two *cun* and four *fen* in width, inscribed with the seal-script as prescribed:

**Tai Shang Talisman for Driving Rain**
**Iron Charter for Overturning the Sea to Bring Rain**

Use an iron charter, two *cun* and four *fen* in width, two *chi* and four *cun* in length, inscribed in vermilion. Seal it in a lined pouch and cast it into the dragon’s grotto. Once rain has fallen sufficiently, retrieve it as before. Perform the three-day ritual upon the altar and issue the oral decree.

The Most High Lord Lao resides upon the ninefold heavens, amidst ten thousand layers of dense clouds, riding a qilin with a decree. He commands the Great Perfected King Qiao Ma Yi of the lower realm and the Dragon King to dispatch the lunar-attendant, solar-attendant, and hourly-attendant dragon officials to bring forth rain. Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and decrees of the Later Sage Lord Lao.

This oral decree issues from the golden mouth of the Most High. When establishing the altar, position the Four Attendant Deities at the four corners:
- **Southwest:** Fire Radiance Flowing Essence Lord
- **Southeast:** Jade Thunder Luminous Master Lord
- **Northwest:** Void Essence Great Hua Lord
- **Northeast:** Cavern Yang Mysterious Spirit Lord

These four deities are the essence of Heavenly Unity and the ancestors of the dragon spirits.

**Incantation:**
Protect the Luminous Consort, Pure Flower Gold,
Celestial Heroes, Dipper Stalwarts, Mysterious Spirits.
The Primordial Lady of Grand Unity commands the water troops,
Penglai Envoys, Masters of the Water Court.
Weak Waters gleam clear without the slightest turbidity,
Governing seas and rivers, overturning the Four Seas.

Within lies the Cavern Yang Mysterious Spirit,
Jade Thunder’s Luminous Master swiftly raises his voice.
Mighty rides the Great Hua Celestial Steed,
Flowing Essence and Jade Radiance rush to the Fire Bell.
Black clouds billow as the sea’s *qi* ascends,
Pouring down upon the hundred rivers, rain like cords.
A span of moisture swells to fullness,
The Rain Master and his retinue array the stellar ranks.
Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and decrees.

After performing the three-period ritual upon the altar, sprinkle water. Cast the iron-plaque talisman and pace the *gang*.

Proceed as in the rain-praying ritual, reciting the incantation for three days. At dawn, dispatch the talisman and command; at noon, hasten the clearing.

**Three-Five Pacing the Gang Method**
The master says: Pacing the *gang* is the method for strengthening the body and activating *qi*, the formula for stabilizing the hun and subduing the po.

The "three" in "three-five" refers in the Dao to the Three *Qi*, in heaven to the Three Heavens, in radiance to the Three Lights, in spirits to the Three Primes, and in humans to the Three Hun. The "five" refers in the Dao to the Five Elders, in heaven to the Five Phases, in celestial bodies to the Five Stars, and in humans to the Five Viscera.

The ancestral master says: The Three *Qi* are the essence of the Three Lights, and the Three Lights are the masters of spirit and essence. The Five Phases are the ancestors of the Five Stars, and the Five Phases are the thieves that harm the body. Thus, if the practitioner can cultivate and ascend to perfection, they cause the Three Lights to return to the Three *Qi* and the Five Phases to return to the Five Powers. The Three Hun become the Three Lights, the Five Viscera become the Five *Qi*, the Five *Qi* return to the Three *Qi*, and the Three *Qi* merge into the One *Qi*, naturally attaining perfection. Hence, it is said: Humans thereby attain longevity. Those who cannot cultivate cause the Three Lights to become the Three Corpses, the Three Corpses to become the Three Paths; the Five *Qi* become the Five Phases, and the Five Phases become the Five Sufferings. These are the Eight Difficulties for humans—this is the meaning of "three-five."

*Gang* means "guiding principle." Arranging the Dipper to pace is to pull the guiding principle and operate the mechanism, hence the name *gang*. It is also said: *Gang* is yang. The natural yang within pacing subdues yin demons, so the Dipper’s stars ride their light upon the Great Crimson Heaven, hence the name *gang*.

The Celestial Master of old said: The Northern Dipper is the Central Dipper. The Central Dipper’s nine stars transform into the Nine Spirit Pacings—this is called the Stellar *Gang*. Thus, one symbolizes the Supreme Ultimate, two symbolize heaven and earth, three symbolize the Three Lights, four symbolize the Four Seasons, five symbolize the Five Phases, six symbolize the Six Pitch Pipes, seven symbolize the Seven Stars, eight symbolize the Eight Trigrams, and nine symbolize the Nine Spirits.

However, the Nine Spirits’ transmission has long been interrupted, and its formula lost. Thus, I now establish the diagram, taking the Nine Spirit Ancestral *Gang* as its head. This *gang* is the ancestor of pacing methods, the origin of Yu’s pacing, and by pacing it repeatedly, there is nothing it cannot accomplish. The so-called "Huoluo Dipper" of recent times traces its source to this.

The pacing method need not be overly complex; if the heart comprehends the Nine Stars, the feet tread the Nine Spirits, and the body embodies the Nine *Qi*, one will naturally attain mastery. Thus, the methods transmitted in the present age are mostly erroneous, and I now specially simplify and demonstrate the wondrous essence of non-complexity.

**Prostrating to Submit Petitions and Breaking the Gang Pacing the Void Method**
**Transcending the Three Realms Pacing the Void Gang Method**

**The Daoist Gang of the Celestial Immortal Generals**
**The Gang for Audience with Heaven and Memorial Submission**
**The Gang for Subduing Demons and Quelling Spirits**
**The Three Terraces Gang**

The above *gang* methods are all ancestral to the various arts. They involve pacing but no incantations; one holds the intention without clinging to the form. In the teachings of the Great Peace, the *Yu’s Pacing* was transmitted anew, becoming the *Gang for Regulating the Five Phases, Cultivating the Body, and Subduing Demons*.

**The Twenty-Fifth Scroll of the Supreme Mystery-Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method’s Essential Principles Concludes**
**The Twenty-Ninth Scroll of the Supreme Mystery-Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method**

**Chapter Thirty-Five: Invoking the True and Delivering from Calamity**

The Master said:
To *invoke the true* is to perform the *Dipper Memorial Rite*. The Dipper governs the throat and tongue of Heaven; all matters of human fortune and misfortune, prosperity and adversity, longevity and premature death, are determined by it. Thus, when Heaven sends down reprimands, when ghosts below lodge false accusations, when ancestral spirits summon litigation, or when the deceased implicate the living—any of these occurrences bring misfortune in their wake. The severity of the affliction corresponds to the gravity of the offense. Without practicing the urgent memorial method to effect resonance, even if one were to amass incense into mountains or burn offerings for generations, one could not achieve communion or response.

Thus, the adage states: *One’s nature is like fire; the method is like sulfur—touch them, and they ignite.* The same principle applies here. Though Dipper rites are numerous, the initial steps for beginners are not easily distinguished. With minds cluttered and intentions scattered, how can one attain clarity? Therefore, I now specially present the *Urgent Memorial Secret Petition* within this chapter. Perform it with sincerity, and the true will respond to Heaven.

In all matters of invoking the Dipper and beseeching the true, authority lies with the *Two Envoys of the Striking Bell*. These two deities are solely responsible for inspecting the purity of the ritual altar. If one is not devout, these spirits will report it, and the celestial perfected will not descend. They also oversee human fortune and misfortune, life and death, and are especially attended by the *Nine August Ladies, Inner Consorts, and Jade Maidens* who present the memorials. If these deities do not descend, the petitions will not reach their destination, and all ritual preparations will be in vain. Furthermore, the transmission of the memorial to the *Mysterious Bureau* to request the descent of gracious decrees is the purview of the *Four Direct Envoys, Nine August Celestial Officers, Embroidered-Robed Envoys, and Messengers of Communication*. If they do not descend, the true sincerity will not be conveyed; if the *Lifting Bell* does not descend, the Celestial Perfected will remain unaware, and all offerings of incense and flowers will be wasted, unable to elicit a response.

Moreover, if the practitioner has violated taboos of impurity, consumed meat or pungent foods, harbored impure thoughts, or maintained an unclean body, even if the true scribes are summoned, they will not descend. The *Four Bureaus* will record the transgressions, and the resulting offenses will be immeasurable. Be cautious.

When invoking the Dipper, one must not approach slaughterhouses, taverns, rowdy markets, or licentious chambers. The best locations are empty halls, grand temples, or official Daoist abbeys. Avoid disturbances and keep away from wailing. If monks, nuns, coffins, chickens, dogs, cats, or individuals in mourning attire (wearing white cloth) enter the altar space, the deities will neither descend nor respond.

When the practitioner enters the state of *storing and circulating*, if one does not *summon the qi*, the true will not respond; if one does not *ingest the talisman*, the body will not become numinous; if one does not *concentrate on the deities*, the true will not descend. One must achieve the union of *qi* and spirit, the resonance of inner sincerity, so that the response is swift and luminous, as if engaging in conversation.

In the Tang dynasty, there was a Minister of Waterworks named Zhang Shuo, who resided by the Xiao River. His nine-year-old son was unable to speak. Later, he prayed at the shrine of Zhang, the Waterworks Minister (who was also Zhang, the Judge of the Underworld), and offered sacrifices to the deity of Bian Mountain. Suddenly, the deity descended and spoke: *"When your son was born, he offended the Dipper Bureau. You must urgently memorialize it."* The deity had once served the Dipper and possessed a secret method, which was extremely simple. He transmitted it to Zhang Shuo, who later rose to the position of Prime Minister. This secret method was buried atop the great peak of Juqu. Now that the Great Teaching is flourishing, this method has been revealed to the world. Practitioners should keep it confidential.

To first memorialize the Dipper, prepare four clean mats, seven plates woven from artemisia flowers (each the size of a small dish), seven cups of pure tea, seven bowls of jujube broth, seven oil cakes, seven offerings of fruit, seven incense burners, and seven lamps. Face north and make the offerings. The practitioner should advance on their knees, bowing seven times to each star, and secretly pray for the matter at hand. Submit the urgent memorial petition and burn it in the incense burner with a blazing fire.

Next, the practitioner enters the chamber, visualizes, and bows nine times. Imagine the five viscera emitting five-colored *qi*, forming a golden bridge that connects to the celestial realm. Envision the seven palaces of the Dipper Bureau as jade halls with golden towers. After a long while, see the *Embroidered-Robed Envoy* leading you across the bridge. Gradually, you will perceive a path of purple clouds, where the *Nine August Officials* in vermilion robes with square collars and nine-tiered crowns guide you to ascend and enter the palace of your natal star to present your petition. You will see only golden light, too radiant to gaze upon directly. Once the petition is presented, if you see a red light, it signifies that your request has been granted. Return by the same path and enter the *Mysterious Gate*. After a long while, swallow your saliva, click your teeth, and withdraw.

**Burning the Altar Talisman**
Burn the talisman and recite the incantation, visualizing the first layer of the jade platform rising from the earth.

**Incantation:**
*Clear and numinous, true qi sweeps away the miasma.*
*Empty mystery’s true image: the first layer of the jade platform.*
*Divine qi descends in response; we bow to the exalted ones.*

**Incantation:**
*The Great Void is without form; the cloud paths are clear and level.*
*The second layer of the jade altar forms as the heart desires.*
*Demonic miasma is stilled; the human realm is at peace.*

**Incantation:**
*As the true light descends, the third layer of the jade platform appears.*
*The empty mystery takes form: the gate of all wonders.*
*Invite the immortals—they arrive; summon the sages—they attend.*
*Sincerity moves the heart; the Dipper’s numen descends.*

Burn the three flying talismans, visualizing the three-tiered jade altar rising, purple clouds ascending, and golden light in the void connecting to the Dipper’s extremity.

**Next, burn the Demon-Quelling Talisman**
Write it in vermilion and send it flying. Recite the *Great Slaying Text*, sprinkle water to the four directions, and recite the incantation.

**Incantation:**
*Supreme purity of the Dao, dispatching the celestial soldiers.*
*Driving dragons and riding tigers, casting fire and ringing bells.*
*Cloud paths are swept clean; demonic hordes are revealed.*
*True fire strikes first; halberds and polearms punish behind.*
*Dare any disobey? Sever their heads and annihilate their forms.*

Ghosts and demons fall silent; welcome the descent of the exalted perfected.
Burn the Ascending Report Talisman and the Slaying Text, write in vermilion, and send two flying. Visualize *Vajra* descending, then ascending, then descending again, and bow twice.

**Incantation:**
*The heavens’ qi is pure; it guards the adept’s flying spirit.*
*What is prayed for is granted; the adept’s numen is made manifest.*
*The two perfected ascend with the report, swiftly fulfilling the heart’s desire.*

Visualize the High Perfected’s Descent-to-Earth Talisman.
Form the Dipper mudra, send seven flying, all written in vermilion.
Then burn the Urgent Petition.

**Incantation:**
*The Jade Emperor bestows upon me the right to invoke the perfected.*
*On this auspicious day, the incense of my heart ascends.*
*The seven perfected descend, curing illness and expelling spirits.*
*They bring blessings and dissolve calamities, granting peace and safety.*

**The Master says:**
When worldly people suffer from illness or hardship, they have no time to present formal memorials. Since matters are urgent, the method of the Urgent Petition is employed—simple and direct, seeking the perfected is sufficient.
Use a sheet of light yellow paper, one foot and two inches long, six inches high. Write the adept’s title and position in detail, stating the matter clearly, in no more than one hundred characters, all in vermilion.
When finished, fold it eight times, then four times, seal the corners, and inscribe only: *"Your humble servant [Name] respectfully submits and seals."*
Dispatch the Dipper’s Direct-Service Merit Officer to transmit it in the fast.
Burn it in a censer of blazing incense, ensuring thick smoke but no flame. While visualizing, bow, and once the smoke dissipates, close the altar.

**Format for the Urgent Petition:**
Write according to the prescribed form, fold it, then fold it into four sections. Burn it in a censer of blazing incense, and a response will arrive immediately.

*"Your humble servant [Name], on behalf of [Person] of [Place], born on the [Year, Month, Day, Hour], now beseeches the Imperial Perfected for [Matter], to resolve grievances, harmonize fate, and swiftly dispel calamities, granting peace and safety.
In haste, I submit this urgent petition to the Jade Palace beneath the Northern Dipper’s [Star] Constellation, humbly imploring Your decree for immediate action. I await the response, prostrate before the altar."*

**The Master says:**
This method is Zhang Shuibu’s *Urgent Petition to the Teapot Altar of the Dipper*, simple and ancient, neither cumbersome nor crude, with the swiftest response. It resembles the talismanic commands in the *Prohibitions Canon* but differs in minor ways.
The adept may adopt it without seeking excess. When the time is right, the *Prohibitions Canon* will ultimately be their proper guide.

Here ends *The Supreme Mystery of the Three Heavens: Jade Hall Great Method*, Scroll Twenty-Nine.
*[Note: Previous scroll referenced is Twenty-Seven.]*

**The Ascent and Descent of the Two Luminaries**

**The Master says:**
The Jade Hall takes the *High Ascent to the Sun and Moon* as its ancestral method. By extension, it may be applied to others to cure illness and expel evil. Cultivated within oneself, it enables communion with the perfected and attainment of immortality. Yet the *High Ascent* is not easily practiced; one must first advance through the ranks to receive and preserve it.

Ascent signifies the meaning of *ascent* [to the luminaries], while descent signifies its application to others and to oneself. Heaven and earth mark day and night by the sun and moon, and all transformations of yin and yang, cold and heat, arise from them. Thus, nothing moves heaven and earth or stirs ghosts and spirits more than these.

**Method for Ingesting Sun and Moon Light on Dawn and Full Moon Days**
At sunrise on the first day of the lunar month, the adept sits facing east, visualizing the sunlight nine feet before them. The sun has nine rays, and within them, five-colored luminous *qi* descends into the adept’s mouth, entering the five viscera, radiant as a crimson sun. Recite the incantation:
> *Oṃ va-dri-ra guṇa-sūri svāhā.*
> Five Emperors of the Sun, true *qi* descend swiftly.
> Pierce my abdomen, enter my viscera, *qi* surging, *qi* strengthening.

Then inhale the *qi* nine times, swallowing nine times, until warmth is felt within the abdomen. Perform this thrice. After a year of practice, the *qi* will be robust and the spirit vigorous; when deploying talismans or consecrated water, responses will arise naturally.

At moonrise on the full moon, the adept sits facing east, visualizing the moonlight nine feet before them. The moon has ten rays, and within them, five-colored luminous *qi* descends into the adept’s mouth, entering the five viscera, luminous as the full moon. Recite the incantation:
> *Oṃ va-candra ra □-ra svāhā.*
> August Sovereign of the Moon, Five Perfected Ladies,
> True *qi* descends, piercing my body’s court.
> Preserve my immortal life, ten thousand years unshaken.

Then inhale the *qi* nine times, swallowing nine times, until warmth is felt within the abdomen. Perform this thrice. After a year of practice, the *qi* will be pure and the body numinous; when treating illness or subduing malevolent spirits, responses will arise naturally.

**External Ascent to the Two Luminaries**
On a quiet night, the adept enters a chamber and sits in stillness, banishing thoughts and emptying the mind. They visualize crimson *qi* emerging from their heart, coalescing into a cloud chariot. Their body ascends the chariot, rising gently to the Solar Palace, where they behold the Solar Emperor bestowing the *Talisman of the Sun’s Nurturing Perfection*. After ingesting it, they descend with the Emperor into the *Niwan* [palace], lingering until form is forgotten. They then knock their teeth, swallow saliva, and withdraw.

After completing the ascent to the sun, the adept again visualizes white *qi* emerging from their kidneys, ascending from the crown to form a cloud chariot. Their body ascends the chariot, rising gently to the Lunar Palace, where they behold the August Lady of the Moon bestowing the *Talisman of the Moon’s Nurturing Perfection*. After ingesting it, they descend with the Lady into the *Niwan*, lingering until form is forgotten. They then knock their teeth, swallow saliva, and withdraw.

This Way of the Two Luminaries should be practiced daily in moments of leisure, diligently and consistently. Over time, wondrous and extraordinary responses will arise, beyond full description.

**Method for Inscribing Talismans and Infusing the Brush**

Whenever the adept wishes to inscribe the talismans of the Three Luminaries, they must first silently recite the incantation of the Lord of the Sun one thousand two hundred times. The incantation of the Lady of the Moon is to be recited likewise.

Next, the adept forms the mudra of the Lord of the Sun, visualizing the sun before their face. From within the sun, five-colored *qi* emerges, infusing the brush. The incantation is recited twelve times, and twelve breaths of *qi* are drawn into the brush. The incantation reads:

*"True light of the Great Yang,
Nine rays of solar fire.
Flow down to the brush’s tip,
Inscribe the talisman’s turning script.
Longevity and enduring vision,
Dispelling all inauspicious omens."*

Next, the adept forms the mudra of the Lady of the Moon, visualizing the moon before their face. From within the moon, five-colored *qi* emerges, infusing the brush. The incantation is recited twelve times, and twelve breaths of *qi* are drawn into the brush. The incantation reads:

*"True brightness of the Great Yin,
True water purifies form.
True light enters the brush,
Infusing the talisman with reality.
Expelling filth and banishing evil,
Preserving spirit and protecting the body."*

Upon completion, the adept may inscribe the talisman as they wish. If inscribing the talisman of the Three Luminaries, they further form the *Ding* mudra with the second finger of the left hand. The incantation is recited:

*"Oṃ gaṃ da li svāhā."*

Thirty-six times, with each recitation, the adept draws in *qi* and exhales upon the brush before inscribing the talisman. After visualizing the ascent of the sun and moon, they return to the altar and ingest the mudras of the *Talismans of the Sun’s and Moon’s Nurturing Perfection*.

**Talisman of the Sun’s Nurturing Perfection**
The *Talisman of the Sun’s Nurturing Perfection* is inscribed in cinnabar on light yellow paper, then burned and taken in jujube decoction. While ingesting, the adept recites the incantation.

**Talisman of the Moon’s Nurturing Perfection**
The *Talisman of the Moon’s Nurturing Perfection* is inscribed in ink on light yellow paper, then burned and taken in jujube decoction. While ingesting, the adept recites the incantation.

**Methods for Expelling, Restraining, and Subduing**

The Master said: Those born in the *xia-yuan* *jia-zi* year are of meager fortune and scant virtue; blessings shun them, yet malevolent spirits, demons, and baleful influences readily assail them. Thus misfortune befalls their households, or they themselves encounter grotesqueries and suffer untimely or unjust deaths. Therefore, the Most High revealed the *Decree of Expulsion* and established the *Methods of Restraint and Subduing*, that demons might not trespass, and humankind ascend to longevity and well-being—how splendid indeed!

Yet once these teachings emerged and spread through the ages, hearsay and misinterpretation obscured the true and gave rise to the false, fracturing the orthodox methods. Thus, their application lost efficacy, and expelling demons yielded no response. Fragments of texts and broken talismans left the profound and wondrous untransmitted, a failing of those who uphold and transmit the methods.

This foundational stage, then, is not meant to establish distinctions among talismans or degrees of transmission. Worldly folk, fickle in their pursuits, begin but do not persist, treating sacred texts with levity, as mere child’s play. Thus, this initial stage is set to gauge the aspirant’s capacity for the Dao. If one proves steadfast in purpose, the transmission of the orthodox lineage and the continuation of the great teaching truly commence here—how could one not proceed with utmost care?

The Master said: This foundational stage of *Methods for Expelling, Restraining, and Subduing* does not imply concealment or omission. These methods, transmitted by the Master’s decree, are the simplest to practice and the most readily efficacious. Yet one must reflect: such encounters are not easily come by, and their execution is no small feat. Among these secrets are those unrecorded in the canonical texts; here they are first recorded to instruct the novice—take heed.

The Master said: Ghostly *qi* prevails in the lands south of the Yangtze, most densely in the Hundred Yue regions, where customs revere spirits and believe in perverse forces. Thus, people invite chaos, attracting malevolent influences to assail and afflict them. The benighted, unaware of their own harm, instead place their faith in these forces, and those poisoned by them grovel in servitude, blind to their plight. Such is the unchecked rampancy of ghostly *qi*, rising to offend the celestial *qi* of the clouds and heavens, its foul vapors violating heaven and earth. The Perfected Ones grow wrathful and no longer descend, while demons rejoice in their unchallenged dominance. Thus, in the world, private altars and temples—whether in monasteries or shrines—abound with false spirits masquerading as gods. Without the great methods to uphold the true teaching, how can these malevolent forces be easily eradicated?

The Master’s instruction for the initial signs of this stage states: In treating afflictions, when confronting great afflictions, one must pity the lesser. What are the great afflictions? They are the factions of spirit temples, the entities clinging to mountains and forests, the usurpers of monastic altars—these are the great afflictions. Their roots extend a thousand *li*, their lairs connect to the four directions, harming the innocent and ensnaring the dead into their ranks. Over time, their strong spirits and wayward souls occupy every place, demanding blood sacrifices and spreading poison to harm the people, ceaselessly. Thus, to treat one affliction is to provoke the multitude. If the multitude, thwarted in their demands, face execution, the response echoes from the four directions and a thousand *li*, rallying their followers and depleting their ranks to battle the true method. If the novice harbors even a trace of hesitation, the demonic horde seizes the advantage, the true method fails, and the people suffer—how lamentable!

The so-called lesser afflictions are but wandering souls; one should pity their lingering state and enable their deliverance. To treat lesser afflictions with ease while struggling against the great is to lose sight of the Most High’s original intent in establishing these methods.

**Talisman for Subduing the Factions of Great Afflictions**
*Jade Clarity Highest Emperor, Supreme Clarity Great Emperor, Grand Clarity Great Emperor, Jade Sovereign Emperor, Supreme Limit of the Great Lofty Jade Clarity, Upper Prime General, Middle Prime General, Lower Prime General—seize, bind, and execute all wayward ghosts and spirits. Upper Terrace of Void Essence, Middle Terrace of Sixfold Purity, Lower Terrace of Crooked Life—wherever you arrive, bestow mighty numen. Eight Execution Generals, Four Execution Spirit Lords, Execution Ghosts, Celestial Soldiers—execute all wayward and malevolent ghosts and spirits. Open the Gate of Heaven, Close the Door of Earth, Bar the Human Gate, Block the Ghostly Path. Left Celestial Stem, Right River Demon—execute demonic ghosts, thunderous roars. Twenty-Eight Constellations, Level Heaven General, Level Earth General—lead the celestial soldiers to capture ghosts and spirits, annihilate demonic essences.*

**Incantation for the Talisman**
The Emperor issues the talisman, the celestial decree is majestic.
Heavenly Penumbra, Black Executioner, Dark Warrior—guard the heavens.
Commanding the celestial soldiers, the celestial stalwarts follow.
Fire formations spread in four directions, thunder and wind roar.
Search the void, inspect the earth, overturn mountains and rivers.
Dare any rebellious ghost charge before me?
The stem fire incinerates, flames and smoke fly.
Severed without mercy, eternally imprisoned in the dark springs.
The Emperor’s decree is issued, wind and fire swiftly transmit.
I act by the authority of the Northern Culmen Purple Tenuity Great Emperor.

For this talisman, visualize the Great Emperor of the Northern Culmen above your head, the Four Saints arrayed at the sides, black clouds filling the four voids, weapons and armor teeming. The novice receives this talisman from the Northern Emperor, swallows it, and firelight bursts forth in all directions, thunder resounds. Then, open your eyes and inscribe the talisman on a full sheet of yellow paper with ground cinnabar, facing north. This talisman bears the Emperor’s ultimate punishment; when affixed to the household courtyard, ghosts and spirits within the four directions are expelled nine *li* beyond. If burned at a haunted site, the celestial generals will manifest their might, sweeping and purging an area thirty *li* in all directions to stillness. When inscribing the talisman, maintain utmost sincerity: enter the chamber, silently present your petition, sit in stillness, and then proceed.

**Great Execution Text, Northern *Qi***
*Three Officials’ General Talisman for Searching Out and Expelling Evil*
Upper Prime Heavenly Official—executes spirits,
Middle Prime Earthly Official—executes ghosts,
Lower Prime Water Official—executes essences.
Three Primes, Unicorn Envoys—center.

Celestial Stem Great Sage Gouchen, Yellow Court—center.
*Zi-Wu-Mao-You*—center.
Thunder Duke, Fierce Officer Xin Hanchen—body rides a ten-thousand-*zhang* flying serpent, mouth spewing firelight a myriad *li* to burn.
Execute! Fifteen kinds of ghosts in the world—decapitated, dismembered, improperly deceased—all seized and bound beneath the Demon Stem.
Swiftly seize, Zheng Zixin!
Swiftly bind, Guan Zhongxin!
Swiftly capture, Mao Dangxin!
*Wu*—decapitated, blood-dripping general Liu Yan,
Head-lifting, blood-dripping general Liu Zhong,
Head-lifting deputy general Zhang Ziming—execute!

Mighty Celestial Stalwart Ghost-Binding General Lu Jiquan,
Mighty Celestial Stalwart Ghost-Shackling General Deng Yangguang,
Mighty Celestial Stalwart Ghost-Interrogating General Dou Xingwen—*Zi-Wu-Mao-You*.
Fire bells, wind swift—heaven and earth glow crimson, three crows soar within, blazing brilliantly to incinerate ghosts to ash, refine them to liquid.
Heavenly fire, earthly fire, Samādhi true fire—swiftly seize and execute, Zhu Ling!
By the Jade Sovereign Emperor’s decree—fire, swiftly execute ghosts!
By the Northern Culmen Great Emperor’s decree—fire, swiftly execute ghosts!
Execute! *Zi-Wu-Dou*!

The right talisman is called the "Three Officials’ Eighteen Generals’ Retributive Talisman." For all manner of malevolent ghosts and spirits possessing the body, causing madness, or manifesting various demonic anomalies to harm the living, it is fitting to inscribe this talisman. Use gold paper and spirit horses, and at midnight, burn it in the central courtyard. Also inscribe this talisman and fumigate the afflicted one’s bed curtains, chambers, and rooms with its smoke, or burn it to ashes. When performed with utmost sincerity, extraordinary retribution shall follow.

**Talisman for Expelling Demonic Curses and Devouring Ghosts**
*Upper Clarity, Northern Culmen, Purple Tenuity Great Emperor*
*Heavenly Pen Marshal and the Thirty-Six Generals descend into the talisman to execute all lawless ghosts and spirits*
*Swiftly, by the Northern Culmen Great Emperor’s decree!*

*(Above)* Upper Realm’s Great General of Devouring Demons and Consuming Ghosts, Zhong Jian
*(Below)* Lower Realm’s Great General of Devouring Demons and Consuming Ghosts, Xu Guangfu
*Left sun, right moon—illuminate and vanquish demons and fiends*
*Open the Gate of Heaven, close the Door of Earth, preserve the Gate of Man, block the Path of Ghosts*
*□□□□□□□*
*Devouring demons, consuming ghosts—fangs sharp, blades keen*
*Heavenly Pen Mantra Seal*
*Heaven-Slaying Divine Lord, Earth-Slaying Divine Lord, Year-Slaying Divine Lord, Month-Slaying Divine Lord, Day-Slaying Divine Lord, Hour-Slaying Divine Lord—slay all lawless ghosts and demons!*
*Heaven rejects them, Earth bears them not—swiftly!*
*Five Directions’ malevolent ghosts—devour, consume, obliterate, and eradicate!*

This talisman follows the Northern Emperor’s method, to be inscribed while facing the Dipper’s *Gang*. It may be ingested, whereby the ghosts and demons within the body shall be devoured and annihilated. If used for suppression and posting, ghosts and demons shall see it and be consumed without remainder. This talisman is the Heavenly Pen Marshal’s great and mighty *virtue/power*—the method of devouring demons and consuming ghosts.

*Thus concludes the twenty-seventh scroll of the* Supreme Mystery-Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method.

*Compiled by Lu Shizhong of the Song Dynasty*

To ascend and pay homage to the Supreme Origin.

Ascend to assume their governance above.

The Master says: When the solemnity of the Mysterious Altar is fully arrayed, reverence arises within, and august majesty manifests without. Thus, wayward thoughts do not arise, and true mindfulness abides. For those who study the lower mysteries, by this means they may commune with the loftiest Perfected and reach the hidden numinous—how could its benefit be small?

Altar design includes red banners.

**Eastern Heaven-Pacifying Azure Numinous Jade Talisman**

Soaring high to the Crimson Wheel of Fire.

The Master says: These Five Directions’ Heaven-Pacifying Jade Talismanic Feathered Scripts may be employed above to pacify and secure the state, uphold auspicious fortune; below to cultivate nature and destiny, dispel demons and expel evil, succor the dying and deliver the living—none are beyond their use. These are the inner tones of the Five Emperors, not the common words of the world.

**General Knocking of the Teeth**
Three knocks, visualize the Three Responsive Jade Realms.
Hair bristles in dense array, yang radiance bursts forth,
Penetrating and resonating in the four directions.
This is called the wondrous art of communion with the real.

The Master says: Knocking the teeth gathers the yang spirits within the body, yet their uses differ. When beseeching the real and invoking the sacred, communicating with heaven and moving earth, it is called "sounding the Dharma Drum." The Dharma Drum consists of the four front teeth above and below, making eight teeth in total. Three knocks yield twenty-four resonances. The left teeth are called the Golden Bell; the right teeth, the Jade Chime. Know their wondrous efficacy. When the body is free of illness, this is called the True Person. Sounding the Dharma Drum gathers my yang spirits, ascending to commune with the Jade Palace, paying homage to the lofty venerables. All demons bow their heads, and eternal life is forever attained.

**Jade Staircase Curtain-Raising Heaven-Ascending True Talisman**
Execute the Jade Clarity mudra, drawing the qi of the Heavenly Gate.
Brush aside the curtain’s veil, visualize the Great Void’s primordial chaos—no decree is visible.
Then employ the second talisman.
*Incantation:*
The Dao is wondrous yet formless,
Heaven is quiescent, soundless.
Scattered, it is not lost;
Gathered, it does not form.
The distant void bears an image,
The indistinct holds true essence.
Congealed into an auspicious sign,
The image becomes real.
May the Jade Portal open,
That I may pay homage to the lofty venerables.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances!*

**Jade Capital’s Empty Mystery Vision-Form Talisman**
Execute the Jade Clarity mudra, envision the formless world of the Great Void as lustrous jade, without distance or height, all of one hue. Within it, a luminous point shines like a millet grain, its interior and exterior crystalline. Visualize the Primordial Beginning’s Celestial Venerable within, then employ the third talisman.
*Incantation:*
The qi of the Great Beginning,
Spontaneous and non-actional.
The Void Origin bears an image,
Suspended in the empty mystery.
Encompassing the ten thousand beings,
Nurturing and transforming immortals and gods.
Seen yet unseen,
Heard yet untransmitted.
Before and after indistinguishable,
Mystery within mystery.
May the numinous creation open,
That I may personally worship the Mysterious Origin.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances!*

**Audience with the Origin’s Natural Secret Talisman**
Execute the Jade Clarity mudra, visualize the curtain’s front as a true pearl’s mouth, drawing the Dao’s hosts and transforming multitudes of perfected beings to enter. After a long while, see only a golden-hued world, nothing else.
*Incantation:*
The jeweled curtain is drawn,
The jade countenance’s light returns.
Enter the treasure pearl,
Listen to the Dharma’s lingering.
The spirit’s mind is serene and clear,
Fortune and wisdom both arrive.
Preserve my flying immortal,
Ascending to the Jade Terrace.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances!*

**Secret Method for Harmonious Summoning with Bell and Chime**
The Master says: The bell sounds yang; the chime, yin. When the altar’s steps are complete, strike the golden bell and jade chime to summon harmony. Not only to summon harmony, but to gather yin spirits and yang numina, intermingling their qi. Thus, the golden bell is struck twenty-five times, modeling heaven—heaven’s number is twenty-five. The jade chime is struck thirty times, modeling earth—earth’s number is thirty. Moreover, as yin and yang desire their union, the bell and chime are struck alternately thirty-six times, one yin and one yang totaling seventy-two, to connect with the seventy-two seasonal nodes. Yet when yang reaches its extreme, yin arises; when yin reaches its extreme, yang arises. Thus, decline and renewal alternate, adversity and prosperity succeed one another. Yin cannot be wholly yin, so it returns to its yang sound, and the jade chime is struck nine times. Nine is the Qian number, yang. Yang cannot be wholly yang, so it returns to its yin sound, and the golden bell is struck six times. Six is the Kun number, yin.

**Jade Talisman for Summoning Yin Spirits**
*Incantation:*
The Primordial Beginning’s singular qi,
Silently moves the primordial essence.
Harmonizing tones and tuning rhythms,
Stirring the turbid and raising the pure.
The wondrous qi of the secluded and distant,
The wondrous qi’s initial congealment.
Coiling through the empty cavern,
The sound within heaven.
Gathering essence and descending qi,
Issuing forth the true voice.
Yin sounds interweave,
Summoning the ten thousand numina.

**Jade Talisman for Summoning Yang Spirits**
Strike the golden bell once, tap the left teeth once. Strike the jade chime once, tap the right teeth once. Visualize the two qi of left and right within the body intermingling, filling the mysterious altar.
*Incantation:*
Stillness gives birth to movement,
Returning yin generates yang.
The Great Tone enters the wondrous,
Wandering the empty valley.
Sound responds to qi’s seeking,
Intermingling in gong and shang.
Sound upon sound resonates,
Transforming and circulating the mysterious altar.
The sound that arouses yang,
Unites with heaven’s firmness.
Yang spirits intermingle,
True qi blends in harmony.

**Nine Audiences in Three Days**
The *Scripture of Pacing the Void* states: Lofty immortals and great sages ascend the Jade Capital Mountain thrice daily to offer pure fasts, practice the Dao, and soar through the empty void. Thus, the rites of audience with the perfected in the lower realm must emulate this. One gives birth to two, two gives birth to three—hence, one day has three audiences. Three begets nine—hence, three days have nine audiences. In practice, for the morning audience, visualize the yang spirit of the upper cinnabar field paying homage to the Origin’s Venerable in the Mud Pill Palace.

At the noon audience, visualize the yang spirit of the middle cinnabar field paying homage to the Crimson Palace. At the evening audience, visualize the yang spirit of the lower cinnabar field paying homage to the cinnabar field, then ascending from its original place upon the qi.

At dawn, ride the azure qi of the Mud Pill Palace to pay homage to the Primordial Lord. At noon, ride the yellow qi of the heart to pay homage to the Lord of the Dao. At dusk, ride the white-and-black qi of the kidneys to pay homage to the Old Lord. Thus, the inner qi merges with the outer qi, and the outer spirits align with the inner spirits—so that in a single instant, response is as swift as an echo.

**First Day at Dawn: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
The chapter of the Mysterious Cavern of Chaos dispels yin and generates yang.
Crimson radiance illumines above; the golden chamber shines resplendent.
The mysterious altar gleams bright; the gates of heaven stand wide open.
True immortals descend and manifest; demonic trials withdraw in concealment.
Turn the light toward the Jade Portal to refine and nurture the Spirit King.
The nine qi are complete—ascend to the Jade Hall.

**First Day at Noon: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
The golden wheel blazes crimson, its light illuminating the Purple Tenuity.
The Lord Emperor issues his decree to crush and destroy demonic pests.
Light descends from the Three Heavens; the Six Caverns banish evil.
The Three Divisions rest in peace; the Nine Gates remain unharmed.
Pure yang blazes brilliantly; all immortals pay homage.
Rising to the Fire Palace, they attend the cultivation of the Radiant One.

**First Day at Dusk: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
Dawn’s radiance mingles with Brahman qi, pervading the Nine Purities.
Steady and perfect, its illumination penetrates the altar’s courtyard.
Fragrant clouds form auspicious patterns; wisdom candles glow bright.
The Nine Dark Realms open to light; the karmic path flourishes eternally.
Jade light blazes resplendent; the jasper chambers unfold.
Golden light banishes night—ascend with the immortals.

**Second Day at Dawn: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
Pure dawn’s lofty brilliance scatters the shadows of yin’s depths.
The Cavern of Emptiness and the Sunlit Valley see true immortals soaring high.
Fire clouds surge forth; the golden wheel does not delay.
Gathering qi in fusion, light fills the feathered robes.
Fusang initiates its motion; green yang intermingles in swift exchange.
Pay homage to the Great Crimson, refining the subtle mysteries of the Dao.

**Second Day at Noon: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
The radiant vermilion spirits ascend to pay homage at the Jade Capital.
Eight gates stand guard; the Six Heavens disperse yin.
Heaven’s light aligns with the luminous realm; the earthly prisons grow clear.
The crimson talisman circulates within; dark fiends conceal their forms.
The Heavenly Soldiers are mighty, smiting demonic essences.
Corpses and evil perish and fall—eternally preserve the immortal lifespan.

**Second Day at Dusk: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
The pure and luminous true radiance sees bright stars arrayed across the heavens.
True immortals ride their chariots; exalted sages approach the throne.
Clouds form fragrant talismans; the jeweled canopy shelters the true field.
The Divine Mother of Jade Purity bestows enlightenment upon the profound mysteries.
Heaven and earth unite in harmony; ten thousand kalpas stretch endlessly.
In the unity of creation, ascend to the Jade Terrace.

**Third Day at Dawn: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
Eastern Florescence dawns in brilliance; the perfected turn their chariots.
The Cavern of Yang shines resplendent, its light penetrating the clouded robes.
Ascend to pay homage at the Jade Realm, communing with the true and awakening to the subtle.
Wander amidst Brahman qi, refining the golden elixir.
The yang spirits array themselves in order; clarity extends in all four directions.
The kalpic revolutions of the cosmos are preserved eternally without loss.

**Third Day at Noon: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
The midday crimson wheel sees heavenly spirits and perfected ones ascend.
They guard and seal the demonic paths; no malevolent forces dare invade.
The five yang return to the six; the one yin scatters its form.
The Mysterious Palace rests in peace; the Three Radiant Ones grow clear.
Refine the body of unyielding strength to preserve the Great Brilliance.
With power, grind away calamity—unite with heaven in spirit.

**Third Day at Dusk: Recitation of the Dao-Protecting and Spirit-Guarding Incantation**
The inner vision of the Mysterious Void sees heaven and earth conjoined.
Yin and yang are harmonized; punishment and thought achieve completion.
Lofty brilliance, pure and white, illumines my heavenly court.
Jade perfected ones descend in unison; the Mysterious Chamber opens in clarity.
Drink and ingest the yellow qi to preserve the Dao and realize the true.
The five qi converge in union; the Three Officials grow clear.

**At Dawn: Issuing the Crucible**
Summon forth from within your body the Three-and-Five Merit Officers, the Left and Right Palace Attendants, the Golden Lads of Incense, the Jade Maidens of Word and Flower, the Five Thearchs’ Direct Talismans, and the Daily Incense Officials—thirty-six of each.

**At Noon: Issuing the Crucible**
Summon forth from within your body the Cavern-Bright Merit Officers, the Upper Spirit Immortals, the Three Qi Yang Spirits, the Three-and-Five Orthodox Unity Flying Dragon Riders, the Jade Maidens of Fusion, and the Daily Incense Officials—eighty-one of each.

**At Dusk: Issuing the Crucible**
Summon forth from within your body the Three Officials’ Spirit Immortals, the Nine Portal Perfected Ones, the Jade-Light Golden-Color Spirit Lads, the Jeweled-Light Jade Maidens, and the Sacred Assembly of the Cinnabar Chamber—sixty-four of each.

**Establishing the Altar**
Summon forth from within your body the Three-and-Five Merit Officers, the Nine Yang Perfected Body Immortal Officers, the Nine Qi Spirit Lads, the Eight Gate Spirit Immortal Talisman Officers, the Three Qi Orthodox Spirits, and the Daily Incense Officials—twenty-four of each.

**Nine Phoenix Talismans for Purity**
With the Northern Thearch’s mudra, visualize the nine phoenixes upon your head, the Seven Stars pointing forward, then spray the water.

**Incantation:**
Reverently invite the essence of the Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper to descend into this water.
All impure ghosts, swiftly depart ten thousand leagues away—those who do not depart shall be slain and delivered to the White Lad of the West.
*Oṃ vāri oṃ vāri ūnu li du ku ru khaṭa svāhā.*

**Nine Phoenix Talisman for Dispelling Impurities**

**Talisman for Purifying the Body**
**Incantation:**
The impure qi is wholly dispelled; the Three Passes merge in clarity.
The Golden Tower illumines the Jade Chamber, where the Highest Lord of the Mysterious Origin is enshrined.
The Twenty-Four Perfected are complete—body and spirit ascend to the distant void.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances.*

**Talisman for Purifying the Mind**
**Incantation:**
The Crimson Palace governs the spirit qi; Brahman qi follows the light in flight.
The true person’s abode is refined—mundane toil holds no thought.
In tranquil audience at the Mysterious Upper Terrace, sweet dew congeals as jasper nectar.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances.*

**Talisman for Purifying the Mouth**
**Incantation:**

**Talisman for Purifying the Mouth**
**Incantation:**
The radiance of the Flowery Splendor illumines the heavens; jade chambers and jasper fluids flow in communion.
Twelve-tiered towers stand in succession; jade milk advances to the Fountain Palace.
Washing away the dust and filth of the corpse, the Dharma drum harmonizes with the golden bell.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances.*

**Talisman for Purifying Ghosts**
**Incantation:**
Yin scatters as yang returns; the Mysterious Pass and Jade Gate swing open.
The corpse of Peng dissolves to ashes; at midnight, celestial thunder strikes.
Firelight bursts through the Gate of Heaven; the Perfected One’s numinous chariot returns.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances.*

**Talisman for Uniting with the Spirit**
**Incantation:**
True yang guards the spirit’s abode; qi returns to form the celestial Perfected.
The corpse-demons perish and fall; the body conceals itself in perfect clarity.
Numinous qi merges as the One Origin; the Three Spirits ascend to the Upper Capital.
Above lies the Palace of Light—coming and going, the Dao is naturally fulfilled.
*Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the true statutes and ordinances.*

**Tablet of the Three Qi and Three Treasures**
**Master’s Instruction:**
Whenever entering a household to burn incense, at all times—morning and evening—first knock the teeth twelve times outside the door. Step forward with the right foot, and visualize the four Attendant Messengers of Merit-Officials in flowing robes with wide sleeves.
Next, visualize four Jade Maidens and the Lords of the Dragon and Tiger.
Then, visualize the heavens filled with azure, yellow, and white [qi].

Next, visualize five-colored mists rising in swirling vapors—all in accordance with the audience rites of the celestial court.

Here ends *Fascicle Thirty of the Supreme Mysterious Origin Three Heavens Jade Hall Great Method*.
